maloko a wáfrika annivoliwa ntthona na muluku .
wira ntthona nla nririhiwe , atthu èkereja epajerye wixiha wamini waya .
elívuru ila ya katekese yolepeliwa makatekúmeno wira etthareke mpakha obatiziwa ni yolepeliwatho akristu othene wira esukeke ni yinjereryeke wamini waya .
tthiri mabispu à nihimerya wira : akristu othene anniphavela olokihiwa n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ulakiwa n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ulipihiwa murima. wira ekhale atthu òlaleya , khula mmosa ni muteko onvarawe mukereja .
wáfrika nno olelo va , wamini khunlipihenwa orattene : tivó-nto àkhala anisira akristu vohiloka , yawo annittottela murerelo ohisuwela nno w &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; akristu .
ntoko nsu na muluku nipankyaya mutthu mwa yesu , khukhala nihiyo , siso-tho ehapari yorera ehana ovolowa mmakhaleloni mw &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; atthu ale aniwa .
elívuru ila ya katekese entthuna wakhaliherya akristu wira yetteleke masu a muluku mmakhaleloni mwaya , elaleyeke ehapari yorera ni yavyeke orukunuxa mupuwelo ni mwettelo w &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; atthu , ekhalihiwaka atthu asyá okathi wothene w ekumi aya ni mapuro othene .
vanjenexa elivuru ila yolepeliwa makatekista n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; alupale othene èkereja , wira ekhalé muthuko yamwaleleke akhw &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; aya .
katekista , ahinatthi wakhaliherya makatekumeno osuwela itthu sintthunaya wira , yowene amusomeke toko mekhawe katekese ni aikohe mmansawe wira :
miyo vekekhai kinnamini itthu sinlaleyaka ?
vekekhai kinncttela seiyo sinà minaka ?
makhalelo a katekista
katekista ohana :
okhala otthenkaseya
nihinatthi ophiya nihiku na katekese , ireke asommene orattene molumo othene alepeliwe muthukuman &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; owo .
alompeke wira amwaleliwe n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; iroho yowarya .
oreriha nipuro na katekese
apajeryeke ophiya , khutthenkasa nipuro : ovela , ikhattera , matthatto , n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; itthu sothene simphavelawe ovarela muteko .
okhala mutthu onvanelaneya
ahilavuleke mekhawe : avaneleke n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; atthu othene .
awiriyaneke .
ahikuxereryeke wira owo pahi t &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; orina miruku sorera .
ahòveke .
asuweleke orattene makatekumeno awe , asuweleke-tho makhalelo aya .
okhaliheriwa n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; akristu
khula muthukumano , akristu , vanjenexa ale athanliwe okhala anamuku àprekatekúmeno , emukhaliheryeke katekista , wira ahikhaleke mekhawe .
mavalo a katekese
katekista onniwakhelela amusi
othene annikohana ihali .
katekista onnakoha makatekúmeno molumo a katekese avinre , yaliyalá onniwupuxerya .
khula mutthu ahimye muteko wamanenlyawe natiri okhala wira òvara walá khavanre .
makhalelo ahu
khula katekese ompacerya ni makhalelo ahu .
molumo awo annikhaliherya owiriyana sana masu a muluku ni ottemulela mutthaka muluku ontthunawe onihimerya .
katekista asomeke molumo a makhalelo ahu , walá àhimeryeke amusi ni molumo awe itthu silempwe .
masu a muluku
katekista asomeke sana , numalá àkohe amusi yaiwalene sana .
awo ehimyé molumo yiwalyaya .
okhala wira khiyaiwale orattene katekista asomeke-tho .
vano othene evaneleke elikanyihaka molumo a makhalelo ahu ni masu a muluku n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; itthu sinkhumelela mulaponi mwahu mahiku ala , siso anrowa ottemulela mutthaka muluku omphavelawe wahimerya .
murima wa katekese
mutthaka owo wapajenryaya ottemulela evanelaka , onniwanyeya orattene katekista asomaka murima wa katekese .
katekista asomeke ni ahimyeke ni molumo awe wira othene yìweke sana .
ovekela
molumo a ovekela , imara sinjene ari a masalmo .
ni molumo awo anaisarayeli , hatá yesu n akristu yanvekenle muluku ikuru sowettela masu awe .
siso nìreke-tho hiyo .
khula mutthu alompeke-tho ni molumo awe wira amuxukhuru muluku molumo òrera aiwalyawe ni anvekele ikuru so wettela .
ovanela ni olehana
katekista asomeke sokoha .
othene ephaveleke wakhula .
ovanela iwo omaleke wiwananiwaka muteko wanrowaya ovara owani ettharaka molumo a katekese , othene vamosá walá khula mutthu mekhawe .
emmaneke natiri evarelanaka matata .
yixutteke molumo alempwe wira esukiweke mmurimani .
olaxeryana ni nsipo nokhuma
ohinatthi ovolowa okatekúmeno
khavo onwerya okirwela miyo , ahithanliwe n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; atithi
atthu anòniherya otthuna waya okhala akristu , yakheleliweke sana n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; utteliwa murima munlokoni mw akristu .
katekista walá ansiau alehaneke n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; awo nihiku nintthunaya orowa okumana n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; amusi aya , ahikhanle akristu .
evaneleke n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; amusi awo mwaha w otthuna waya okhala akristu : ehimeriweke otteliwa wahu murima , mana nloko nahu khanthanliwa mutthu , khavo onkhottihiwa okela .
muluku tith &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ihu onnihanela okhala an &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; awe n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; amusi .
vano okathi onrerela opajeriwa katekese , nlaihaniweke n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; akristu nihiku n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; owakhelela awo omphavela okela nloko nahu .
katekista khanwerya owakhelela mekhawe , nto yakheleliweke n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; akristu èkomunidade vanjenexa n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; aholeli aya .
owakhelela amusi a nanano
nyuwo mumphavela osuwela nloko na muluku , murweke ni murettele : hiyo n amus inyu .
muthukuman &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ola okhalé ntoko siniraya amusi , evanelaka ni murettele n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; utteliwa murima .
katekista apajeryeke wasuweliha akristu akhw &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; awe wira amusi asyá omphavela okela nloko n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; akristu .
akristu yàthonyeryeke amusi awo otteliwa waya murima w &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; owakhelela . othene esuwelaneke wira yettihaneke ntoko amusi akhweli .
vanrerela okhala-vo animadore a zona .
makhulupale a nloko n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; akristu yopeke mwahá wa molumo ala :
nri vava , mana muluku ònitthana . nitteliweke murima , nimuxukhuruku .
munn ihu ti yesu kristo , yowo ontthunahu omusuwela n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; umutthara wira nettihaneke ntoko amusi .
nyuwo munnipacerya olelo wettela ephiro wira mmusuweleke yesu kristo , musuweleke itthu siralyawe , okhwa n uhihimuwa wawe ni mmutthareke .
ephiro ela ennopixani wobatizoni onrowawe yesu wovahani ekumi esyá .
vano elehaneke nihiku n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ompacerya katekese .
katekese onlikana ni namálwe . wakhula wihaniwa .
katekese ti :
wiwa ni maru ,
wamini ni murima ,
wettela ni mukhalelo ahu wothene .
aprekatekúmeno ehimeriweke orowa omphavela mukristu oniwerya wakhaliherya wettela ephiro y okatekúmeno . katekista n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ansiau yakhaliheryeke aprekatekúmeno omuthanla mukristu onrerela .
muthukuman ola omaleke ni nivekelo ni nsipo .
apwiya muluku , hiyo notteliwa murima vathukumanenlyahu otthara ephiro anyu .
nsipo : nimuttottopele muluku
okhala ntoko axinna
atthu othene a mulaponi anniphavela okhala vamosá yatanàka n akhw aya .
kavo onwerya okhala mekhawe .
hiyo othene onnisivela othukumana ni ovanela n amusi n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; apatthani , ninnimphavelatho muholeli àxariya wira anettihe ni murettele momusini ni vatthokoni nikhaliheryanaka mukina ni mukhw &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; awe .
muluku mwanene t ohenle mmurimani mw &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; atthu othene otthuna wiwanana .
nto mulaponi mothene atthu annikawanyeya , annipuheryana , ni annikumiheryana ikhotto .
hiyo n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; akristu ninnikupali wira atthu othene emuttharaka yesu kristu pahi anophwanya murettele , exariya ni watàna .
owo ti murummwa a muluku orwenle wakhaliha atthu othene omusi omosá w axinna aniphentana .
yesu òvahererya ekumi awe wira amalihe okawanyeya w atthu , vano onniwitthanela othene okhala ntoko axinna .
okhala onokhalihaniwa
ovanela mwaha w ephattu ya munlokoni
makhalelo ahu
mulaponi mu khanthowa mahimo .
mahimo awo aphattunwe n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; amus &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ihu a khalai .
tivó khula mutthu okhalana nihimo nawe n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; atat &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; awe .
mutthu , osuwela nihimo nawe ni nsina na humu awe etthu yulupale ni yorera , ephattu y &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; emakhuwa .
elimalelo y emakhuwa , khula mutthu okathi oninnuwawe , onnixuttihiwa n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ame awe nihimo nawe ni humu oniholela nloko nawe .
okathi omanlyaya ekhotto , anamwane akina àrimela mana khasuwenle nihimo naya ni nsina na humu aya .
vano ole àsuwela , vomukhwela osuweliwa n uphiya owani .
siso-tho atthu akina ayareliwe opoma khansuwela nihimo naya , masi annimuthanla mutthu onarerela wira àkhaliheryeke maxankiho aya :
owo onnikhala ntoko humu aya .
wakhumelela mulattu , munroha vai ?
yakhumelela eretta yulupale , muniwakuvel ani ? .
khavo onkhala mekhawe , ahikhanle ni mutthu onlipanawe , nnakhala mutthu onrowa ovara muteko elapo ekina , weiwo onnimphavela mutthu òlipana .
vanjenexa ayariwa mwana , ikoma , ifesta sotthapela , othelaniwa , nàkhwa , matthanka , itthu iya sothene khasiniriwa humu a nloko ahisuwelihiwe , yowo t &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; oniholela .
onakhalaru mulolo ohiniwananeya munlokoni mwawe , yamphwanya maxaka , humu awe anathukumanya amusi othene à himeryaka wira etakhwa y alolo khivo .
anaruma amusi akina oroweliwa mmusi aya owo nipuro nlo nnihawawe , wira emukhaliheryeke omaliha maxaka aphwanyalyawe .
murima wa katekese
okhalihana w amusi ti nikano norera nnivahiwahu n amuhakhala ihu .
yolimalela ela ya munlokoni n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; emakhuwa , etthu yulupale ni yorera .
ovekela
ninnoxukhuruni , apwiya muluku ahu , mana okhuma khalai munninivaha mahumu annihòlela mmalokoni mwahu .
ovanela ni olehana
okathi ula sivaneliweke itthu satonko okhumelela s &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; okhaliheryana munlokoni walá mmuttettheni .
ninnona okhala etthu yorera munlokoni okhala mutthu mmosa ohòlela nloko nlo ?
mutthu onaholela amusi akhaleke owi sai ?
mutthu ettale arowaka elapo y ottaiwene , onnona okhala etthu yorera okhala mekhawe ?
mahiku ala tithi a mutthu ni mama a mutthu anttittimihiwa sai ?
namakotto khanlipa ahirapenle mwiri !
mwene mekhawe khaniwerya wira etthu yorera , ahikhaliheriwaka n amusi awe .
makhalelo ahu
mutokwene a nihimo nahu akhwa vale , amusi othene annithukumana , yalattulaka hatá atthu a mahimo makina .
alopwana ampacerya ovanela ekohanaka ti pani onrowa okela mpani mw atat aya akhwiye .
vano mutthu othanliwe , onnemexiwa eriyari y amusi othene ehimeriwaka wira :
ola va tata ! orinanyu omwiwelelaka n utthara sinihimyawe , ntoko sawirelanyu atat ale avinre .
vano owo onnihimeriwa wira :
amusi yettihiwa n atat inyu t ala : akumi , alolo ari vava , othene muharihelé otakhwani , t awinyu ! .
okhuma nihiku nenlo amusi othene a nloko nlo annettihiwa ni yowo .
yakhalá enkhumelela munlokoni yorera walá yotakhala , amusi animwakuvela yowo , onakhaliherya omalamaliha muxankih owo .
atat awo annaxekurya mmawannyeya amusi othene , hatá ale ankhala ottaiwene , khiyavaha miruku so wetta sana munlokoni .
othene annattittimiha atata , anniwiwelela , annaphenta , anniwakhela sana vaté vaya , annatumererya an aya wira siso siniraya , mana ti yawo amuthanlale okhala tat aya . -
murima wa katekese
ohumu ti warumela amusi othene .
amusi anniwanana munlokoni , akhalaka mutthu òrera murima onaholela .
humu akhaleke òroromeleya n amusi othene a nloko nlo , wira aweryeke owatàniha .
akhalaka òsuwela n òrera murima onnareriha amusi othene a nloko nawe .
amuhakhalai ahu avinre , ari ntoko mitathari sahu , humu ori ntoko mwiri onatàniha mitathari n iritta .
mwiri wowùma , iritta saya sinnúma . tivo vankhwèleya wira amusi othene etthokeleleke sana ehinatthi omuthanla humu aya ontthuna owettiha .
ovekela
muluku , munivahe murima worera wira nìweleleke mahumu ahu , níwananeke munlokoni mwahu .
ovanela ni olehana
munlokoni mwanyu òkhala mwené othanleliwe n amusi wettiherya nloko ?
ale ahirina , annilipa , annìwanana ?
munlokoni mwahu mwené òttikhiwa onnajala amusi othene ? ohavo onthanyiwa n uwo ?
mwene aphavelaka opaka muthukumano , amusi akina ehinatthuna orwa , annira sana ?
nireke exeni humu ahu ahinettiheke sana ?
mulattu khanikhùwa atat awe , amphuka .
hiyo nakhuwa atat ihu etthu yiralyahu , anira sai onikhaliherya ?
makhalelo ahu
khula mutthu ayariwaka onnikela nihimo n ame awe , khavo onthanla mmansawe .
nihimo nlo ninkhuma wa muhakhala ihu :
owo t opajenrye wihaneliwa nihimo nlo , vano atthu awe khíyìreliwa analexe , ntoko amale , amirekoni , amavele , amulima .
khula nihimo ohavo mutthu oniholela :
amavele amwene aya yihaniwaka yamuthala , atthu a nloko nlo annihaniwa anamuthala .
akina ekhalaka amirekoni , mulupale aya ihaniwaka yapaphaya , amusi aya othene annihaniwa anapaphaya .
mukina akhalaka akhurupuwa , amusi annihaniwa anakhurupuwa .
hiyo nokhalana nihimo nahu , nokhalana atat ihu , nloko nahu , nsina nahu , vano nirwenle-ni va ?
mahimo a vathí t òkawanyeya .
onokhwani annirelana iperwa , annikhaliheryana ovitha evaraka miteko sothene sinkhweleya okathi ule , nto annivehana ni annikuxa solya ehivekelanne , khíyakawana okathi ole .
annirelana siso ettharihaka iperwa .
makhalelo ala annikawanya mahimo , yavalanyaka akina n akhw aya .
masu a muluku
vaphiyalyaya okathi wathanliwe , muluku òmuruma mwan awe .
ola ahiyariwa ni muthiyana , ettihiwaka n ikano s ayuda , wira awòpole ale yettihiwa n ikano seiyo , ni wira hiyo niwerye okhalihiwa ana òleliwa a muluku .
murima wa katekese
muluku , tithi àtthu othene , onnarumihela mòpoli oniwatàniha wira ekhaleke nihimo nimosá .
muluku awehaka makhalelo àtthu antepa okawanyeya , onnamorela ikharari ni onnarumihela mwan awe yesu kristu , yowo onixuttihale wira muluku ti tithi àtthu othene , awo ari axinna .
tivo vahinreraya othanyana n upuheryana , mahimo othene ahana okhala ntoko ephula nnitho .
khalaixa yahikhala atthu ntoko amuhakhala ihu , nloko naya nari n amakampusi n alimi , nihaniwaka na isarayeli .
mwa nloko nenlo muluku ahimuthanla muthiyana , nsina nawe maria , yowo amuyanre yesu kristu .
atthu a maloko othene annitthaniwa ni yesu wira ekele omusi ola .
khinnithanliwa nikhuli , nihimo , elapo , elavulelo walá ephattu .
ovekela
apwiya , muluku ahu , munivahe ebarakha wira natàneke , nimuttharaka yesu kristu .
ovanela ni olehana
ninnisuwela itthu sinkina sinakawanya atthu , enathanyana ni enapuherya ?
mapuro antumihiwa itthu , oxipiritali , oxikhola , mapuro anvariwa muteko , mapuro amphukiwa milattu ?
nywo munupuwela-ni mwaha wa nloko n akristu ?
atthu a nloko n akristu t èlapo emosa walá t a nihimo nimosa ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
yesu ti mulupale a nloko n akristu , oniwatàniha atthu othene .
ophenta ovilelá !
makhalelo ahu
mulupale a nloko na vathi-va onnavaha miruku atthu anaholelawe , wira ekhalaneke murima mmosá worera , wowiwanana , ephentaneke , ekhaliheryaneke .
masi àkhala akina ahintthuna omwiwelela , ankhotta miruku sorera sinavahawe , anetta ni enamuna entthuna murim aya .
awo annimunyokha humu aya mana makhalelo aya t otakhala .
annona wanyonyiha miruku sorera sinatumereryawe wettela .
hatá atthu awo yiraka siso , humu aya khananyanyala , imara sikina onnipaka mithukumano n amusi wira aphwanyeke miruku s owokolola ale ahiniwananeya , ahimyaka wira :
etakhwa y alolo khivo .
siso yesu kristu varwalyawe àphwanyale atthu othene ekawanyeyalene n inamuna sinjene :
athajiri yàhaxaka òthoiwa ;
akumi yàthanyaka aretta ;
alopwana yàpuheryaka athiyana ;
alupale yàpuheryaka axikhani ;
anjene etthukiwaka vahimulattu .
masu a muluku
yesu ahikelela wettetta elapo yothene y ocalileya , awixuttihaka atthu mpani mwaya mothukumana , mwihaniwa sinagoga , alaleyaka ehapari yorera y omwene , àvonihaka atthu iretta saya sothene n ikwerere saya sothene .
ovuwa wawe wahimwarela mulaponi mothene m osiria : tivó varuheliwawe atthu othene yahawa , ehaxiwaka n iretta ni sotakhala sa khuia enamuna , n ale yavariwe ni malaikha òtakhala , n atthu yawereiwa ejili n alipa-òrakala .
vano yesu anavoniha .
mittitthi sulupale s atthu sanimutthara , sikhumaka ogalileya n ilapo ya dekápoli n oyerusalemu n oyudeya n ilapo y okhopela wa yordani .
murima wa katekese
yesu ti mòpoli ahu orummwe n atithi , ontthuna wira niphentaneke ntoko axinna .
yesu kristu khatthunne otthara solimalela sakawanya atthu , aphenta atthu othene , khamuthanyale mutthu .
yesu anaphavela-tho athajiri , àtumereryaka wira yakhalihereke alipa-òthoiwa , mana othene amusí , othene àna a muluku .
nloko nlo vakhani vakhani novira ninnuwaka mpakha omwarela mulaponi mothene mwa vathi .
vano yesu onninihana-tho hiyo wira niphentaneke , nimoneleke vatthu khula mutthu .
ovekela
apwiya , muluku ahu , munivahe omusuwela yesu , munikhaliheryeke watàna n atthu othene !
ovanela ni olehana
mahiku ala , mulaponi mu , ninnona wira atthu annìwanana , walá annikawanyeya ?
yesu ahamorela ikharari aretta n alipa-òhawa .
mulaponi mu awo annoneliwa watthu ?
hiyo ninwònela sai alipa-òhawa ?
hiyo nìreke exeni wira nimutakiheke yesu òmoriwa ikharari ?
momusini mwahu ninniwanana n atthu a mahimo makina ?
okwesa ompajeriwa mpani , khiyakela otá !
malhalelo ahu
masu a muluku
yesu ahettetta ilapo sothene , awirelaka atthu sorera , awòpolaka othene ale yari ipottha .
vano atthu yahimwiva , emukhomelaka vamwikimanyo .
masi mmurottoni mwaya , muluku òmuhihimuxa mokhwani , khunvaha wisoniherya , khahiyó w atthu othene , masi w ale yathanliwe wopaceryani ni muluku wira ekhalé anamona .
murima wa katekese
yesu ahìra sorera , ahilupatthiwa , khwiviwa , nto muluku òmuhihimuxa .
yesu anixuttiha wira muluku onnaphenta atthu othene , ntoko tithi sinaphentawe à n awe .
yesu ari mmasikhini , kharina nipuro n okhala , àmuroromela muluku pahi , yowo ori tithi awe .
yesu aniwixuttiha atthu wira ettittimihaneke , ekhaliheryaneke .
anahimerya athajiri ni makhulupale a mulaponi wira ehapuheryeke atthu axikhani n alipa-òhawa , ehathanyeke .
makhulupale yahinyonyiwa ni mwixuttiho wa yesu .
tivó vaiwanannyaya omotheryasa yesu n umwiviha .
yesu anisuwela wira arowa wiviwa , nto khakumihale ekhotto , khanvehale mutthu , khùpuwenle otthyawa , ahivilela amuroromelaka muluku amurumme ni àphentaka hatá ale yamulupattha .
ohìviwa akhomeliwaka vamwikimanyo , ntoko okathi ule sirihiwaya alavilavi n anawive .
muluku khamunyanyanle yesu .
vakhwiyawe ni vavithiwawe òmuhihimuxa mw alipa-òkhwa mmurottoni mwaya .
vahihimuwalyawe , yesu ahisoniherya w apatthani awe , yawo yamutthara .
vano ori ni muluku tithi awe , nave , hatá nihimonaka , ori-tho ni hiyo .
ovekela
apwiya yesu , mwakhwenle atthu othene , munivahe ebarakha yo waphenta atthu othene , hatá ale annirela sotakhala .
ovanelani olehana
yesu ni mwixuttiho awe ni makhalelo awe , exeni yaphavelawe wasuweliha atthu ?
yesu alupatthiwaka ahaxiwaka ti pani amuroromelawe ?
vakhwalyawe yesu ni exeni yamukhumelenle ?
akristu anlipa nani ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
yesu kristu ti mòpoli àkhwenle atthu othene .
namurera murima nlitti nawe khannixa !
ekhalawa khinlyihiwa n ule ohilyiye !
makhalelo ahu
mwanamwane opopihiwaka ni yotakhala , anari n atithi awe , khanòva .
atthu annopopihiwa n itthu sotakhala sowatta ni ankhala yòvaka , khanamini wira muluku ori vakhiviru vaya .
amus ihu a khalai yanisuwela wira muluku òkhala . awo yanihimya wira :
muluku ti mwanene itthu sothene .
mukhulukana muluku yola .
nanwara sothala , muluku onnimona . muluku òkikhunèla !
muluku mukhwatapari onetta awehaka vathi .
masi amus ihu awo a khalai khiyàsuwela wira muluku ti tithi aya atthu othene ni wira , mopuhani walá movelavelani , muluku onnikhala vavo , khiyakhaliherya .
tivo , eripiwaka murima , vahimyaya wira :
muluku òkitheya . muluku òkitthulamela .
hiyo nanò ripe : ohawa wonlimalela !
oripa woniha itthu . nikhuli nla ti notakhala .
vakhanleru siso , mohawani ni motakhaliwani yanona wira yahimurakamela muluku . tivo , yanatthyawelela amusi aya akhwiye , wira yawo evaneleke ni muluku . siso yanihela mukuttho , yanimutthukwa natiri , wira amuhatat aya yawo yakhaliherye , yavekeleleke wa muluku .
okathi w owereiwa walá w otakhaliwa , yanihimya wira apipi yale akhwiye ànanariwa , walá ohavo onakhalela nrima .
siso mukhalelo aya wari woripiwa .
olelo va khavo anira siso ntoko siraya amus ihu awo a khalai ?
vano-nto , hiyo ntthikeleke otthara ephiro yeyo ?
amus ihu a khalai yananyiherya wira ehimutthunkwe natiri , ehihenle mikuttho , walá ehivanhe solya , muluku khàvaha iye saphavelaya , ntoko ekumi , solya , epula ni sikinaku sorera .
masu a muluku
yesu ahahimerya awixutti awe wira :
murima ohovaveni mutthokelelaka yoyla , walá yowurya emphavelelanyu olipa nnánkhala muhivelavelé ni sowara simphavelelanyu erutthu anyu .
vekekhai , ekumi khahiyó yulupale ovikana yoyla ?
nave erutthu khahiyó yulupale ovikana sowara ?
nkàweheni axipalame anvava musulu : khanàla , nnákhala khanihepha , hatá kharina ntatha n osuka solya . vano , atith inyu ari wirimu annaphwanyiha solya iyo . khi nyuwo , khamuhiyó alupalexa wavikana axinuni ?
ti pani a nyuwo , onwerya orakamiha hatá vakhani olekela w ekumi awe ?
nave-tho , munripeliwa-ni murima mwaha wa sowara ?
mòneke waleya wa ithutu sa mmathalani :
khasinvara muteko , nnákhala khasintthava ikuwo .
vano muluku , yowo oniwariha siso malaxi a mmathalani , ankhala olelo , melo khupahiwa , onotepa wowarihani nyuwo , atthu òwamini vakhani .
tivó , muhithanané mwiraka :
nilye exeni ?
niwurye exeni ?
niware exeni ?
ahinimusuwela muluku t anetta ephavelaka itthu iya sothene .
masi nyuwo , atith inyu ari wirimu annisuwela wira sothene iya sinnohalelani .
murima wa katekese
yesu ònithonyerya ni makhalelo awe wira muluku tith ihu , onnisuwela ohawa wahu , ori ni hiyo khula nihiku .
yesu onninixuttiha wira muluku tith ihu , ohinweryahu omuhoverya , onniniphenta ni khanninyanyala .
vayariwahu , nakhala mulaponi mu , mana muluku onniniphenta . owo onnimusuka khula mutthu , khavo onimurihelawe osalani .
yesu khalavunle molumo pahi , nto ohòniherya n itthu sawirenlyawe atthu wira muluku onnisuwela muhawelo wa khula mutthu .
khavo onimuliyalawe . yesu aniwattamela aretta n ale òthanyiwa , khwamorela ikharari .
ninlelo yesu òleva ekumi awe , wira àkhalihe atthu othene axinna hatá awanani awe .
vekekhai anamini wira hatá ale yamwirela yotakhala , yari ana a muluku . tivó ahalevelela othene , ahimyaka wira :
tithi , mwalevelele , okhala wira khansuwela sinirava .
yesu ahixintta wova , mana ahimwamini muluku tithi awe .
tithi , matatani mwanyu kinovahereryani eroho aka .
tthiri , muluku ahimwakhelela yesu , khumuhihimuxa mokhwani .
ovekela
apwiya muluku tith ihu , nyuwo ti mwanene itthu sothene .
ninnamini wira muri khula nipuro , molikanana onikhaliherya khula okathi .
ovanela ni olehana
amuhakhalai ahu moxankani mwaya yanatthyawelela alipaòkhwa .
vano hiyo ninniroromela mukhaliheryo aya walá ninniwova ?
yakhweyá alipa-òkhwa anniwerya oniriha yotakhala ?
yesu ònixuttiha wira muluku ti tithi òrera murima , onniphenta . omuroromela wahu t uwi ?
wetta mekhawo wisiva !
mutthu khanira : kètte nani ? muluku ari-vo !
makhalelo ahu
katekúmeno mmosá orotthukweliwa okhatteya , weiwo-tho atthukweliwa amiravo araru òtanzania avirinhe miyeri mili sihiphukiwaka milattu saya .
okhala wira kharina amusi omosambikhi nno , annihawasa etala n orirya .
nto katekumeirowo okathi wothene onruheliwawe yolya n amusi awe onnakawela akhw awe awo .
masu a muluku
ophenta wanyu okhaleke w ekekhai , muthanyeke sotakhala .
mwalompeleke ale anolupatthani ;
munvekele muluku wira àvahe itthu sorera , ahiwirelé sotakhala .
mutteliweke murima vamosá n ale antteliwa murima ;
muhiphaveleké itthu sowittittimiherya , mwilikanyiheke n ale ahinòneliwa vatthu .
muhisupuweleké okhala asuweli .
muhilivé yotakhala emreliwanyu ni yotakhala ekina . muhaweleke wira sorera oholo w atthu othene .
murima wa katekese
okhala axinna okawelana otteliwa murima ni ohawa .
yesu onnixuttiha wira niphentaneke ntoko axinna okhala wira muluku onipattunxe ori mmosaru ni onnaphenta atthu othene ahathanlaka .
hiyo othene n àn awe .
nimonaka mutthu onihawa walá onvonya , khaninwerya omàla ni wikhurana , mana mmus ihu , òphentiwa ni muluku .
nimukhaliheryeke wira arerihe makhalelo awe . yesu ohakhwela atthu othene .
ovekela
apwiya muluku tith ihu , munivahe murima worera , wira nettihaneke ntoko axinna , nikawelanaka sorera sinivahalyanyu .
ovanela ni olehana
mmus ihu awereiwaka ninnirowa omuxekurya hatá akhalaka ottaiwene .
ankhi namwattamanan ihu a nihimo nikina awereiwaka , nnira sai ?
akristu èkekhai anaphenta ni analevelela a nloko nayaru pahi ?
namonaka mukhw ihu alimaka ematta yulupale , walá atenkene empa yorera , ninnisiveliwa ni yowo , walá nimmukhalela nrima ?
ale arina mihakhu yireke exeni wira ekhaleke apatthani akhw aya òthoiwa ?
nireke exeni wira noniherye okhalihana othene ntoko axinna ?
ovaha wàla , wimana wariká !
muluku iralé : an ak awo ! .
makhalelo ahu
khalai vavirikana ni vano , mana itthu sinjene sorukunuwa .
axitith ihu a khalai yarowa vai otumiha miritti saya ?
okathi w ekhotto onnilikana ni vano ?
itthu sothene sirukunuwaka , sinnithonyerya okelela oholo w atthu ni wunnuwa w elapo .
khula mutthu onniphavela oreriha makhalelo awe .
okilathi t okhwa .
namanyonyiwa , oholo khan etthu .
wahivareke muteko , onona mwanene . vatthokoni ninnivara miteko siniphwanyiha murerelo , ntoko oteka empa , olima , wapeya , okattha ikuwo , okwesa mpani ni vaté .
masu a muluku
amusi aka , kinnotumereryani ni nsina n apwiya yesu kristu wira , muhettaneké amusi anetta vohiloka , ehinatthara ikano siwixuttihalyakani .
nyuwo mwaxinene mosuwela enamuna y okitakiha miyo . miyo nkinette ni nyuwo vohiloka , walá nkitonko olya mahala yolya y anene .
ohiya vo , kanikukhumuwa n uhawa othana n uhiyu , kivaraka muteko , wira kihimukhule nnákhala mmosa a nyuwo .
khahiyó wira nkaphwanela okhaliheriwa ni nyuwo , nto kaphavela wothonyeryani ephiro , wira mukitakiheke .
okathi waryaka ni nyuwo , kanohimeryani wira : mutthu ohintthuna ovara muteko khamphwanela olya .
vekekhai , kihìwa wira eriyari anyu àkhala atthu ònyonyiwa , anihiya ovara muteko , enatthuwatthuwa ehivaraka etthu .
yala kinnaruma , katumereryaka ni nsina n apwiya yesu kristu , wira evareke muteko ni murettele , ni siso elyeke yolya ekukhumuwenlyaya mmansaya .
vano nyuwo , amusi aka , muhojeleké wira sorera .
akhalá mutthu ohinlwelela ikano sihimyalyaka mpapheloni-mu , mmusuwelihe , mmuhiye akhaleke mekhawe , wira uliwe muru , nto muhimwettiherye ntoko nwanan inyu munvahe miruku , okhala wira mmus inyu .
murima wa katekese
muluku onipattunxe anivahaka ekumi n ankhili wira nakiheryeke makhalelo ahu ni nikeliheryeke oholo nivaraka muteko .
yesu onninixuttiha wira muluku onnaphenta atthu othene ntoko an awe , ontthuna wira othene ekhalaneke ekumi ni mukhalelo worera .
mwaha wa muteko onvarahu t onrerihanahu ekumi ahu .
muluku onimwavaha atthu othene ikuru n ankhili , wira eruweryeke sorera sinaphiyerya .
ale anlovela muteko ale antthyawa miteko sa mmatta , ale aniwehererya simphavelaya wohukhuwa , othene aya annanula ephome akhw aya anvara muteko ni annihonona makhalelo àtthu othene mulaponi .
yesu ahinatthi owixuttiha atthu molumo a muluku apajenrye mwanene ovara miteko sa mmatta ni so kalapintero aphwanyihaka murerelo vatthokoni v axitithi awe ni mulaponi mwawe .
neteteyeke wira an ihu yixutteke miteko ntoko okalapintero , opaterero , wupa mwapu , otthava ntthatto , ethokwa ni miteko sikina .
nihana wukhuwa vanjene wira emp ahu ekhaleke yorera ni yotthuneliwa sana , niphaveleke oreriha nipuro n orupa n an ihu , niphaveleke itthu sinàpeliwa ni sinlyelyiwa niphaveleke mesa , ikhattera , mikhora , elatirina .
nipasopeke wira nihimwarexeke musurukhu n itthu sihimphwanyiha murerelo vatthokoni , ntoko evinyu , khankala , esuruma .
vatthokoni vannirerela wàla miri sa mihokorokho ntoko :
mipaphaya. miraranje , milimau , mikole , mana mihokorokho saya nalyaka , sinnikhaliherya ophwanya ekumi yorera .
ovekela
muluku tith ihu , munivahe ikuru wira nivareke sana miteko sahu , wira nikhaliheryeke murerelo w atthu othene .
ovanela ni olehana
mutthu mukumi , onkhotta ovara muteko , onokilathi pahi , awehereryaka ovahiwa , onoreriha mukhalelo w ekumi ?
ti sivi itthu sulupalexa mutthu sirinawe wetetela wira vatthokoni vawe ni mmawani okhaleke murerelo ?
miteko xeni axitithi sinonaya orerela owixuttiha an aya. wira oholo saphwanyiheke makhalelo òrera vatthokoni vaya ?
khula mutthu ahimyeke muteko onrowawe ovara vaté vawe .
onyonyiwa khunlyiwa , onlyiwa otthuwatthuwa !
muluku khanira : munyawe wira kovaheni !
otthenkaseya w ovolowa
katekista amuhimeryeke ansiau wira wophiya okathi wo waweha aprekatekúmeno .
yiwananeke nihiku nintthunaya othukumana n akristu , alattuliweke animadore a zona .
ethukumanaka , numala ovekela eroho yowarya , esomeke mwettiheryo wa makatekúmeno .
eweheke makhalelo aprekatekúmeno vanjenexa vatthokoni vaya , yakhanle wira ahòniherya oru kunuxa murima .
etthokeleleke enamuna yo wakhaliherya omutthara sana pwiy ahu yesu .
yari wira evoloweke nanano walá yululeke mithukwnano s aprekatekúmeno .
yakhalaka mwayawo ahinrerela ovolowa , ansiau ni katekista ewihaneke ni yahimeryeke wira epajeryeke olokiha makhalelo aya ni vatthokoni vaya .
ahinatthi opaka muthukumano mukina .
makhalelo ahu
katekista àkoheke aprekatekúmeno muteko xeni ovanryaya vale vaya , wira ereriheke etthoko aya .
olelo va ninrowa wupuwela molumo niwalyahu mithukumano sivinre . mwa molumo othene yiwalyanyu mpakha va , t avi akhanle mmurimani mwahu ?
khula prekatekúmeno àkhuleke , ahòvaka ni ahònaka ehaya .
murima wa katekese
ovolowa ephiro y okristu ti omutthara yesu .
murwaka okela nloko nahu nla , hiyo akristu othene notteliwa murima , nnowakhelani .
ninnisuwela wira atthu khankhala mekhaya , àkhalana nihimo naya n atat aya anaholela , yawo t aniwatàniha amusi othene a nloko nlo ntoko sinonelaya orera .
vano hiyo n àkristu , mulupale ahu ti yesu kristu .
owo òvirikana ni mamwene a vathí-va , mana orwenle owatàniha atthu a maloko othene , wira ephentaneke ni ekhaliheryaneke ntoko axinna .
atthu akina khiwasivenle mwixuttiho wa yesu . tivo yaiwanannyaya omwiva , emukhomelaka vamwikimanyo .
hatá akhomeliwene siso , yesu khonne onyanyaliwa ni muluku tithi awe , nto ahimuroromela yowo .
tthiri muluku khawerya omunyanyala mwan awe .
tivó vamuhihimuxalyawe mw alipa-okhwa .
yesu òhihimuwa , mukumi ni onkhala mapuro othene .
vano onninitthana hiyo wira nimutthareke naphentaka atthu othene .
esumana eyo nvolowaka ephiro y okristu , munrowa watàna n amus ihu othene anettela ephiro yeyo vathi-va .
àlakiherye itthu sintthunaya wira , makatekúmeno evarelaka mwikimanyo n anamuku aya etthittaka nlepa na mwikimanyo vayuji v an aya .
àhimerye ntoko silempwaya wira :
esumana eyo , khula mmosa a nyuwo onorowa oholo ovarela mwikimanyo , ammanelaka yesu natiri òkhotta sotakhala , ntoko : wiva , wiya , oraruwa , wotha , ohapaliwa , ohiwanana vatthokoni , n itthu sikinaku sotakhala .
mana ti sotakhala seiyo simwivale yesu .
niraka sotakhala iyo ninnimukhotta yesu onnitthana wira niphentaneke .
nimupuwele yesu okhwale akhomeliwaka vamwikimanyo , wira awatànihe atthu a maloko othene , àkhaliheryeke ottharuwa sottheka saya .
yesu ahihimya wira :
ole ontthuna okitthara miyo , aikhotte mwanene akapatte nihiku ti nihiku mwikimanyo awe , akitthareke .
ni molumo ala yesu onninitumererya wira , hatá niphwanyaka itthu sorika , nimwaminiki yes uwo , nimuroromeleke .
hiyo n atthu òlosowa , nilompeke okathi wothene , vanjenexa vosisu , othana eriyari n uhiyu .
apwiya yesu !
miyo kintthuna okhotta sotakhala sothene wira kottharekeni nyuwo .
ekwaha yopacerya y okatekumeno
biblia :
masu a muluku a nloko ni masu a nloko na muluku
mithukumano sivinre nihiwa wira muluku òphavela vanjene owatàniha atthu a maloko othene , mana tithi aya , vano awo othene axinná .
tivó muluku vapajenryawe walavuliha atthu a nloko na isarayeli wira mwaha wa yawo , atthu a maloko othene esuweleke otthuna wawe w owatàniha .
muluku ahàlavuliha anaisarayeli awoniheryaka waphenta wawe mwa itthu sothene sakhumelela .
mmakhaleloni mwaya mothene anaisarayeli yanithonyerya omwamini muluku ni watàna ni yowo : n isipo sipaya , n ikoma sìnaya , ni mavekelo yalompaya , n ikano salakiheryaya an aya .
mwa itthu sakhumelela , yanikupali wira ti muluku awettiha :
mohawani ti muluku attaruxa sottheka saya ;
movelavelani muluku ti ntthyawelo naya ;
mopuhani yanimuttottopela muluku awoponle , elaihanaka wamorela ikharari akhw aya , ntoko muluku sàmorenlyawe .
wopaceryani , sahivira iyakha sinjene atthu awo ehisuwelaka olepa , masi axitithi yanahimerya an aya wahala òwopoliwa opakiwe ni muluku .
vottharelana , akina mwa yawo yahupuxeriwa ni muluku wira emulepeke wahala àmuhakhalai aya , isipo saya , malompelo aya n ikano sàvahaya an aya wira emwaminiki muluku à woponle , yatàneke ni yowo , emuroromeleke natiri ammanenlyawe .
molumo aya othene yalempwe ti biblia orinahu , onnihimerya watàna wa nloko na isarayeli ni muluku .
biblia ahivira alempwaka iyakha sinjene n atthu anjene a nloko nlo .
ti muluku awupuxenrye atthu awo ekekhai yatthunaya olepa .
siso solempwa ilivuru miloko mixexe n ithanu na mosa , seiyo sinnalakela ephattu , ni makhalelo ni sokhumelela sa nloko na isarayeli ni watàna waya ni muluku .
ilivuru iyo sinihaniwa watàna wa khalai .
ilivuru iyo opaceryawene silempwe okanàni , opalestina , numalá ilapo sikina ntoko vamwaramwareiyaya anaisarayeli awo mwaha wa maxakha yakhumelela , ntoko obabilonia , wejitu , osiria , ogresia .
alipa-òlepa othene yahupuxeriwa ni muluku mitthaka saphavelawe wahimerya atthu othene .
ehapari yorerexa t ila :
muluku onkhala vamosá n atthu othene , onnaphenta ni onniphavela owòpola .
owo onnatàna n atthu , onnathukumanya nloko nimosa n an awe , onnalaiherya opuha wohimala .
nto alipa-òlepa awo khiyakhanle okathi omosarú nnákhala elapo emosaru ni makhalelo aya yahivirikana .
yanalepela atthu òkathi aya ni nttava naya , ehimyaka itthu sakhumelela okathi ule mulaponi mwaya .
vano hiyo namusomaka biblia niphaveleke toko osuwela makhalelo àtthu òkathi ule walempwe wira nittemuleleke mitthaka muluku saphavelawe onihimerya hiyo mahiku ahu ala mwaha wa itthu sinkhumelela , sihana epantte yovirikana n iye sa khalai n epantte yolikana .
mwanene ilivuru iyo ti muluku awupuxenrye atthu awo olepa .
sisotho hiyo nisomeke nimwaleliwaka ni muluku , yowo omphavela watàna ni hiyo mwaha wa masu awe alempwe .
watàna wa khalai onetetela watàna wa nanano , mana onimulaleya mòpoli àtthu , orummwe ni muluku .
owo ti yesu kristu , onatàniha maloko othene .
numala ohihimuwa wawe yesu mokhwani , solempwa-tho ilivuru miloko mili n ithanu na pili , seiyo sinihaniwa watàna wa nanano .
mwa ilívuru iya , ixexe sinireliwa ehapari yorera .
seiya sinihimya makhalelo , molumo , sowira ni miteko sa yesu kristu .
ilívuru iya ixexe silempwe ni matheyo , ni marko , ni luka , ni yohani .
ilivuru sikina sinihimya makhalelo àkristu òpacerya ni molumo arummwa a yesu yawixuttihaya atthu .
molumo ò watàna wa nanano annitaphulela molumo ò watàna wa khalai .
yesu kristu onnimaliherya molumo othene a biblia , mana ti nsu na muluku , nipanke mutthu , ti muluku onetta vamosá n atthu .
biblia othene ori ntoko mwiri .
mitathari ti maprofeta alempe watàna wa khalai , emuroromelaka muluku atthuna ommaliherya natiri awe .
mwiri ti yesu kristu ommalihenrye natiri a muluku aivahereryaka mokhwani mwaha wo waphenta atthu othene , khuhihimuwa .
iritta ni mihokorokho t arummwa n akristu òpacerya alempe watàna wa nanano emwaminiki yesu ohihimuwale ni emuttharaka .
vano hiyo namusomaka biblia , ninnivahiwa ororomela wa maprofeta ni wamini w arummwa wira natàneke ni yesu onniphentexa , hiyo-tho nikhaleke iritta sawe nimaka mihokorokho sorera so wiwanana n atthu a maloko othene .
sorera muluku sawirenlyawe atthu a isarayeli , yowo ontthuna-tho onirela hiyo .
makhalelo ahu
omalamala w elimwe , ohiyu ononeya overunya ni eniwanyeya etari .
itthu iya ithonyeryo so wattamela w eyita .
atthu annihimya wira muluku onokukutteya .
ale ahilokinhe emp aya annipacerya olokiha wira ehimoré .
masu a muluku
nsu na muluku ninniruma mmàsini , muluku òvuwa onnikukutteya , nsu na muluku ninnikhuwela mphareya .
owerya wa muluku onnikhera miri , onnintakasa miri sorekamexa .
nsu na muluku ninnithukumeliha miyako : ninnituphiha miyala ntoko ntthupi .
nsu na muluku ninnikawanya overunya
nsu n apwiya ninnithukumeliha itakhwa
murima wa katekese
muluku onninilavuliha ni onninikhaliherya omusuwela yowo mwa sokhumelela mmakhaleloni mwahu .
khalaixa , vakhiviru iyakha ekonto emosá ni iyakha imiya pili , elapo yo kanàni , olelo okhanle opalestina , nahikhala nloko n amakampusi yetetasa mmathalani ni mmiyakoni elyihaka inama saya .
awo yaitthaniwa anaisarayeli . mulupale apajenrye nloko nlo t abrahamu . yowo ahithamela okanàni akhumaka elapo ekina yottaiwene vakhiviru miyakha imiya thanu na mosa sihinatthi .
anaisarayeli awo yanamini wira muluku ahinvaha elapo eyo abrahamu owo wira axisulu awe ekhaleke .
okanàni weiwo sahikhala-tho mittetthe sarukureriwe ni makokoro . khula muttetthe warina mwene aya n anakhotto aya awo yanalupattha amakampusi wira envaheke mwene inama saya , okhala wira ti mwanene elapo .
amakampusi yanikhotta opuheriwa ni mamwene awo ni yanamini wira muluku .
anaisarayeli yaniwupuwela amuhakhalai aya yathamenle wejitu weiwo yahivarihiwa miteko sa ipottha ni mwené òlapo eyo , nto muluku ahiwopola .
awo khiyàsuwela olepa , khiyàrina ilivuru , masi yanalakiherya an aya wahal aya ni omwamini waya muluku .
ovekela
muluku t ikuru saka , wilipiha waka ni wopowa waka .
avuwihiwe muluku !
muluku òkikumiha movelavelani owo òkòpola , mana onnikiphenta .
ovanela ni olehana
ninnikupali wira muluku ori ni hiyo ni wira t onnikhapelela ?
ninnikupali wira molumo awe t annivaha ekumi ni ohakalala ?
makhalelo xeni yarinaya amuhakhalai ahu ?
ikano xeni sinihiyenryaya ?
makhalelo aya yalikana n awo ànaisarayeli ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
muluku t axariya ni t òroromeleya , onkhala vamosá n atthu , onnalakiherya watàna .
muluku ahimyá , khavo onvanya !
khavo ònne , khavo osuwenle ephattuwelo y olumwenku ni okathi aya .
ekekhai ti wira elapo yopacerya okhala votthima wa muluku opattunxe wira ekhale nipuro norera , ninkhalaya atthu òwitthyala yatànaka ni muluku ni yaworu .
itthu sothene sipattuxeriwe atthu okhala akumi ni òtteliwa murima .
elivuru yopacerya ya biblia ti maphattuwelo , elempwe okathi anaisarayeli yavareliwaya omalaponi obabilonia .
atthu alempe atakaniherya ithale salakeleliwaya n amuhatithi aya .
yanalepela akhw aya yavareliwe wira ewiriyaneke mmithukumanoni mwaya khula esábadu .
adamu ni hawa t alopwana n athiyana othene .
obabilonia wanikokhoreliwa nsuwa ni mweri , yahikhala amuluku òpatthiwa a maluku ni a mwiri . anaisarayeli yanehereriwa wakokhorela amuluku awo èthiru .
sosoma iyo s asábadu sanilipiha wamini waya wira yatàneke ni muluku akhweli yowo awoponle amuhakhai aya wejitu , wakhalihiwaya ipottha .
khivo etthu hatá ekhalaka yulupale ni yowerya eri muluku .
owo ori mmosá pahi , òhinòneya .
àpattunxe atthu àvahaka ekumi yarinawe .
awo t akhanle ekhove ya muluku itthu sikina sothene sipattuxiwe , muluku ohavaha atthu wira esukeke ni evarelaneke miteko sinarerela othene aya .
maluku khantthuna wira atthu akinu yakhalihe akhw aya ipottha yakhanyererihaka ovara muteko khula nihiku , ntoko sakhanyererihiwaya anaisarayeli obabilónia .
atthu othene apattuxiwe elikanyihiwaka ni maluku owo òpattuxa olumwenku mahiku mathanu na mosa , siso-tho atthu evareke muteko mahiku mathanu na mosa nihiku nanethanu nenli , othene anniphwanela omumula .
makhalelo ahu
hiyo othene ninnisiveliwa okhala vamuttutthini , nsuwa naluttuwa , ninnolya vamosá n an ihu mihokorokho sa miri .
ohiyu nonaka mweri waryaka , osulu osareiyene itheneri , ninkhala òsiveliwa .
nave-tho ninnisiveliwa okhalana màsi òrera wira niwuryeke , nrapeke , nikattheleke ikuwo sahu .
hiyo ninnisuwela enamuna yarowahu okhala , naharina itthu iya ?
sothene iya sihana murerelo mwekumini mwahu ?
itthu iya n iye sothene sinònahu sinkhuma vai ?
masu a muluku
wopaceryani , muluku opattunxe erimu n ilapo ya vathí .
vano elapo yira ehinatthi omalelihiwa , khiyàkhanle etthu ekumi ;
màsi yarokhuneleya ni piphi ; vano iphumu sa muluku sarophuramwela vamàsini .
vano muluku ahira : okhumelele okokola !
okokola wahikhumelela .
muluku ahona wira okokola iwo wari worera , khuvalànya okokola ni piphi . vano muluku ahivaha okokola iwo nsina n othana , khuvaha epiphi nsina n ohiyu .
vano vàhila ni vàhixa : siso nahikhala nihiku nopacerya .
muluku ahira-tho : ekhalé erimu eriyari ya màsi , wira evalanye màsi awo vawaya-vawaya .
muluku ahipattuxa erimu , khuvalànya màsi yari vathi n ale yari osulu .
muluku ahivaha osulu iwo nsina na erimu .
muluku ahona wira vorera . vano vàhila ni vàhixa : siso nahikhala nihiku nanenli .
muluku ahira-tho : màsi ari vathi va erimu ethukumane nipuro nimosa , yòneye etthaya yolipa .
siso vàhiraneya . nipuro nlo nowuma muluku ahivaha nsina na etthaya , vano nipuro nathukumanne màsi ahivaha nsina na ephareya . muluku ahona wira vorera .
muluku ahira-tho : etthaya emeleke sorerela sa khula enamuna : makukhu ni malaxi anima epyó ni miri sinima mihokorokho sikhalanne inuku saya .
siso vàhiraneya .
etthaya yahimela sorerela sa khula enamuna makukhu ni malaxi anima ipyó sa muxovo aya , sikhalanne inuku saya .
muluku ahona wira vorera .
vano vàhila ni vàhixa : siso nahikhala nihiku naneraru .
muluku ahira-tho : sikhalé mithuko wirimu , wira sivalànye ohiyu ni othana , wira sisuweliheke mahiku ni miyeri n iyakha , seiyo-tho sikhala mithuko sa wirimu sinimwalèla elapo .
siso vàhiraneya .
muluku ahipattuxa mithuko mili sulupale : mmosá mulupalexa wira omwalèleke othana , mukina mwamukhani wira omwalèleke ohiyu ahipattuxa-tho itheneri .
muluku ahipweha mithuko iyo wirimu , wira simwalèleke elapo , sèttiheke othana ni ohiyu , sivalànye okokola n ipiphi . muluku ahona wira vorera .
vano vãhila ni vàhixa : siso nahikhala nihiku nanexexe .
muluku ahira-tho : mmàsini satteke itthu sikumi , navé musulu evaveke axinuni .
siso vàhiraneya . tthiri muluku ahipattuxa inama sulupale sa mphareya n itthu sothene sikumi sa khula enamuna sinetta mmàsini , ahapattuxa-tho axipalame othene anvava musulu , khula enama muxovo aya .
muluku ahona wira vorera .
muluku ahireriha inama iyo , iraka :
murelaneke , munjereryeke musareyeke mmàsini a mphareya axipalame etotholaneke mulaponi .
vano vàhila ni vàhixa : siso nahikhala nihiku nanethanu .
muluku ahira-tho : mulaponi sitotholaneke itthu sikumi sa khula enamuna : inama sa vaté n iye sinípurula n inama sa mutakhwani , khula enama muxovo aya .
siso vàhiraneya .
muluku ahipattuxa inama sowali sa mutakhwani n inama sa vaté n iye sinípurula vathi , khula enama muxovo aya .
muluku ahona wira vorera .
murima wa katekese
muluku t orerexa murima n itthu sothene sipattuxalyawe ti sorera .
olumwenku opattuxiwe ni muluku , khahiyó orokhumelelasa pahi .
muluku , opattunxe itthu sothene , ori mmosa pahi ni t òweryexa .
ephattuwelo n imalelo sa itthu sothene siri mwa muluku .
yowo pahi t onavaha atthu itthu sothene wira sarumeleke .
nsuwa , mweri , itheneri , ni sothene simphwanyaneya mulaponi mu , khahiyó amuluku ;
sothene sipattuxiwe ni muluku , anipattuxeryaka hiyo nri an awe .
ekumi yothene enrwa wa muluku . wira ninnuwihe ekumi ahu , nihana omusuwela sana muluku ni wiwelela masu awe .
narumelaka itthu , nimuxukhuruku muluku opattunxe sothene , wira sikhale murerelo ahu .
mwanene ekumi ti muluku : niphavelaka oreriha ekumi ahu , nitthareke molumo awe .
muluku t òrerexa murima , itthu sothene sipattuxiwe ni yowo ti sorera : khivo-vo etthu erinahu othanya , nakhelakaru n omuxukhuru muluku .
muluku oniweryexa sothene , khumurikenle opattuxa sothene .
muluku opattunxe sothene ni nsu nawe .
nsu na muluku ti noweryexa , khivo etthu muluku enojelawe .
masu a muluku makumi : annira etthu enihimyaya .
ovekela
nyuwo atthu òrera murima , munvuwihe muluku .
molumo àpwiya t ororomeleya , miteko saya sothene sinnitthara ekekhai .
elapo yothene yosareya orera waya murima .
nulumo na muluku nopattuxa erimu : nsuwa , mweri n itheneri sipattuxiwe ni yowo .
nyuwo atthu a maloko othene , mwattittimihe apwiya .
ovanela ni olehana
ninnitteliwa murima ni murerelo wa itthu sothene sinonahu ntoko miri sinima mihokorokho walá ipyo sa mmatta ?
nimuxukhuruku sai muluku onipattuxenrye itthu iya sothene ?
ninlokiha ni ninlima muluku onipattuxenrye itthu iya sothene ?
nìreke exeni wira nakiheryeke itthu sorera sipattuxiwe ni muluku ni ninjereryeke ?
nihiku nattiminku ninniruha ipyo sa mmatta wira navahe okathi w ovelela , wira nimuxukhuru muluku ni nakhaliheryeke ale òthoiwa ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
muluku ti mpattuxa ni pwiya a wirimu ni èlapo ya vathi .
owo ti tithyihu onniphenta .
mavaheryo a muluku wàtta !
makhalelo ahu
hiyo ninnaphenta axitith ihu aniyanre , an ihu n axinn ihu arina ephome ahu emosaru ;
mwettelo ahu onolikana .
nave-tho nàlikanaka ni mwan ihu , ninnisiveliwa vanjene .
ayariwaka mwana , etthu yopacerya axitithi awe amphavelaya osuwela , ti wi mwan ihu onnilikana ni hiyo .
siso muluku onsiveliwa wira atthu elattaneke n uwo àpattunxe àphentaka ntoko amama animphentaya mwan aya .
masu a muluku
muluku ahira : nimùpe mutthu onlattanahu , onlikana ni hiyo .
akhalé mwanene ihopa sa mphareya n ipalame sa musulu n inama sa vaté n inama sowali sa mutakhwani n iye sothene simpurula vathi .
muluku ompattuxale mutthu , ailikanyihaka mmansawe muluku ompattuxale mutthu , ailattanihaka mwanene . muluku , àpattuxaka atthu , âpakalé alopwana n athiyana .
vano muluku ahareriha , àhimeryaka wira : mwayareke an inyu , munjerereyeke : musareyeke mulaponi mothene . mwettiheke elapo yothene .
apwiya muluku yahihavula etthaya vakhani ya vathi , yahimupa mutthu , khumwiselela mphulani n iphumu s ekumi : siso mutthu khukhala mukumi .
apwiya muluku yahihimya wira : khivamurèrenle mutthu okhala mekhawe .
kintthuna ompattuxerya mukhaliheryo womphwanela .
vano apwiya muluku yahimuruhela mulopwana ikhove sinjene : varupalyawe , yahimukumiha eparari emosã , nipuro naya yahipharihela-vo ethayi .
eparari yakuxalyaya wa mulopwana , apwiya muluku yahimupa muthiyana , khumuroihela mulopwana .
vano mulopwana , vamònalyawe muthiyana , ahihimya wira : tthiri ola nikhuva na makhuv aka , erutthu y erutthu aka ! ola nsina nawe ti muthiyana , okhala wira okumihiwé mwa mulopwana .
tivó mulopwana onahiyawe atithi awe n ame awe , anakhala vamosá ni mwar awe , òwanli aya enakhala ntoko mutthu mmosaru pahi .
vano òwanli aya , mulopwana ni mwar awe , yakhala pwitipwiti , nto khiyònasa ehaya .
murima wa katekese
muluku àpattuxerya atthu makhalelo owatàna .
mutthu ti pani ?
opattuxeriwe-ni ?
hiyo n àpani ?
ninkhalela-ni ?
mutthu , mulopwana ni muthiyana , ti muteko wa muluku wotepaxa orera !
atthu othene , hatá akhalaka mwanamwane , mulipa-òrakala walá namukhw anepa , apattuxiwe ni muluku , khuvahiwa murerelo mmosaru .
muluku ti tithi a khula mutthu , yowo pahi t ukhanle mwanene atthu .
oninveha mutthu , onninveha muluku ; vano onimuttittimiha mutthu , onnimuttittimiha muluku .
mutthu onlattana ni muluku atànaka n atthu othene .
muluku ompattuxale mutthu , ailikanyihaka mmansawe àpakalé alopwana n athiyana .
khivamurèrenle mutthu okhala mekhawe .
molumo ala a bíblia anninihimerya wira atthu , aniphentana mukina ni mukhw awe , annilikanyihiwa ni muluku , mana owo ophentá .
muluku onninvaha khula mutthu owerya w osuwela , w otthuna ni w ophenta wira akhaleke atànaka n akhw awe .
khula mutthu onniphwanela ottittimihiwa n uphentiwa n akhw awe othene , n uwotho ohana wattittimiha ni waphenta akhw awe .
otthuna wa muluku ti watàna w atthu , khula mmosa avaraka muteko onarerela atthu othene .
mulipa-ònyonyiwa , namuhapaliwa n alipa-ottheka othene , annihonona watàna w atthu ntoko muluku sintthunawe .
mulopwana ni muthiyana annilattana ni muluku ephentanaka vatthokoni .
mulopwana ni muthiyana anthelana annilikanyihiwa ni muluku ephentanaka .
khula mmosa onninvaha mukhw awe murerelo awe n ikuru sawe wira emaliheryaneke mukina ni mukhw awe , enakhala ntoko mutthu mmosaru pahi .
anniphentana vekekhai khula mmosa upuwelaka ni murima wa mukhw awe , ònaka ni maitho a mukhw awe , ahawaka n iretta ya mukhw awe .
vatthokoni walá mulaponi axinene khahiyó alopwana pahi , nnákhala athiyana pahi .
khavo opattuxeriwe okhalihiwa epottha .
othene n àxinene elapo .
anamwane ti muhokorokho w ophentana waya amai n atithi vatthokoni .
othene aya ahana ovara muteko wo walela ni wo wahuwa .
anamathelana yahiyareke , khahiyó mulattu womwalanela , okhala wira nlelo muluku onnareriha òwanli ni onniwitthanela wunnuwa vamosá mophentani mummaleliheryanaya mulopwana ni muthiyana .
ovekela
vanwehaka erimu , muteko wa matat anyu , kònaka mweri n itheneri sipwehalyanyu-vo .
nyuwo mompattuxa mutthu onihala vakhani olikana ni nyuwo momusariha ovuwa ni nttittimiho .
momukhaliha mwanene itthu sipakalyanyu monvaha owerya w oruma itthu sothene .
ovanela ni olehana
anniphentana vekekhai ale anupuwela ni anòna ni murima wa mukhwa ya :
ti siso sinirahu vatthokoni vahu ?
niriná murima mmosá ?
nnupuwela-ni mwaha w axilopwan ale anahiya axar aya mulattu w ohiyaraka ?
ti yorera omukhaliha muthiyana epottha wira àyareke ni àhuweke anamwane ni amurumeleke iy awe ?
aximama n axitata , yàlelaka yawo pahi ana a vatthokoni , emuhiyaka ottuli pap aya , annittharihela otthuna wa muluku ?
vano papa àleleke sai an awe ?
nisukeke mmurima ni mwahu
muluku ompattuxale mutthu , ailattanihaka mwanene , owo àpattunxe alopwana n athiyana , ahivirikanyihaka mattittimiheriwo aya .
ehipa khenlima ehina nvini !
ntata mekhaya khaninteka empa !
othanyana khunvolowa mpani .
othelana ovilelá .
makhalelo ahu
elapo emosá yahikhala etakhwa yarina nratta okathi wothene nanikhalana màsi , yahawelela .
sanikhala ihopa .
atthu a muttetthe ole yaniphwanya màsi ni mathapa .
vano ahiphiya vavale mutthu mmosá aphavelasa miri sopakela ithapwa .
ahipacerya wuha , khulima vavale ematta yulupale ya nxotte . anamuteko awe yahitthela vatthiyani murette wira yivé ihopa .
vaphiyalyaya elimwe , nratta nle nahiwelela .
muttetthe mukina wahikhala muró wowakuva òwelela .
nto atthu yanihawela màsi .
atthu akina a muttetthe yowo yahupuwela ottiya mur owo wira nipakeye nratta .
siso yahivara mutek owo , khuthukumana màsi manjene . sanikhala vavo ihopa sinjene .
muxerexere mwaya yahàla mo minika ni mimanka , mikhasu , enalima-tho mihokorokho sikina .
màsi awo annireriha makhalelo àtthu a muttetthe ole mpakha vano .
masu a muluku
wopaceryani , okathi muluku opattuxalyawe miteko sawe , òvalanya sikina n ikhw aya .
òvaha itheneri sawe miteko saya wa mahiku othene , okhuma opattuxiwa waya mpakha wokiseryani waya .
numalá , muluku ahiweha vathí , khusariha sovaha sawe .
òsariha vathi inama sa khula muxovo inama iyo sinotthikela vathí vakhumalyaya .
muluku ohápattuxa atthu ni oloko , àpattuxeryaka ohokolowela vatthayani .
owo òwalakelela atthu mahiku aya ni okathi wolikana , khwavaha owerya w oruma itthu sothene .
ohàvaha atthu ikuru solikana ni sawawe , ohàpattuxa atthu àlattanihaka n owo .
ohàvaha owerya wo wopopiha itthu sothene sikumi , wira atthu erumeke inama sowali n axinuni .
muluku ohàvaha atthu ankhili ni nlumi ni maitho ni màru ni murima wira etthokeleleke .
ohasariha ankhili ni osuwela ohathonyerya mwettelo worera ni mwettelo wotakhala .
òhela osuwela mmirimani mwaya , wira yoneke wunnuwa wa miteko sawe .
murima wa katekese
muluku ònivaha ankhili wira nivareke muteko , nisukeke itthu wira sarumeleke atthu othene .
niwehaka muxerexere mwahu ninnona miri , malaxi , inama sa khula muxovo , imatta , isòpe , ipalame n axikokho :
sothene iya sipattuxeriwe wira sikina sikhalé soly ahu , sikina sowara sahu , sikina siphwaneliheke elapo .
muluku ohavaha atthu othene elapo ni mihakhu saya , khavahiwe atthu vakhani pahi .
khula mutthu ohana osuka murerelo wa itthu sipattuxeriwe atthu othene .
khula mutthu ni muteko awe onninnuwiha ekumi awe ni onnikhaliherya murerelo w atthu othene .
nihiku nnopexa nsuwa , vano hiyo khuvira nettaka n iphiro , nananoru khutthyawela mmuttutthini wa mwiri mulupale wowatta makukhu .
oviraka okathi vakhani ninnipacerya wakhela epheyo yorera ni yorirya , mpakha onrwela ikhove .
ti muteko w epheyo eyo enkhuma mmwirini mwaha wa makukhu makithi .
ale anuha miri sa mutakhwani vohitthokiheya , annihonona ekumi eniphavela miri sinakumiherya atthu epheyo yorera wira emumuleke sana .
opaha itakhwa onnihonona wunttelana wa imatta , onnumiha miro , onninjererya oviha , khunihiya sinnuwaka itthu sothene sikumi sirivo .
ninnihonona makhalelo ahu okathi wothene ninnanarihahu mapuro ankhalahu .
ntoko : mmuró ni mwehimeni munwuryahu , naitthelaka ikokhola , ilàta sa khalai n itthu sikina sonanara .
ahavo anjene ahininanela solya sinlyaya , nnâkhala màsi anwuryaya , khantokosa vanrowaya orusa n unya .
iphepele sinkotela vamavini , sinnikuxa miyuku sikhanixa mmettoni mwaya , khiyamorihela muyolyani ni mmàsini .
miyuku iyo sinninéla mwerutthuni mwahu , sinnivaha iretta . niteke esentina yovalana ni vaté .
nihirapeké vakhiviru v ehime ya màsi òwurya , nihitthuniheryé inama owurya n unanariha màsi awo .
ovekela
apwiya , muluku tith ihu , munipattunxe munilattanihaka ni nyuwo : munivahe ankhili n osuwela .
munithonyerye mwettelo worera ni mwettelo wotakhala , munikhaliherye oreriha makhalelo ahu .
ovanela ni olehana
atthu a mittetthe iye mili t avi aniwonanyu ottharihela masu a muluku , anihimya wira muluku ohàvaha atthu owerya w oruma itthu sothene ?
nettiheke ni nisukeke saí itthu muluku sinipattuxenryawe ?
nireke sai wira nivukule iretta ? nahapeyeke màsi ?
nihererya wàla miri sinima mihokorokho vaté vahu ?
nòvaka oloiwa , othipeliwa murette , ninnikupali okhala axinene itthu sothene ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
muluku ohàvaha atthu ankhili ni nlumi ni maitho ni màru ni murima wira etthokeleleke .
atthu maitho èlapo !
miruku khisiniyeva. oniyeva ti mwanene !
muluku khansiveliwa n upweteya w atthu akumi
mulakiheryo w etampi y adamu ni hawa onnoneya ntoko wahimmwe n anaisarayeli womaleloni w omwene wa salomoni owo ari òsuwelexa ni òweryexa , nto ahapuherya anaisarayeli .
owo ahaphenta axar awe anjene àmalapo athiyan awo yahihonona murim awe .
ahasiveliha yawo attharaka edini aya yahimya wira enowa ekokhoreliweke .
vuluvanlyawe ahira sotakhala , khaiwelenle samurummyawe muluku , khettenle exariya , khwavarihaka atthu miteko sowoma sinjene .
makhulupale anaisarayeli yanitthara mwettelo wonanara wa mwene aya , emuliyalaka muluku awoponle amuhatithi aya mwepotthani .
kayini ti yale othene anahukhumu ni aniwiva akhw aya .
mutaseke ni empa yorakamexa ya babeli , malikanyiho ahimmwe ni maprofeta wira anaisarayeli ettharuweke sotakhala siraya .
mamwene aya , ntoko salomoni uwo , ni makhulupale aya yanalielela mikuttho amuluku àmalapo , yaniteka ipa sorerexa ni sulupale yakhanyererihaka alipa-òthoiwa ovara miteko sowoma . itampi iyo saninveha muluku ni sanaphwanyiha atthu awo opweteya ni omwarexeliwa omalaponi .
itampi iyo ni ihukhumu saya sinnonaneya hatá mahiku ala .
biblia khannihimerya enamuna ene sakhumelenlyaya okhwa ni sotakhala sikina , nto onninithonyerya wira simphattuwa khula okathi atthu wammwalanaxa ni muluku ekhottaka molumo awe èkumi .
atakhali annilattula okhwa ni molumo aya ni miteko saxa .
makhalelo ahu
mulaponi mwahu sinnikhumelela itthu sinniripiha murima vanjene siniriwa n ale anipaka makhulukana , anihimya wira anikumiha mirette sinahonona atthu , nto aniwotherya ni aniwtyerya ale aniruwerya , elimaka mmatta .
miyo kihòna ni maitho ak ala .
makhulukan awo yahiphiya vatthokoni v asahuneti .
vakumihalyaya mirette sathipeliwe vamukhora , yahimukhanyererya waliva 300.000 mt , yahikuxa-tho isakho pili sa makhaka n epuri emosa .
yahirowa-tho etthoko yanenli , owannyawe sawaya . yahimukhanyererya waliva 200.000 mt , epuri emosa n esakho emosa ya ikole . etthoko yaneraru yaphiyalyaya , yahitepa opaka sa manyala emwirelaka mwanene wira ahana waliva 400.000 .
owo kharina musurukh uwo . nto awo yahikuxasa mijoma mili s omuro n ikuwo sothene .
vano yahitthukwa emp awe emwirelaka wira ahivolowe mpani mmo ahilinve toko . ahiliveru , emp eyo yorowa opahiwa .
ekhotto yomala , masi nlelo yohala ekhotto ya mmawani .
masu a muluku
enowa yari mulavilavi ovikana inama sothene sa mutakhwani apwiya muluku sipattuxalyaya .
enowa eyo yahimukoha muthiyana wira :
ekekhai wira muluku ohòkhottiheryani olya mihokorokho sa miri sothene sa mmatta ?
muthiyana ahakhula wira : ninniwerya olya mihokorokho sa miri sa mmatta . nto muhokorokho wa mwiri ori mmatta eriyari , muluku ohimyalé wira :
muhilyéru yowo , nnákhala muhivaréru yowo . mwalyaru , munimokhwa .
enowa yahimwakhula muthiyana wira :
nnari , khamunokhwa .
muluku onnisuwela wira nihiku ninkelanyu olya , maitho anyu anotthukuwa . nyuwo munokhala ntoko muluku , musuwelaka orèriwa n utakhaliwa .
muthiyana ahona wira mihokorokho sa mwiri ule sanirèrela , awehexexaka sanimukumiha murima , saniphwanela otthukula muru .
t arukunlyawe muhokorokho mmosá , khulya ; ahinvahatho iy awe ãrinawe , n uwo-tho khulyaka .
okathi ene yowo òwanli yahitthukuwasa maitho , khwisonelaka wira khiyawanr etthu . tivó yahitthavasa matakhuru a murale , khwitthukelasaka muyununi .
vano yahiwa mukhitto w apwiya muluku yettakasa mmatta , makáripi variryalene .
mulopwana ni mwar awe yahitthyawasa va maithoni v apwiya muluku , khwipithasa eriyari ya miri sa mmatta .
apwiya muluku yahimwihana mulopwana yiraka :
nyuwo muri vai ?
ahakhula wira :
kìwale mukhitto anyu mmatta , kihòva , okhala wira nkiwanre etthu , kihìpitha .
apwiya muluku khwira :
mulèliwé nani wira khanwanre etthu ?
murimolya muhokorokho wa mwiri ule wokhottihenryakani ?
mulopwana ahakhula wira :
muthiyana okivahalyanyu okhala mwar aka t okivahale muhokorokho , miyo kiholya .
vano apwiya muluku yahimukoha muthiyana yiraka :
mwirenle-ní siso ?
muthiyana khwakhula wira :
enowa p ikotonthe , miyo khulyaka .
vano apwiya muluku yahihimerya enowa wira :
okhala wira ohira siso , onotakhaliwa wa inama sothene sa vaté ni wa inama sothene sa mutakhwani .
onimwìpurulaka ni erukulu awo , onimolyaka etthaya mahiku othene ontthunawo okhala .
miyo kinowlnaniha weyo ni muthiyana , kinimwinaniha nloko nawo ni nloko na muthiyana , osulu awe onimonyakela muru , weyo ophavelaka oluma nnawu .
murima wa katekese
etampi enninimwalanyiha ni muluku n akhw ihu , enninikhaliha-tho ipottha .
muluku ohàpattuxa atthu òtaphuwene , wira ethanleke yorera votthuna waya , ehikhanyereriwaka , etteliweke murima yatànaka ni muluku .
vapattuxiwaya atthu yanitteliwa murima n irutthu aya , khiyòna ehaya , mana yanimuxukhuru muluku owùpale votikiniha .
ekhottaka omwiwelela muluku atthu àmalamaliha opatthani warinaya ni yowo , n akhw aya , n itthu sothene sipattuxiwe .
yahipacerya ohiwanana , wotheryana , owana ekhotto , ohitthunana , wunlelana ikuhu , ohaxana .
mwaha w etampi otakhala wokela molumwenkuni-mu .
muluku ophentá , khamwalanne opatthani wapakalyawe n atthu .
tivó vamuhimenryawe satana wira :
kinowinaniha weyo ni muthiyana
muthiyan owo ahimmwe , ti maria , oniyarenle yesu , mòpoli àtthu othene .
nimwalanaka ni muluku , mwanene ekumi , ninnihonona ekumi .
okathi ene yowo muluku onniniweha ni mphento , naisuwelaka wira nihira yotakhala , nivekele nlevelelo .
muluku onninakhela ni mphento n urera wawe murima .
ovekela
apwiya , mukimorele ikharari n uthunku anyu : n ulevelela wanyu muttipihe itampi saka !
muluku , kivaheni murima woloka , mukiruhele-tho eroho y ekekhai .
ovanela ni olehana
muluku ohàvaha atthu ankhili wira etthokeleleke .
okathi xeni atthu vapajenryaya ohawa ?
ti muhokorokh owo wàhononne , walá ohikupali waya ophentiwa ni muluku ?
nireke-ní wira nikhale atthu òwiwanana ?
hiyo niraka etampi , muluku onniweha sai ?
nìreke exeni wira wonaneyeke murettele mulaponi ?
khula mutthu upuweleke etampi enìrexawe .
athanleke eniweryawe ovara wira amalihe etamp iyo .
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
etampi onveha muluku , nikhottaka molumo awe .
muluku khanimuhiya mutthu !
makhalelo ahu
mário inmiravo mmosá àkhala n uthoiwa vanjene .
numalá omuthela mwar awe , ihaniwa isabeli , attharihaka ephattu , ahipacerya witthokihasa atthukulaka imatta sulupale sa nxotte , nakhuwo , mattuvi , ikhutte .
eyakha yamalaka , onniwerya okumiha solya sinjene seiyo sinkawanyawe ikina analya , ikina anatumiha .
khula eyakha onnitthokihasa musurukhu awe , anathuma iye simphavelawe , siso annikhalasa sana vaté vaya .
masi juwakhi , mulupale awe mário , ahipacerya omukhalela nrima n umunlela ehaje .
ahirowa ohakoni wira asuwele mota xeni muhim awe aruweryawe sisale .
ahilèliwa wira wari mwaha wa mirette , ni wira owo ahakhelele etthu p itthu yarowawe onvaha , nave-tho athamele ottaiwene .
vatthikenlyawe owani ahahimerya amusi n apatthani awe othene wira ehiphiyeke owanny awe mário , mana namirette .
masu a muluku
adamu ahikumanela ni hawa , mwar awe . owo ahirupala , khumuyara khayini . vano ahihimya wira : kojaliwa n apwiya komuyara mwan aka mwamulopwana .
vottharelana , ahimuyara-tho abeli , muhim awe kayini .
abeli ari makampusi a ipwittipwitthi , vano kayini ari mulipa-òlima .
vaphiyalyaya okathi w ohepha , kayini ahavaha apwiya mihokorokho sa mmatta .
abeli avahale inama sopacerya ototholiwa ni makhur aya . apwiya yahisiveliwa n abeli ni sovaha sawe , khuhisiveliwa ni kayini ni sovaha sawe . tivó kayini ahinanariwa vanjene owitho wawe wahirwela mannyari .
apwiya yahimwirela kayini wira : exeni enanareliwanyu ?
kayini ahimuhimerya muhim awe abeli wira : nrowe omatta .
vaphiyalyaya omatta , kayini ahimutuphela muhim awe abel , khumwìva .
vano apwiya yahimukoha kayini wira : abeli , muhim anyu , ori vai ?
kayini ahakhula wira : kahiki . khino miyo kàmulipeleli a muhim aka ?
apwiya yahimukoha-tho wira : mwirale-ní ?
ephome ya muhim anyu emwarenxanyu ennikikhuwelela miyo .
vano motakhaliwa , mòmoliwaka etthaya eyo ewunrye ephome ya muhim anyu omwivalyanyu .
mwalima vale , khamunruwerya , munokhala namutthyawatthyawa ni namwettakasi mulaponi .
kayini ahiwakhula apwiya , iraka : otakhaliwa waka khurere winnuwa , khunvileleya . vano , olelo vava munokòmola elapo ela , miyo kihana wipitha ottaiwene wa nyuwo , kinrowa okhala mmalapo kitthyawatthyawaka mulaponi .
apwiya yahimwakhula wira : weso , mutthu ene yowo onrowa owivani onimunleliwa ikuhu mpakha vathanu na venli .
vano apwiya yahimuhela kayini ekanyeryo , wira mutthu ti mutthu arowa okumana ni yowo ahimwivé .
murima wa katekese
onimwiva mutthu onnimutthekela muluku onvahale ekumi .
khula mutthu munn ihu .
muluku onnaphenta atthu othene ni onkhala ni yawo , hatá n ale anira sotakhala .
mutthu onimukhalela nrima mukhw awe , onnihonona omusi .
sotakhala sothene simpacerya mmurimani mwa mutthu , yowo opattuxiwe òtaphuwene wira athanleke yorera votthuna wawe , vohi khanyereriwa .
muluku onnimulavuliha mutthu mmurimani mwawe , onnimuhakalaliha , wira ahiripiweke murima .
nto ole onkhotta molumo a muluku ni onkhalela nthiti wupuwela yotakhala , onnira yeyo .
kayini ahikhotta molumo yahimeriwawe ni muluku : mwiraru sorera , ekhove anyu enimòkokolani .
siso ahithipelela , khumukhalela nrima muhim awe abeli , mwaha wa nrima nenlo ahimwiva muhim awe .
etthu yiralyawe kayini , annira-tho atthu akina animwiva mukhw aya vohikhala ni kapwitthi walá n ikatana pahi , nave-tho ni wòtha ni nrima n ulavilavi .
sothene iya sinnimwiva munnihu .
muluku khatthunale okhwa wa kayini , khantthuna-tho okhwa wa mutthu , hatá akhalaka natampi .
ola onohawa mwaha w etampi awe . masi aìsuweleke ni ahiruneke etthu yiralyawe hatá ahòniwe .
siso onoleveleliwa , onohokolowela okhala mpatthani a muluku .
ovekela
muluku tith ihu ,
nyuwo monipattuxa munlattanihaka ni nyuwo , munòpole mukhalelo ahu wotakhala .
mirima sahu sinnettela wisona ni nrima , munikhaliherye oxintta , nitteliweke murima mana nophentiwa ni nyuwo , naphenteke akhw ihu othene .
ovanela ni olehana
nimonaka mukhw ihu orina makhalelo òrera , ninnitteliwa murima walá ninnimwalanasa ni yowo nimotheryaka ?
wĩya , wiva , oraruwa , sonanara sothene sinkhuma mmurimani mwahu .
nikhotteke sai miyupuwelo sinniripiha murima ni sinniriha sotakhala ?
nimwiriheke exeni mutthu irale yotakhala ?
khula mutthu aphaveleke onvaha murettele mukhw ihu oninyokhanahu .
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
etampi ennihonona watàna wahu ni muluku n axinn ihu , ennaraviha atthu othene , ennihonona ekumi .
ntata navará màvi , khannikitthiwa , nnorapihiwa !
nrima wiva !
makhalelo ahu
niwiriyane epaphelo enilepenlyawe mam ihu mmosá .
miyo kahiwereiwa eretta yotikiniha .
miyo n amusi aka nahixanka .
ay aka yahirowa waxerya ehako , khuhimeriwa wira mam owo atteliwe ni majini .
vano ohiyu omosá kahiloha :
miyo kikhwiyene kithatiwa , kirowaniwaka ovithiwa , vavo yahikhala eruwa , vasulu vaya ahikhala mutthu amukunxe xahuko mmakhatani ni etoso emosa mmatatani mwawe .
owo ahikitthana akikohaka wira :
edini anyu t ivi ?
òhibatiziwa , mukristu walá mmaka ?
miyo kahimwakhula wira ka mukristu vano owo ahikivaha musurukh ule iraka :
mwàthame , mmirye musurukh ula ohintekeliw etthu .
kimiryakaru , kahivenya .
kahupuwela oloha iwe , kikupali ohiya sothene kiraka , kitthikela olompa .
varowalyaka okomunidadi , akristu yahikakhela sana , khukikhaliherya otthikela ephiro aka yakirimenle .
miyo nkinimova-tho jini hatá ephattu ahu , muluku okikumiha mwepotthani mwa satana , khukitthikiherya ekumi yohakalala .
kinnaxukhurela akristu akakhenle mukomunidadi .
masu a muluku
apwiya yahona wira vathi-va atthu yanvira etepaka otakhala murima , mupuwelo aya wothene n otthuna waya wari opaka .
vano muluku ahimuhimerya nowé wira :
miyo kihupuwela wamaliha atthu othene , okhala wira mwaha wa yawo elapo yothene yosareya owali .
vano miyo kinimwamaliha atthu vamosá n ilapo .
mpake ekalaw anyu yulupale ya mattoro ; muthikilanye ikatthi muhiná mmaré ni onyoma otá ni muhina .
miyo kinkela orupiha epula ya mutaseke , yeyo enrowa opwetexa vathi-va itthu sothene sikumi : sothene siri mulaponi-mu sinomala .
vano miyo kinimwatàna ni nyuwo , munrowa okela mukalawani nyuwo vamosa n àn inyu n amwar inyu n axar aya an inyu .
mukelihe mukalawani inama pili sa mixovo sothene , emosa yolopwana , ekina yothiyana , wira sikhale sikumi vamosa ni nyuwo .
mukuxe solya sinjene , musuke , wira mulyeke nyuwo n inama iyo sothene .
nowé khwiraka sothene sarummwawe ni muluku .
yahirupa epula yinjene mpakha mahiku miloko mixexé vohihiyererya .
mási yahinjerereya , yahittukhula ekalawa eyo , khukhala vasulu va masí itthu sothene sa mulaponi sarina ekumi sahikhwasa .
muluku ahimupuwela nowé n inama sothene sowali n iye sa vaté sarinawe mukalawani .
vano muluku ahirumiha epheyo mulaponi , màsi khwìkhalelaka .
vano nowé ahikumiha ekhuntta , wira yawehe màsi yawelenlene vathí .
vano ekhuntt eyo , ehonaka nipuro n okotela , yahihokolowela wa nowé mukalawani , okhala wira màsi nlelo yahikhunela elapo yothene ya vathí .
nowé ahòkolela mono , ahivara ekhuntta , khukeliha mukalawani .
ahiwehererya nlelo mahiku mathanu na manli , numalá , ahikumiha-tho ekhuntta .
ekhuntta yeyo yahihokolowa makáripi , eruhaka nikukhu nikithi n olivera , epampene ni munupi .
vano nowé ahisuwela wira mási yahiwelelasa mulaponi .
nowé ahikhuma vamosa n an awe n amwar awe n axara an awe inama sothene sowali n iye sothene sa vaté , ipalame n itthu sinipurula vathí , sothene sahikhuma mukalawani , muxovo ti muxovo .
muluku ahimuhimerya nowé vamosá n an awe , wira :
miyo kinimwatàna ni nyuwo n osulu anyu , n itthu sothene sikumi sirinanyu : ipalame n inama sa vaté n iye sowopiha sa mutakhwani , inama sothene sikhumme mukalawani .
kinimwatàna ni nyuwo : itthu sothene sikumi khasinihononiwatho ni epula ya mutaseke , nnákhala khinrupa-tho epula eyo ya mutaseke enihonona elapo .
ethonyeryo yo watàna waka ni nyuwo n itthu sothene sikumi sirinanyu , eri wa maloko othene a ohòlo , t ila :
kohela ekhweyi aka mmekuni ekhweyi yeyo enrowa okhala ethonyeryo yo watàna waka miyo n elapo .
okathi onkhunelaka elapo ni meku , enokhumelelaka ekhweyi mmekuni memmo . vano miyo kinimupuwela watàna waka wiralyaka miyo ni nyuwo n itthu sothene sikumi .
khinrowa-tho orupa epula ya mutaseke enrowa ohonona itthu sikumi .
murima wa katekese
muluku onniwopola atthu , awo animuroromela ni animwiwelela .
elapo enihononeya mulattu wa sotakhala siniraya atthu .
akina anniwiva akhw aya , anjene anniwiyerya , anniwototha , annapuherya .
khula nihiku atthu anniviwa okhottoni , aretta anjene annokhwa mulattu wohithokoreriwa ehinavahiwa murette worera ; anjene annokhwa mwaha w ohilyaka sana , ehimonaka mutthu òwakhaliherya .
sotakhala siniriwa n atthu othene sinlikana ni màsi èpula yulupale , yahononne elapo yothene .
vano muluku t omoriwa ikharari ni t òvilela , òpisa onanariwa , òrera murima ni òroromeleya , ontthuna wira atthu othene yopowe ni ehakalaleke , epuheke vohimala-tho .
muluku onninihanela ekumi ntoko samwihanalyawe nowé , wira nitteliweke murima nikhalaka apatthani awe .
muluku oninnopola namuroromelaru , nirakaru sinnirumawe , ntoko siralyawe nowé .
màsi a mutáseke nthonyeryo na màsi òbatiso annirapiha mwa itampi sothene ni annivaha ekumi ya muluku tith ihu .
ekalawa ya nowé nthonyeryo na ekereja , nloko n akristu .
ovekela
mwepiphini muryaka kinniwihanani , apwiya .
nto nyuwo munnilevelela itampi sahu , wira norumelekeni , nottittimihakani .
tthiri apwiya t omoriwa ikharari vanjene awo khunarikela owòpola atthu .
ovanela ni olehana
solimalela xeni sinàhapala atthu khiyakumiherya maxankiho malupale ?
evinyu , esuruma , oraruwa sikaro sinnakhaliherya atthu wunnuwa ni murettele ?
etalá , wùma wa miró , iretta saniphwanyá nnupuwela-ní ? ti muluku onnitthulamela ?
nowé àlimpe nani ?
àwova yale yamutheya , apaceryaka oteka ekalawa , muttetthe wahakhanle ephareya ?
hiyo nilipeke nani ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
mwaha wo wamini , nowé ahimwiwelela muluku , apakaka ekalawa , yeyo yamòponle owo n atthu ètthoko awe .
oreriwa wa mutthu khahiyó orapa eriya .
makhalelo ahu
muttetthe mmosá worekamelana ni mittetthe sikina , khiwarina eloja .
mutthu , arummwe ni guvernu , ahathukumanya atthu a muttetthe owo , khwahimerya wira :
amusi : niwanane , nitakanihe musurukhu , niteke eloj ahu .
atthu awo yahitteliwa murima ni molumo ala , khuruhasa musurukhu aya .
yahathanla atthu athanu wira yakheleleke musurukh uwo , eroweke opoma , yathume saphavelaya : makha , ikuwo , makhura n itthu sikina .
varowalyaya , tthiri yahiruha itthu iyo , khíyatumiha .
siso musurukhu wahinjerereya , nto wahipacerya wahapala atthu awo athanu .
ekwaha yanenli , yahipacerya othuma itthu saya ni musurukhu yole wa loja yotakanihiwa .
hatá sakaratari a muttetthe ole anikuxa ntoko ti sawawe .
musurukh ule wanivukuwa , okhala wira khula mutthu yàle yaholela , yanikuxerya emutakihaka sakaratari .
musurukh ule wa loja wahimala , wiwanana iwe wahihononeya , muttetthe owo khiyàkhanle-tho eloja .
masu a muluku
elapo yothene yarina elavulelo emosa ni molumo mamosaru . atthu ethamelaka ilapo s onikhuma nsuwa , yahiphwanya nipuro nowataleya , khukhalaka memmo .
numalá yahihimeryana wira : nrowé , nupé ixixolo , nipahe .
siso ipa saya khisatekiwa ni maluku n uloko , satekiwa n ixixolo ninnyomelo .
vano yahihimeryana-tho wira : nrowé nteke muttetthe ni empa yorakamexa : ethok aya ephiyé wirimu .
vano apwiya yahikhuruwa , wira yone muttetthe n imp ele yorakamexa yatekaya atthu awo .
apwiya khwira : atthu ala ari nloko nimosa , elavulelo aya eri emosaru , vano àpacerya muteko aya .
okhuma olelo sothene sintthunaya wira , awo khanojeya .
nrowé nikhuruwe , nivirikanyihe malavulelo aya , wira ehíwananeké-tho .
apwiya yahiòmola atthu ale , khwamwarexela mulaponi mothene , tivo , yahojela oteka muttetthe owo .
tivó-tho muttetthe owo wihaniwaya obabeli , okhala wira weiwo apwiya yahivirikanyiha elavulelo y atthu othene , khwamwarexela atthu mulaponi mothene .
murima wa katekese
wisona ni wikuxererya onninimwalanyiha .
muluku ahira : nimúpe mutthu onlattanahu , onlikana ni hiyo .
satana ahimuhimerya muthiyana wira : muluku onowotothani , mulyeke muhokorokho wokhottihenryaweni , munokhala ntoko maluku .
muluku ahimuhimerya nowé vamosá n an awe wira : miyo kinimwatàna ni nyuwo n osùlu anyu .
obabeli atthu yaniphavela oteka empa yorakamexa , ethok aya ephiyé wirimu , ekhale nloko nowerya ni novuwa .
muluku ahivirikanyiha elavulelo aya , khwamwarexela mulaponi mothene .
vano nikohaneke wira : muluku onlavula ekhweli walá ononiwoka ?
muluku onnilavula ekhweli : onniphavela vanjene wira nisiveliweke ntoko yowo , nikhale an awe a nloko nimosá .
ti satana , nwanan ihu , onniwoka anithonyeryaka ephiro yohiloka , ehimpixa wa muluku hatá ehininreriha .
mutthu arowaka mapuro ahinsuwelawe , onira-ní wira ahithwelelé ?
ole pahi onèmererya ni ontthara miruku sorera sinivahiwawe , onniphwanya ephiro y ekekhai ni onniphiya onkelawe .
masu a muluku , aniwiwa ni murima ni anttemuleliwa mbibliani , annithonyerya ephiro y ekekhai ennipixa wa muluku tith ihu , nikhalaka an awe n amusi mukina ni mukhw awe .
ti ephiro yatthanryawe abrahamu , ihaniwaka ni muluku , ntoko sinrowahu wiwa oholo .
ovekela
apwiya , murim aka khumphavela itthu sulupale nnákhala maitho aka khanisona .
nkiniphavela wisunnuwiha , nnákhala itthu sulupale sokivikana miyo .
vano kinnimàliha murim aka , kinnitthyaliha , ntoko mwanamwane ovonne mmutheteni mw ame awe .
ovanela ni olehana
niweryeke sai ovirikanyiha nsu na muluku ni masu òwisona ni òwikuxererya ?
mulupale a muttetthe ole n ale yatumiha muloja , nsu xeni yaiwelenlyaya ?
nìreke sai wira okhalé wiwanana wekekhai , khula mutthu avaneleke , avareke muteko n akhw awe , enamwi evirikanaka makhalelo ?
mwa hiyo onokhala opatthani wekekhai , nihiweryaka wattittimiha n uwakhela akhw ihu ?
mmatthokoni mwahu , nnowerya okhala òwiwanana n osiveliwa , muluku ahiri-vo ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
owiriyana masu a muluku ni wettela onninithukumanya omusi omosá .
ohilèleya , onnihàxa .
miyo kinrowa okhala muluku anyu .
siso sahimyaya anaisarayeli emuxukhurelaka muluku elapo yorera yavahalyawe ni emupuwelaka abrahamu muhakhalai aya alaiheriwe ni muluku elapo yeyo .
owo ari makampusi àkhanle vakhiviru va iyakha ikonto pili kristu ahinatthi .
khino elapo yo mesopotamia oyariwawe yakhumelenle maxakha ntoko otothowa elapo mwaha wa miro sasanrye tivó atthu yathamenlyaya ilapo sowuma .
abrahamu ni sara , amwar awe , yahivenyasa ekupaliki wira sokhumelela iyo sakhanyereriha okhuma , ari muluku mukumi awitthana alaiheryaka wira arowa wavaha osùlu munjene ni elapo yowunttelana .
awo yanimuroromela muluku yowo pahi .
ntoko awo isakhi ni rebeka , yakobe ni rakheli ni liya , yosefe n axinn awe , othene aya yakhala yettihiwaka ni omwamini muluku mukumi , owo akhala ni yawo ntoko mmusi , mpatthani òroromeleya ni ohanyanyala .
amakampusi awo khiyàmanke mmittettheni mwakhalaya mamwene òwerya ni athajiri yawiyerya atthu , yawotothaka yiraka : miyo ka muluku anyu .
abrahamu n an awe yahikupali omaka mmathalani walá mmiyakoni ekosopaka mihuwo saya n imatta saya , emuroromelaka natiri muluku ammanenlyawe .
ovekela
apwiya ! miyo kihophavelani ni murim aka wothene , murim aka onnunkheliwa ni masu anyu .
mukihapuxe ephiro yo wotha , mukisuwelihe otthuna wanyu .
ovanela ni olehana
molumo ala , ohiya elapo n amusi annihimerya exeni ?
olelo va omwamini muluku , wira sai ?
nìreke sai mahiku wira nikhale anamòna òwamini n uroro mela w abrahamu ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
abrahamu ti tithi àtthu animwamini muluku : anayuda , amaka , akristu .
wamini omwiwelela muluku mwa itthu sothene sinnihimeryawe .
muluku khanvanyiwa !
khapá onètta n emp awe !
makhalelo ahu
mwene mmosá ahikhala n axisulu awe . vano ahalaka okhwa , ahathukumanya , khwahimerya wira : mmatta-mu wovithiwa muhakhu munjene . mwahalaka , mphaveleke , munophwanya .
axisulu awe awo yahipacerya opwattha yixerihaka mpakha vathi yahipwattha ematt eyo yothene , khuhiphwany etthu .
vonalyaya wira khiyarere ovara muteko , yahihimeryana wira : nrowé , nàle mele n ikhutte nnakhuwo ni nxotte .
khwiraka siso .
vaphiyalyaya okathi w ohatta , yahisariha matath aya khuphwanya musurukhu munjene yahitumihalaya nxotte , nakhuwo ni solya sikina .
masu a muluku
apwiya yahimuhimerya abramu molohani wira : nyuwo abramu , muhové ! miyo kinimokhapelelani , otthuveliwa wanyu onrowa okhala wulupalexa .
apwiya muluku aka , munrowa okivaha exeni ?
khamukivanhe mwana vano mmosá àrumeyi aka t unrowa wakhela sohiyeriwa saka .
vano apwiya yahimuhimerya abramu wira : khahiyó owo onrowa okhala mukelamp anyu .
okathi yowo apwiya yahimukumiherya vaté abramu , khumuhimerya wira : nwehé osulú , mwalikele itheneri , mwaweryaka walikela .
siso sattalyaya itheneri , osúlu anyu onrowa watta siso .
abramu ahiwamini apwiya vano , mwaha wo wamini wawe , apwiya yahisiveliwa ni yowo , khumwakhelela .
yahimuhimerya-tho abramu wira : miyo k apwiya , ti miyo kokumihaleni elapo ya wuri , okhaldeya , wira kovaheni elapo ela , ekhalé yawinyu .
apwiya muluku aka , kintthuna osuwelexa sai wira kinrowa okhala mwanene elapo ela ?
apwiya khumuhimerya wira : mukiruhele mwanyompe òthiyana a iyakha ttharú , n ipuri ya iyakha ttharú , n ipwittipwitthi ya iyakha ttharú , ni nsiya nimosá ni ekhuntta nlelo muhoro .
abramu ahirowela inama iya sothene , ahithikilasa eriyari , khwiyathiki khula ekapatte awehanihaka n ikhw aya ; vano ipalame khathikinle .
vakenlyaya nsuwa , epiphi vakhunenlyaya elapo , nahikhumelela nìkho natthuwa mwixi ni moro wavarela , khuvira eriyari ya ikapatte iye sa inama .
nihiku nenlo apwiya yahatàna n abramu , khumuhimerya wira : kinimwavaha elapo ela an inyu n osulu anyu .
vano khamunrowa-tho wihaniwaka abramu , okhuma olelo munimwihaniwaka abrahamu , okhala wira miyo kinrowa wokhalihani tithi a maloko manjene .
murima wa katekese
abrahamu ahimwamini muluku ammanenle natiri wira arowa okhala tithi a nloko nulupale .
abramu à huluvala .
nto amuroromelaka muluku amwihana , khojenle othama elapo awe ni wahiya amusi awe , arowaka elapo yalaiheriwawe ni muluku .
ahihiya elapo awe ahisuwelaka warowawe .
amwamini ni amuroromela muluku pahi. amulaihenrye wira arowa okhalana elapo awe n osulu munjene , anamwi owo vamosá n amwar awe yahàwerya oyara .
elapo n osulu , muluku yamuhimenryawe abramu onvaha , ti nthonyeryo n omphenta ni watàna wawe n abramu , mpatthani awe .
siso wira amupuweleke natiri awe , muluku ahinvaha nsina n abrahamu .
vaphiyalyawe mulaponi yahimeriwawe ni muluku , abrahamu ahikhala ntoko namurwa .
mwar awe , sara , ahimuyarela mwana mmosá pahi , isakhi .
nto abrahamu anamini wira sovaha sa muluku sanivikana sorera sakhenlyawe vathí-va .
osulu w ekekhai w abrahamu t àle anamini , t àle aniwehererya muttetthe ohinweriwa opwetexiwa , yowo wupuweliwe n utekiwe ni muluku .
ovekela
miyo kinnaroromela apwiya , kinnalipelela ni murim aka wothene : eroho aka enniroromela sinihimyaya .
murim aka onnalipelela apwiya onvikana mutthu onlipelela oxa .
ovanela ni olehana
mutthu onimwamini ni onimuroromela muluku , onira-ní ?
ninnamini wira muluku oniphavela onireriha ntoko simurerihaiyawe abrahamu ?
ninroromela wakhela sorera sa vathí pahi walá ninnitteliwa murima mana muluku onnivaha sorera sihinòneya sinivikana iya sa vathí-va ?
elapo xeni n itthu xeni muluku onkivekelawe wira kihiyé , kimutthareke yowo ni makhalelo masyá ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
wamini vinamuna y okhalana itthu sinlipelelahu , ni t osuwelexa wira sokhala itthu sihinònahu .
yovahale muluku , khunkhwa ohiphwannye !
makhalelo ahu
niwiriyane onamòna wa sipriano .
sipriano oyariwe onapano , mwana a pariti ni ànifa , oleliwé n anakhe awe alima guarda .
àkhala ni àsoma omissau w omweriya , nakala a velha , eyakha ya 1956 .
obatisiwe nihiku 21 / 9 / 58 . khwathela amwar awe paula nansema nihiku 1 / 1 / 67 , khwayara àna athanu .
sipriano ohettiha obatizo awe ni makhalelo òrera , n ukathi wothene òkhalela onamòna votthuna wawe omwamini yesu kristu mpakha okhwa .
ari mutthu asuwela olevelela ni murim awe wothene , tivó imara sinjene amusi awe khiyàsiveliwa .
vathanliwawe animadore a zona , ahivara muteko n ikuru sawe sothene n utthuna wawe wothene , okathi wòvilaxa .
eyakha ya 1982 mwaha w etala yavonle mmuttettheni mwawe. ahithamela omatalane .
weiwo ahithukumanya nikhuru nimosa n akristu , siso khutthukula ekomunidade , yeyo yathanleliwawe okhala ansiau .
nihiku na 29 / 8 / 84 , ekhotto yahiphiya omatalane .
anakhotto awo erwaka mphironi yahinvara mulopwana mmosa , wira à thonyerye w asakaratari .
