yesu anakhaliherya atthu othene wamini wira muluku , tithi a ikharari , onnisuwela ohawa w an awe othene ni onkhala ni yawo . muluku , khavo ommurihelawe osalani .
makhalelo ahu
etthoko emosá y akristu yahayara an aya anli , khwabatiziha . othene aya yanetta okapela . ekelelaka oholo , amam aya yahivariwa ni jini. khwineliwa ni khupakeliwa exilompiwa . tivó mam owo vahiyalyawe wetta okapela , khuhala yettaka amwann awe n an awe .
ehapari yorera
yesu n awixutti awe ahiphiya okafarnawu , nihiku n asabadu ahikela mpani mothukumana , yihaniwa sinagoga , aniwixuttiha atthu , othene wanatikiniha mwixuttiho awe , mana axuttiha ntoko mwanene , khahiyó ntoko awixuttihi a ikano .
vano , ahikhala-mo mulopwana avariwe ni nlaikha nonanara . nlaikha nlo nonanara nahikhuwela , nìraka : yesu munazarethi , murina-ni nyuwo ni hiyo ? murwenle onipwetexa ? miyo kinnosuwelani : nyuwo mwá mwana a muluku .
yesu ahiruma nlaikha nlo nonanara n ikuru , ìraka : omàle wé , omuhiye mutth uwo .
vano nlaikha nlo nonanara nahimuthukumeliha mulopwan owo n ikuru , nahikhuwela vanjene , khumuhiya .
atthu othene yahitikinihiwa vanjene , khukohanasa , yiraka : exen ila ? ola mwixuttiho wa nanano , onlriwa n uwerya wa mwanene ! owo onniruma hatá malaikha , khlyamwiwelela .
nananoru ovuwa wawe wahimwarela mapuro othene èlapo y ogalileya .
murima wa katekese
yesu khanova ni onninikumiha mwepotthani , anakiheryaka owerya wa sotakhala .
yesu ahikela mpani mothukumana , khupacerya wixuttiha : khula ettiminku vanthukumanahu okereja , ti yesu yowo onnixuttiha-tho wira othene n axinna . muluku tith ihu , onniniphenta. onkhala ni hiyo .
yesu axuttiha ntoko mwanene , khahiyó ntoko awixuttihi a ikano : awixuttihi awo yanihimya ni yanitaphulela ikano sa moise . yesu anivanyiha ni aninjererya ikano iyo àhimeryaka atthu wira : muhiwa ele ehimmwe wira : mumphenteke mukhw inyu , mmunyokheke nwanan inyu . nto miyo kinol èlani wira : mwaphenteke awanan inyu . mwavekeleleke ale anolupatthani . siso munokhala ana àtith inyu ari wirimu .
okhala wira muluku mwanene ahimulavuliha moise , yesu awerya sai ovanyiha ikano seiyo ni wunjererya ?
ovekela
apwiya !
mwixuttiho anyu ti wosiva mwano mwaka , ovikana yolya yosivexa walá oravo !
atakhali àkithipela nlitti : masi miyo nkihapunwe iphiro sanyu .
soruma sanyu ti muhakhu aka wa mahiku othene : seiyo sinnikitteliha murima .
ovanela ni olehana
itthu sonanara siri mmurimani mwahu pì sivi ?
sinkhala sai mirima s akristu ale ahiniwanana n akhw aya ni ahiniwiriyana masu mahiku àttiminku ?
nikhalaka òkawanyeya n uwanawana ninnamini oniphenta wawe muluku ?
nlaikha nonanara nanimusuwela yesu tivó vamutthyawalyaya . hiyo nimphavela omusuwela yesu wira nireke xeni ?
yorera xeni enirahu enòniherya wira nnimutthara yesu ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
yesu ti nsu noweryexa na muluku , ninnikhaliha ana a muluku ni ninnakiherya ikuru sa satana .
nsuwa n òpaka , mweri khunàrya !
makhalelo ahu
asira anova vanjene orowa ottaiwene , ame awe ehikhanle , masi khumwiwelela patiri , amuhimenrye wira arowa ovona .
vaviralyaya isumana pili , medik owo ahihokolowela okarapira amuruhaka asira avonnene . vakhuruwalyawe mukaroni , ahirowa wa patiri . vamphwanyalyawe , ahitaphula nifutta nawe. ahikumiha enika emosa ni mukatthe , khumeya , khunvaha patiri vomuxukhuru mana ahivona .
ehapari yorera
vano yesu ahiwakhula wira : nrowé okinaku , mittetthe sowattamela , wira weiwo-tho kalaleye ehapari yorera p itthu kirwenlyaka yeyo .
khwettetta elapo yothene y ogalileya , alaleyaka mpani mothukumana , òmolaka malaikha ònanara .
murima wa katekese
yesu onvenle ovoniha , wòpola , ni onivaha ikuru s oxinttana iretta .
khatthuniherya malaikh awo olavula : xeni yesu akhottiheryaka malaikha ònanara olavula ? mukhulukana onnisiveliwa wira muteko awe olaleiwe vosuweliwa . nto yesu khatthunne osuweliwa okhala mukhulukana mulupale , àtthunne , khakhottiherya malaikh awo olavula . yesu ahavoniha aretta wira òniherye wamorela wawe muluku ikharari atthu othene anihawa . yesu omphavela wira hiyo nimalamalihe ohawa wothene . ephiro enihiyenryawe ti mwettelo awe ni molumo awe .
ovekela
apwiya yesu nyuwo mwawirenle atthu sorera , mwanavoniha aretta , nvahe ekumi erutthu ahu , nvahe-tho ikuru eroho ahu , wira nawereiwaka nivoneke .
ovanela ni olehana
nakhaliheriwaka ninnisuwela oxukhuru ? apiyamwan awo n asira yinre-ni ?
namalá olompa okapela ettiminku , owani nnira exení ? yesu numalá olompa , ìrale-ní ?
yesu vamanlyawe olompa mpani mothukumana ahirowa wavoniha aretta . hiyo namala owiriyana masu a muluku , nnoniherya sai molumo yiwalyahu ?
ehapari xeni yorera yesu alaleyawe àvonihaka aretta ?
yesu aphwanya vai ikuru s olaleya ehapari yorera ?
makhalelo ahu
hassani mwaná òrera orina iyakha pili . ame awe nattottó . atithi awe khansuweliwa . nihiku nimosa ame awe yahithipa nlitti , yahimuhwela , khuhiya murú pahi otá . mutthu mmosa ahimuttemulela , ahimukuxa , khunvahererya irima oxipiritali .
irima vamulonlyawe , ahavekela akristu wira etthoko emosa emuliuweke mwanamwane ole . animadore a parókia ahimurowana owannyawe . vano okhala wira kharerena anamwane . hassani ahipacerya ohawa . etthoko ekina nlelo yaharina mwana. yahivahererya omukhapelela , siso hassani ohaphwanya amama n apapa animuhuwa n umphenta valupale ntoko mwan aya òmuyara .
ehapari yorera
yesu ahiruheliwa anamwane wira akwannye . vano awixutti awe yahapwapwela atthu yàruha anamwane ale . yesu , ònaka etthu ila , ahinanariwa n awixutti awe , khwahimerya wira : mwahiye anamwane ekirwele miyo . muhakhottiheryé , mana omwene wa muluku ti wawaya ale ari ntoko axinamwane ala . kinolèlani ekhweli wira : ole ohinakhelela omwene wa muluku ntoko mwanamwane , khanwerya okela momweneni memmo . numalá , ahakuxa anamwane ale mmatatani , khwareriha , awixatheryaka matata .
murima wa katekese
yesu onnixuttiha wattittimiha anamwane ni owakhela vatthokoni , munlokoni mw akristu ni mulaponi .
okathi wa yesu anamwane khiyòneliwa vatthu. khiyahiyó atthu khiyàkhapeleliwa walá khiyàpuha mirerelo s atthu . anamwane yàri a tithi mutthu. ntoko athiyana sakhalaya a mwann ava n ipottha sakhalaya sa mwanene . mwanamwane amwirela yotakhala mutthu , tithi awe t aliva . ikwasuni n athiyana anamukhweli yanihawa vanjene mwaha wohikhalana òwakiha .
makhulupale khiyàtthuniherya anamwane othwela vakhiviru vaya .
yesu òrukunuxa makhalelo ala othanyiwa anamwane . yesu ahakhuparela anamwane , khwareriha , ni òhimya-tho wira : omwene wa muluku ti wawaya ale ari ntoko axinamwane ala .
okhuma erupaliwakaru , anamwane ankhala vekekhai atthu , ana a muluku , aihaneliwa ekumi yohimala . muluku ori tithi aya òrera murima ni musuweli , onnakhapelela othene ovikana siniraya axitithi aya ayanre . murerelo w anamwane ti okhala atthu a muluku onaphenta , awo annakhela mahala sovaha sothene mwa yowo .
yesu onnalattula atthu othene wattittimiha ni wakhapelela anamwane ntoko satthunaya omwakhela yesu yowo , mòpoli aya . onnalattula-tho atthu othene omuroromela muluku ntoko anamwane sinaroromelaya aximam aya ni wihiya yettihiwaka ni yowo .
otakhala murima w atthu alupale omphavela ophwanya sothene n ikuru saya , emuhiyaka muluku , ntoko siralyawe adamu . yesu òhimya wira : khavo oniwerya wona omwene wa muluku , ahivariwe-tho vasyá .
molumwenkuni-mu sinnikhuma ikhotto , mana khula mutthu omphavela ophwanya itthu sothene n ikuru sawe ni waruma akhw awe .
omwene wa muluku ti wawaya ale anàkhela sothene wa muluku tithi , ntoko axinamwane . tivó vansuwelaya okawana n atthu othene mana t axinn aya .
ovekela
apwiya muluku aka , vayariwaka , ti nyuwo mukikelinhe molumwenkuni-mu ti nyuwo mukipwehale mmatatani mw ame aka , wira kisukiwe .
vayariwaka , ti nyuwo muyareliwe : okhuma oyariwa wene , nyuwo mwá muluku aka .
ovanela ni olehana
yesu ònixuttiha walompa atithi ari wirimu . ninnalompa atithi awo nitteliwaka murima naroromelaka ntoko sinirawe mwanamwane mmatatani mw ame awe ?
ninnamini wira ekumi ahu yothene nimphwanya wa muluku tithi onnisuka ?
nnimukhotta sai satana onnererya wira nihimuroromeleke muluku , nalokihaka makhalelo èkumi ahu ?
ninnasuwela anamwane òhawa ntoko hassani ? nireke exem n anamwane siso ?
nnàlela sai anamwane ? vatthokoni omusuka mwana mwankhani , muteko w apapa n amama. walá ti w amama pahi ? nàlela niwopopihaka ni nahukhumuku pahi ? yesu atthuna wira-ní ?
niwakhelela sai anamwane vanlokoni v akristu ? ninninvahererya muluku mwana oyariwa nanano ntoko siryava mmalompekmi ?
epajervaka winnuwa an ihu annilompa vamosá ni hiyo , walá ankhala otá erukuneyaka pahi ?
hiyo n àlupale , sihavo sorera sinnixuttihaya anamwane ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
khula mwana ti ovaha wa muluku okhuma erukulu ene . ekumi yothene y atthu ti yorerihiwa ni muluku .
anamwane muthoté !
makhalelo ahu
mutthu ahàkhanle namakuttula , khaphiya iwo . patiri pahi t aphiya wira aheleleke mukuttho w okaristiya . patiri damião ahiwonela othunku anamakuttula awo , khwivahererya okhala weiwo vamosá n awo . siso analipiha murima evaraka muteko w oteka ipa saya n ulima imatta saya n omuteka alumasiya wira esukeke mo solya savahiwaya n atthu yawonela othunku .
patiri damião analalèrya atthu awo òhawa ehapari yorera ya yesu , wira emusuweleke mòpoli aya . vakhanlyawe iyakha ixexe n awo , patiri damião ahirava makuttul awo .
anari namakuttula siso , ahakhaliherya anamakuttula akhw awe n utteliwa wawe murima , mana anamini wira muluku animphenta ni ononvaha opuha wohimala wirimu .
numalá iyakha muloko ni pili , awereiwaka makuttula , patiri damião ahikhwa mmatatani mw apatthani awe , yawo akhalihenryawe .
ehapari yorera
mulopwana mmosá namakuttula ahimwattamela yesu , ahikokhora oholo wawe , khunvekela , ìraka : mwatthuná vale , munowerya okireriha !
yesu , ahimmorela ikharari , ahòkola ntata , amwixatherya , khumwirela : kinnitthuna , vonani .
nananoru makuttul ale yahirimelela , mulopwan owo ahivona .
vano yesu ahimulavuliha n ikuru , khumulaiha , iraka : mwipasope : muhimulèlé mutthu etthu ila . nto murowé mwaisoniherye wa namukuttho : nvelele yovaha , mwaha w orerihiwa wanyu , ntoko sirumalyawe moise ; eyo yakhalele atthu onamona .
vano-nto mulopwan owo , avenyakaru vale , ahipacerya olaleya n uvuwiha ehal ila . tivó , yesu khawerya-tho okela omittettheni òniwaka : àkhala mapuro yahaviriwa . vano , atthu a mipantte sothene yanrowa wa yowo .
murima wa katekese
yesu onniwakhelela òwomoliwa ni onnakeliha-tho munlokoni mw atthu .
okathi wa yesu , namakuttula anihawa : anirummwa wira awareke sothala , ahivaseké ikharari sawe , aikhuneleke mpakha mwererum khiyakhuwela iraka : ka namwikhol ka namakuttula ! . siso atthu akumi khiyàmwattamela mana othene yanova orava erett eyo . namakuttula ahàna okhala mekhawe otá wa muttetthe .
yesu khonve orava makuttula , nto ahim òkolela ntata namakuttula , amwattamenle aminiki wira anwerya omureriha .
tthiri yesu ahinvoniha wira amutthikiherye munlokoni mw atthu akumi .
yesu ahimuruma owo avonihiwe , wira amuxukhuru muluku , avelelaka yovaha . yesu khatthunne ovuwihiwa mwaha w etthu ile yiralyawe .
etthu yesu yamwirenlyawe namakuttula ennithonyerya omusi wananano yesu onrwawe opacerya . omusi owo khontthuna womoliwa mutthu ni okhottiwa , nnákhala mwaha w eretta hatá solimalela walá ikano s ephattu .
ovekela
mulaleye ni miyo ovuwa wa muluku : ninnuwihe nsina nawe othene vamosá .
kahaphavela apwiya , awo àkiwelela , àkakiherya sowopiha sothene .
ovanela ni olehana
khalai mulaponi mu , yakhalihiwa sai anamakuttula ?
nabatiziwaka ninnikela omusi musyá wa yesu . nolikanana ohimuthanya-tho mutthu ?
atthu xeni olelo va ahinoneliwa vatthu ntoko khaiai sahoneli waya vatthu anamakuttula ?
nireke sai wira ehikhumelele-tho atthu akina ahinoneliwa vatthu mulaponi mwahu ? .
ti pani onnivaha ikuru s othukumana ni sophentana , nihimuthanyaka mutthu ?
mwa solimalela s ephattu sokhala mikho sinakhottiherya atthu akina owattamela akhw aya ? nireke exeni wira atthu othene eweryeke onattamela ehinòvaka ?
vano sokhala miretle sinvoniha makuttula . ninnasuwela anamakuttula ? nnira-ni wira othene eloliweke ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
ekomunidade y akristu ti nloko ohikhanle-vo mutthu onthanyiwa nnákhala onathanya akhw awe .
muluku , khavo mutthu ommurihelawe osalani !
makhalelo ahu
muthiyana mmosá òrupala , wahiphiya okathi w oyara . yahivira mahiku manli ahawaka vanjene . mwann awe ahahimerya amusi amwar awe wira , vanrerela amwar ak ala warowana oxipiritali . amusi awo yahimuruma mulopwan owo orowa ophavela ekaro , masi uwo ahakhula iraka : arett ala nakuxe vakhittanttani . àtepa owereiwa . amusi awo khiyàtthunn etthu .
vano mwann awe owo ahavekela akristu akhw awe wira emukhaliherye warowana amwar awe oxipiritali . awo yahimutthunela mana yari akristu òwamini .
arett awo , vapixiwaya oxipiritali. yahiloliwa nananoru , khumuyara mwan aya . owanli aya khukhalasa akumi : mama ni mwana .
amusi yahira : mmus ih ula àri owani , khàvona , amunikhwela . ahikhala oxipiritali mahiku vakhani. khutthikela owani , amusi othene ettelasiwene murima .
ehapari yorera
vaviralyaya mahiku vakhani yesu ahihokolowela okafarnawu , khusuweliwa wira ori owani . siso , yahithukumana weiwo atthu anjene , mpakha ohinaphwanyaneya opuro nnákhala va mukhora .
yesu analalèrya atthu awo masu a muluku . vano yahiphiya akina emuruhelaka mulopwana òrakala , athatiwe n atthu axexe . nto khiyàwerya ompixa varyawe yesu , mwaha w atthu yaharere . tivó , yahivenula nipatho voluluwana ni yesu , yahimwarya etarato , khukuruxa vavale nrepa nataleliwawe orakal owo .
yesu , vonalyawe waminixa waya , ahimuhimerya òrakala yowo wira , mwan aka , itampi sanyu soleveleliwa .
vano yakhala-vo awixuttihi akina a ikano ekilanthene vavo . awo yanupuwela mmurimani mwaya wira : mutth ula onlavulela-ni siso ? ola onninveha muluku ! tani onwerya olevelela itampi , ahikhanle muluku pahi ! .
nananoru mulopwan owo ahemela , ahittukhula nrepa nawe , khurowa , atthu othene emonaka . othene yahitikinihiwa , enanvuwiha muluku yiraka : khantonko wona etthu sisa !
murima wa katekese
yesu òkhalana owerya w olevelela itampi . ola onninveha muluku ! mutthu ànvehá muluku , eyo t iyo , mutthu àhimyá wira muluku t òtakhala walá ahihimye owerya wa muluku , ahana wiviwa . yesu anisuwela ekano ela . tthiri , vaholo vaya , onrowa wiviwa mwahá wo wipaka mwana a muluku ni mwaha w ovara miteko sa muluku .
hatá vakhalaka siso , yesu ahimuhimerya òrakal owo wira : itampi sanyu soleveleliwa ! atthuna omuhimerya wira : muluku khanohukhumuni , owo ti mpatthan inyu .
okathi wa yesu , atthu yantthokelela wira eretta yari ehukhumu muluku anvahawe mutthu mwaha wa itampi siralyawe . yesu òtthuna owoniherya atthu wira eyo khahiyó ekekhai , hatá awixuttihi a ikano etthunaka omwiva mwaha w olavula siso .
awixuttihi a ikano yaniwixuttiha atthu ikano sa moise , yaniphuka milattu , khíyahimerya atthu itthu sirummwe n iye sikhottihiwe n ikano .
awixuttihi awo a ikano yanamini wira muluku òkhalana othunku ni onnilevelela itampi. masi àlevelelaka anaxariya pahi , yawo yira sorera , yahela mikuttho , yavaha musurukhu mpani mwa muluku . mutthu òrakala ahawerya wir etthu , aleveleliwa sai ?
yesu anvonihaka orakal owo , apajenryawe omulevelela , onnithonyerya wira muluku t òsareya othunku ni onnalevelela atthu , mana
owo t òrera murima , khahiyó mwaha wa sorera siniraya atthu . tthiri yesu akhomeliwaka vamwikimanyo , mwaha wo wihimya okhala mwana a muluku , ohàlevelela hatá ale yamwivale .
ovekela
apwiya !
mwathokoreryá sottheka sahu , ti pani onalipé oholo wanyu ?
masi nyuwo munnilevelela itampi sahu , wira norumelekeni , nottittimihekeni .
ovanela ni olehana
atthu axexe yahimuthata mulopwana òrakala , khumuroihela yesu . hiyo nnira-ní mmus ihu walá mutthu mukina àwereyaxiwa ? nnupuwela-ní mwaha w akristu ale yàrowanne amwar awe mukhw aya oxipiritali ?
ahinatthi onvoniha orakal owo , yesu ahinvaha ororomela n utteliwa murima amulevelelaka itampi sawe . tthiri aretta ari ni murettele , mana annatàna ni muluku n atthu , anniwerya ovona vowakuveya wavikana ale anòva ?
ti pani onwerya onimwalanyiha n uphenta wa kristu ?
awixuttihi a ikano yantthokelela wira eretta ti ehukhumu ya muluku . atthu akina ehinatthi orowa oxipiritali , anrowa ohakoni ephavelaka osuwela wira eretta ti ya minepa , ti yoloiwa walá ti ya muluku . khino atthu awo khanúpuwela ntoko awixuttihi awo a ikano ? yesu onnihimerya-ni ni ehapari yorera yiwalyahu ?
yesu ahilaleya ikharari muluku sinamorelawe atthu othene . hiyo ninlaleya ikharari seiyo walá ihukhumu ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
mukristu t ule onarowana apatthani awe wa yesu , wira esuweleke ophenta wawe ni ephwanyeke ekumi mwa yowo .
murima wotteliwa murettele w erutthu : murima woripiwa wumiha makhuva !
yesu oniwakhelela anatampi
yesu , vakhumalyawe onazarethi , ahirowa okhala okafamawu vamosá ni maria , ante awe . animwakhela mutthu ti mutthu : atothi a ihopa , afarísi , alipa-dliviha mpósito , amasikhini n aretta , anilya vamosá n awo . anirowa-tho olya owanny aya ale yamulattula .
anaisarayeli , elyaka vamosá , yanoniherya opatthani mulupale , yanikhalihana amusi .
mwettelo wa yesu wanivirikana ni mwettelo walimalenlyaya atthu othene . owo akhala ntoko namurwa . tthiri asamariya , yahatthuniwa n ayuda , yari apatthani awe ni yesu anattottopela .
yesu àrerelaka murima anatampi , anakupaliha wira sottheka saya soleveleliwa . anatampi , atthu òhawa ni òpuheriwa yanitteliwa murima vanjene yiwaka wira muluku onnalevelela hatá ale ahimphwanela . yesu àvonihaka aretta ni àlevelelaka anatampi , anikumiha mmurimani mwaya wova wothene warinaya . wari ntoko oyáriwa-tho vasyá .
nto makhalelo awo masyá ni wamini n uphenta wananano , wanivirikana n ikano s ephattu sattharaya anaisarayeli ni mikho sovava orava . tivó ale yakupalexa otthara ikano s amuhakhalai aya ni solimalela saya , yahipacerya okhala awanani a yesu .
makhalelo ahu
iyakha sivinre alupale a mulaponi , yahipacerya ohimyasa wira muluku khavo . akristu yansuwela wira alupale awo khiyàsiveliwa n edini , masi yanikhalela nthiti walalèrya atthu ehapari yorera n ulompa .
akristu akina ekhumaka elapo aya ni eviraka nipuro nakhuliwa epanja , yahimphwanya mukhulupale mmosá aharere olavula n ikuru wira : muluku khavo . vano awo yahimwirela mukhulupale owo wira : ohiy ula ninrwa omaka owannyu .
tthiri ohiyu ole akristu yahirowa omaka owannyawe mukhulupale owo . khulyasa vamosá n atthu ale yahakhanle akristu . vano makhulupale makina yahakoha akristu yiraka : nyuwo munnihimya wira etampi etthu yotakhala vamaithoni va muluku . mmakenle-ni owannyawe natampi onihimya wira muluku khavo ?
akristu yahiwakhulasa wira : mulupal ihu yesu , arwaka vathi-va àrwenle atthu othene hatá ale ahinimwamini .
ehapari yorera
yesu ahivenya-vo arowaka-tho ophareya . vano mittitthi s atthu sanimuthukumanela , nave owo aniwixuttiha . aviraka , ahimona levi , mwan awe alfeyo , akilanthene valiviwa mpósito , khumwirela :
mukitthareke .
yesu , vawiwalyawe , ahiwakhula wira :
khahiyó atthu akumi aniphaveleliwa mukhulukana : aretta t aniphaveleliwa . vano miyo nkirwenle owihana atthu òrera murima : kirwenle owihana alipa-òttheka .
murima wa katekese
yesu onnimwitthana khula mutthu ni makhalelo awe wira amutthareke .
okathi yesu walaleyawe ehapari yorera , tiberio ari mwené mulupale òroma . mamwene òroma n ikuru s anakhotto aya yahikuxa omwene wa ilapo sinjene . khula elapo yahimuhiya okhala mwené èlapo eyo . ogalileya ari herodi , masi owo n atthu awe yahana oliva mpósito wa mwené mulupale òroma .
alipa-òliviha mpósito yari atthu ògalileya , yoliha opuro woliviha mpósito , envahaka mwené mulupale òroma musurukhu warumawe , mukinaku wanjererihaya , yanihalana . yohani mbatiza ahahimerya awo wira : muhiliviheke ovikana sirummwanyu atthu anjene khiyàsuwela mpósito mwené mulupale warumawe , tivó alipa-òliviha vaweryaya owototha atthu .
alipa a mpósito yaninyokhiwa vanjene n atthu alsarayeli , yànyiherya okhala anawíye n apatthani aroma yàpuherya .
vano ti mmosá w atthu awo yanyokhiwa . yesu amwihannawe , amwirelaka : mukitthareke . levi uwo òvariwa murima n othunku wamonenlyawe yesu , khumuttharaka ahiyaka muteko wa mpósito .
yesu ahirowa-tho olya owannyawe levi vamosá n alipa-òliviha mpósito , apatthani a levi owo .
katekese ovinre , nihiwa wira awixuttihi a ikano yanimwapa yesu mulattu w omulevelela mutthu òrakala itampi sawe . tivó yanimwapa yesu , yupuwelaka wira mutthu a muluku ahana omwalana n anatampi .
molumo àkhunlyawe yesu t òwiwanyeya : aretta t aniphaveleliwa mukhulukana . yesu àrwenle alipa-òttheka mana awo t aniphaveleliwa mòpoli aya . hiyo othene n anatampi , ale anisona okhala àxariya , khanòpoliwa . ale anihimya itampi saya vamaithoni va muluku , anrukunuxa murima , t anopoliwa .
ovekela
apwiya ,
nyuwo motokosa murim aka , mokisuwela , mukhalaka ottaiwene , mosuwela mupuwelo aka ; kakilathi walá kemelaka , nyuwo mosuwela .
kettaka walá karupathiki , nyuwo munnikona , munnikiholela iphiro saka sothene .
ovanela ni olehana
alipa a mpósito yananyiheriwa okhala anatampi . ninniwerya hiyo wavalanya atthu àxariya n anatampi ?
itampi sinkhuma mmitekoni walá mmurimani mwa mutthu ?
mukomunidadeni mwahu ahavo akristu anvara miteko sa guvernu , muxikhola , muxipiritali , oloja n ukompanyia ? annivara muteko n ixariya ? ninniwovelela wapwapwela yahiyaka otthara ehapari yorera ?
mamwene a khalai yanaruma atthu aya oliva mpósito , siso maguvernu a vano . ninnisuwela enlivelahu ni miteko xeni sinvareliwaya ?
maguvernu ahana ovara miteko yavarelaka atthu èlapo aya , ntoko opaka musurukhu , oteka ixikhola , ixipiritali , otthukula ni olokiha iphiro , wakhapelela atthu ni owakiherya mwa sotakhala sinahaxa . ti sinnirelaya ale anettiha elapo ahu ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
ekereja ti nloko n amusi animutthara yesu ephavelaka exariya ni murerelo wyatthu othene .
onipulela t ule onwereiwa !
makhalelo ahu
ahikhala mukristu mmosá aronwe wa mpatthani awe owurya evinyu . ahapaliwene ahivenya orowa owani , masi khimorela mphironi , khurupaka . vano , yahivira apatthani yarinawe , khumuhiya .
ehapari yorera
mwixuttihi mmosá a ikano aphavelaka onvelaveliha yesu , ahemela , khumukoha wira : mwixuttihi , kireke-ni wira kiphwanyé ekumi yohimala ?
yesu ahimukoha wira : mulivuruni mwa ikano mulempweni-mo ? nyuwo munsoma-mo sai ?
owo ahakhula ìraka : mwaphenteke apwiya , muluku anyu , ni murim anyu wothene n iroho anyu yothene n ikuru sanyu sothene n usuwela wanyu wothene ni mumphenteke mukhw inyu ntoko sinìphentanyu .
yesu ahimwirela : muhakhula orattene . mwireke siso , munophwanya ekumi .
vano mwixuttihi uwo a ikano , aphavelaka othonyerya wira okoha wawe wari woloka , ahimukoha-tho yesu , ìraka : masi , mukhw aka ti pani ?
vano yesu khukoha wira : w atthu ale araru , ti pani ommonanyu okhala mukhw awe ole akumanne n alavilavi ?
mwixuttihi a ikano ahakhula wira : t ule ammorenle ikharari .
yesu ahimuhimerya wira : muroweke , ni nyuwo mwireke siso .
murima wa katekese
ole ommonela othunku onvelavela , ti mukhw awe .
nipaceryaka mithukumano sa katekese , nahihimya wira nokawanyeya mwahá wa mahimo . khasinthowa itthu sinakawanyiha atthu : nikhuli n erutthu , malavulelo , edini , musurukhu n itthu sikina .
nahihimya-tho wira muluku khansiveliwa ni makhalelo àtthu ankawanyeya ethanyanaka , tivó vamurummyawe mwan awe yesu kristu . vekekhai , kristu yowo ti murettele ahu . yowo òlupanyiha maloko manli , khukhaliha omusi omosaru . yowo , ahimoroxa exiri yamwalanyiha maloko ale , yari onyokhana .
vano ni mithukumano iya sokiserya , nihiwa ehapari yorera , nihòna wira tthiri yesu ophavenle omalamaliha okawanyeya n uthanyana w atthu . yesu òwoniherya atthu wira muluku ori vamosá n aretta , n anamakuttula , onniwonela othunku anatampi , hatá ale avariwe ni satana , tivó khavo omphwanela othanyiwa .
ni nlikanyiho nla na musamariya òrera minima , yesu onnihimerya wira nihana okhaliheryana mukina ni mukhw awe moxankani mothene hatá nakhalanaka idini n iphattu sovirikana .
asamariya n ayuda khiyàtthunana . musamariya , yesu onimuhimyawe ni nlikanyiho , ahimmorela ikharari muyuda , khumukhapelela vanjene hatá asuwelaka wira ayuda othene yanathanya asamariya . tthiri uwo òxintta winana n unyokhana , khumphenta mukhw awe , khumukhapelela ntoko mmusi awe , ahonaka nikhuli nawe walá mukhalelo awe .
ti musamariya inre entthunawe muluku , tithi àtthu othene . namukuttho ni mulevi yanirowa olompa mpani mwa muluku oyerusalemu , masi khiyàmwiweienle muluku tithi , yowo onaruma atthu wira : mumphenteke mukhw inyu ntoko siniphentanyu .
nipuro nnihawawe mutthu , vavo t uri muluku onnihana wira noniherye omphenta wahu mukhw ihu ni wamini wahu .
ovekela
tith ihu ! otthuna wanyu wireye ntoko wirimu siso vathi-va .
ovanela ni olehana
khula nihiku ninlompa wira : otthuna wanyu wireye ninsuwela sai otthuna wa muluku , nimusomaka katekese pahi , walá naphavelaka atthu òhawa , nnakhaliheryaka ?
mulaponi mu , ninnikawaneya mwaha w edini . nireke exeni wira nivukulihe okawanyeya iwo ? ninnirowa olavula ni ovanela n akristu ahikhanle akatòlika , n atthu èdini y ephattu , n asilamu , wira niwoniherye itthu sinwerya onatàniha ?
ahavo-tho atthu ònyokhiwa mwaha w ephattu aya ?
mukomunidadeni mwahu ninnakhaliherya atthu othene ntoko amus ihu , walá nnathanla ale a nihimo nahu ? othene ahu ninnakhaliherya alipa-òthoiwa ?
anakheliwa saí atthu ankhuma ilapo sikina ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
miteko sa ikharari s erutthu t iya :
wavaha yolya avoliwe .
wavaha yowurya ari ni ntthona .
wavaha yowara òthaleliwa .
wavaha opuro aletto .
wakhaliherya aretta .
waxekurya òtthukeliwa .
wavitha òkhwa .
omukhaliherya òxanka hatá ahimusuwelaka , wirenle yorera erutthu awo melo !
makhalelo ahu
atthu a nloko n amakhuwa annitthara solimalela sa khalai .
akhwá mulopwana. anamanloko a mulopwan ole okhwiye. annimuthanla mulopwana mukina wira amutheleke namukhweli uwo . akhottá vale annimomola namukhweli uwo emwakhaka itthu sawe sothene . vano namukhweli ole onnivira ahawaka vamosá n an awe .
athiyana òrupala khanlya moje , mana annihimya wira yalya vale , anayara ana ahirina ikharari .
anamwane khamphiya vanokhwani. mana khalyale ekhalawa. onihimmwa wira olava .
atthu anrowa onokhwani , yakhuma omahiye. etthikelaka owani , ampacerya wemela mphironi , khunyawaka matata , khurapihaka ihipa n ikatana sirinaya vavo .
ehapari yorera
vano afarisi awo n awixuttihi a ikano yahimukoha yesu wira : awixutti anyu ahinttharela-ni ikano sa makhulupal ihu a khalai , anlyelya-ni ehinyanwe ?
yesu ahiwakhula wira : anawothe , profeta yesaya òhimya ekekhai ya nyuwo , valempyawe wira : atthu ala anikittittimiha ni molumo pahi , nto mirima saya siri ottaiwene ni miyo . awo ankittittimiha siyo , ikano sinixuttihaya ti soruma s atthu pahi . nyuwo munnihiya otthara molumo a muluku , munatthara ikano s atthu .
murima wa katekese
okhala mukristu vominyalela okhotta solimalela sihinreriha ekumi .
katekese ovinre ònixuttiha wira ohawa wa mutthu mukhw ihu ori ntoko nsu na muluku nnihanela omukhaliherya .
yesu ònixuttiha-tho wira nihisototheke ni solimalela sipakiwe n atthu a khalai . solimalela iyo sinninihimerya siralyaya atthu a khalai , nto itthu sintthunahu wira mahiku ala ninnixutta nikupalelaka miruku isyá sinreriha makhalelo ahu .
tivó vantthunahu osariha murim ahu n othunku ni nttittimiho ni murettele n utteliwa. nihiyaka wova , ehaya , winiwa murima ni ethanyeryo .
yesu khalempe elivuru , khawixuttihale atthu etthu emosa-mosa entthunaya wira okathi t ukathi . masi molumo othene èhapari yorera , yetteliwa ni yesu , ehinatthi olempwa .
okristu khuhiyó edini y elivuru pahi , walá ya solimalela. masi edini y atthu akumi animutthara yesu àkhwenle awo ni ohihimuwale . edini yorera ni yohipahuwa oholo wa muluku tith ihu , t ila : okhaliherya ikwasuni ni wakhaliherya athiyana anamukhweli mohawani mwaya , nisukaka naxinene òhittheka , niviraka motakhalani mwa vathi-va .
yesu khakhapelenle solimalela sa nloko nayariwawe . khatthunne otthara ikano sikina sattharaya atthu othene . yowo ònivaha nikano nimosá pahi : mphentaneke mukina ni mukhw awe . sisale miyo kophentalyakani , siso-tho nyuwo muhana ophentana .
ninnisototha nihimyaka wira : hiyo ninnilompa , hiyo nobatiziwa , hiyo ninnitthara ikano ni solimalela . vano , akhalá mutthu onihimya wira : miyo kinnimphenta muluku masi okathi yowo anamunyokha munn awe , owo nawothé : vekekhai ole ohinimphenta munn awe onimdnawe , khamverya omphenta muluku ohinimònawe .
ovekela
muluku ! kivaheni murima woloka : mukiruhele-tho eroho y ekekhai .
muhikòmole vamaithoni vanyu , muhikitthyawiheryé eroho anyu yowarya .
ovanela ni olehana
ninnisuwela murerelo wa solimalela s ephattu ahu walá ninnitthara iyo mana nolakiwa ?
ninnirukunuxa solimalela sa khalai sihinrerela-tho mahiku ala ? athiyana n amiravo annitthuniheriwa olavula mmuthukumanoni mwahu ? ninnittittimiha sorera sinihimyaya walá siniraya ?
ohikuxé etthu ila . ohilyé etthu ekina . ohivaré etthu ile : ikano iya sinòneya okhala sa miruku : nto khasirina ikuru s oxintta makhalelo òtakhala a mutthu .
ti pani onnivaha s oxintta solimalela sahu sotakhala ? yesu ahiwoniherya atthu wira solya sothene ti sorera .
muluku ohapattuxerya atthu itthu sothene wira sakhaliheryeke okhala sana : molumo ala annihimerya-ní ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
kinovahani nikano na nanano : mphentaneke mukina ni mukhw awe .
sisale miyo kophentalyakani , siso-tho nyuwo muhana ophentana .
atthu animuluvala , khiyakhwa yixuttaka etthu emosa emosa khula nihiku !
makhalelo ahu
mukomunidadeni mukristu mmosá anivara ni murim awe wothene muteko w ekomunidade . vaviralyaya iyakha sikina , okathi wa pentekósiti akristu a nloko nlo yahona wira varerela omuthanla mukristu mukina omuranttela .
vano owo arantteliwene , khamukhalihenrye mukhw awe okelenle muteko , nto ahipacerya oinwapa , khwisinnuha mmansawe ahimyaka wira : miyo kasuwela ovara mutek owo , khuhikitthuniherya-tho ! nto kintthuna wona !
ehapari yorera
yesu ahihimya nlikanyiho nikina , awasaka atthu akina yàthanya akhw aya , yisonaka okhala anaxariya . yesu khwira : alopwana anli yahikela mpani mwa muluku , wira elompe . mukina ari nfarisi , mukina ari mulipa-òliviha mpósito .
nfarisi ule , emenlene , anilompa ni murim awe , ìraka : múluku , kinnoxukhuruni mwaha w ohilikanaka miyo n atthu akina , akhanle anawĩye , òtakhala murima , anamararuwa : nnákhala nkikhanle ntoko natampi ula . miyo kinnitthukwa mahiku manli khula esumana . kinnivaha mwàvulo wa itthu sothene sirinaka .
mulipa-òliviha mpósito , emenle ottaiwene , khatthuna hatá ottukhula maitho awehaka osulu . animana etthirim awe ahimyaka wira : múluku ! mukimorele ikharari , mana ka natampi .
murima wa katekese
nihimulamuleke mutthu :
muluku pahi t onisuwela mirima s atthu .
ehapari yorera yiwalyahu esumana evinre , yanihimerya wira : atthu ala anikittittimiha ni molumo pahi : nto mirima saya siri attaiwene ni miyo .
vano yesu onninihimerya t avi makhalelo anweryahu omwattamela muluku wira nimphenteke owo ni namoreleke ikharari akhw ihu , ntoko an awe èkekhai .
nlikanyiho ninnihimeryawe yesu , nri ntoko elola : mulolani memmo ninniwerya wona witho wahu . nonaka mwettelo wa nfarisi uwo ni wa mulipa-òliviha mpósito , ninniwerya otthokelela mwettelo ahu .
nfarisi anilompa amuthonyiheryaka muluku sowira sawe sorera ni wiwelela wawe ikano . attharaka ikano iyo , nfarisi owo anisona okhala naxariya othanleliwa wòpowa ni anathanya anatampi .
mulipa-òliviha mpósito , aisuwelaka okhala natampi , animuroromela muluku ni animwamini wira t awerya omòpola . ahittharuwa , khuvekela nlevelelo , tivó vakhumalyawe molompani aleveleliwene .
hiyo imara sikina ninnupuwela ntoko nfarisi uwo , nihimyaka wira : miyo kinnilompa , nto nkinakhela etthu , kinniwelela soruma sa muluku , nto kinvira kihawaka . tthiri hiyo nnolikana ni nfarisi uwo . vano , nireke-ni ?
niwehe owitho wahu , onlikana ni owitho wa nfarisi uwo . nihimye wira nri anawothe , nimaneke etthirim ahu ntoko siralyawe mulipa-òliviha mpósito . siso nniweryahu oleveleliwa . olompa wekekhai khuhiyó omuhimerya muluku wira , miyo kinnophentani pahi , nto onvekela ikuru s otthara soruma sawe .
olompa wekekhai ti wamini wira muluku onniniphenta khula okathi , hatá nimutthekenle imara sinjene .
olompa wekekhai ti ohova otthikela wa muluku ninvekelaka nlevelelo , nirukunuxaka murima .
ovanela ni olehana
olompa wa nfarisi khiwamusivenle muluku . yahalela exeni olompa wawe ?
mulipa-òliviha mpósito ari natampi , masi olompa wawe wahakheliwa . mana xeni ?
hiyo ninlompela-ni ? ninlompela wira muluku anirele sintthunahu , walá ninlompa wira nisuwele otthuna wawe , nitthareke ?
olompa wahu ori okereja pahi onthukumanahu othene walá ninnilompa vatthokoni vahu ?
munnisuwela okathi mukina yesu walompawe ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
olompa ovanela ni muluku tith ihu , ntoko mwana sinvanelawe n ame awe .
muhimya s akhw awe , onihiya sawawe siri leveleve !
makhalelo ahu
lusiano mmiravó orina iyakha muloko ni thanu na mosá . osomme oxikhola mpakha elivuru yanexexe , nto okhala wira kharina musurukhu , khawenrye otthikela osoma . tivó ahupuwela okhuma mmuttettheni rawawe n urowa opoma ovekela muteko . weiwo ahimphwanya pirisori akhumme khalai mmuttettheni mwawe memmo , onasomiha opoma weiwo . owo ahimutthuniherya okhala owannyawe . owo t òthela , ohana anamwane athanú . ararú annetta oxikhola . vano-nto anli axinamwane .
vano lusiano muteko awe t okwesa vapuwani , orowela ikhuni. wasuka axinamwane , okattha ikuwo sothene sa vatthokoni vale ni wokolola ni fero . okhala wira lusiano mukristu , ahinvekela pirisori uwo wira amutthuniherye orowa mukereja ettiminku yaphiya vale , weiwo onrowawe-tho pirisori uwo n amwar awe n an awe . ahimutthuniherya amuhimeryaka wira : wamala olompa , muhipiseke ohokolowela owani nno , okhala wira muteko khurere watta vapuwani va : hiyo khanrere .
vano lusiano akhala khula ewora ni muteko , amumula vakhani okathi warowawe olompa mukereja .
ehapari yorera
yesu ahikela-tho mpani mothukumana : ahikhala memmo mulopwana òrakala ntata . vano afarisi yaninwehexexa yesu , wira emone atthunaka onvoniha mutth uwo nihiku nle n asàbadu , wira emukumiherye mulattu . vano yesu ahimwirela òrakal ole : mwemele , murwé eriyari va .
vano ahakoha atthu ale wira : etthu enemiheriwa nihiku n asábadu tivi ? wira sorera walá sotakhala ? omòpola mutthu walà ompwetexa ?
ale khiyàkhulanse etthu . vano yesu ahawehexexa okherekhere n uviruwa , aripiwene murima mwaha w olipa wa mirima saya , khumwirela mulopwan ole : mòkole ntata .
owo ahòkola ntata , khukhala nikumi .
afarisi ekhumakaru vale , yahithukumana n atthu a herodi , wira evanelele mamwivelo yesu .
murima wa katekese
yesu onninitaphula mwa solimalela sinnikhaliha ipottha .
atthu a isarayeli nihiku na sábadu , yanitthuwa , khuhiyavar etthu . nikano n omumula nihiku na sábadu nahupuxeriwa ni muluku okathi atthu wakhalihiwaya ipottha , ekhanyererihiwaka ovara muteko mahiku othene .
mwaha w ekano y omumula esábadu , muluku omphavela wakiha exariya y atthu othene y ohiya miteko sa vathi-va nihiku nimosá , wira ephwanyeke ikuru mwerutthuni mwaya , ekhaleke vatthokoni n amusi aya ni emuttottopeleke muluku àpattunxe . nvare miteko sanyu mpakha mahiku mathanu na mosa : masi ni-hiku nanethanu na rnanli mmumule , wira emumule hatá epotth anyu ni muletto anyu , ni wira emumule enyompe ni mwaburu anyu .
muluku onnakiha hatá inama wira ehihaxiweke .
siviraka iyakha sinjene nikano na sábadu , nirummwe òwòpola atthu mwepotthani , nikhanle nikano nulupalexa nàkhottiherya atthu ovara miteko hatá sikhani : wanikhottihiwa wapeya yolya , walola aretta , wetta ekwaha yorakama .
siso , atthu yanihawa mulattu wa nikano na sábadu nahataphuleliwe n ekekhai . yesu àvonihaka aretta nihiku na sábadu , òthonyerya wira esábadu t ipakeliwe mutthu , khahiyó mutthu opakeliwe esábadu .
tivó yesu vavonihawe aretta esábadu .
n ulipa waya murima mafarisi yanikhapelela ikano sahawerya okhottiwa nnákhala ni mutthu mmosá . tivó vamonalyaya yesu anvonihaka muretta nihiku na sábadu , yahitthokelela wira anihonona edini yekekhai . ti mana yupuwenlyaya omwiva .
yesu anisuwela wira mafarisi awo khiyàmukupali ni yantthuna omwiva , nto khonve . yesu anitthuna owiwelela atithi yamurumme wira àsuwelihe atthu othene muluku èkekhai ni àtaphule mwa sowotha ni sohaxa sothene , vanjenexa seiyo simpakiwa ni nsina n edini
ovekela
apwiya ! elapo yosareya ophenta wanyu : mukixuttihe molumo anyu . apwiya , nyuwo mokirela ntoko sikihimenryanyu : mokirerela murima miyo , murumeyi anyu .
mukivahe osuwela n ankhili : okhala wira kinniroromela ikano sanyu .
ovanela ni olehana
yesu anavoniha aretta nihiku na sábadu , nto afarisi yanikhottiha ovoniha iwo , mana esábadu yari nihiku n omumula wira atthu emuttittimiheke muluku . hiyo nnira exeni nihiku na ttiminku ?
onihimya-ni okhala òlipa murima ?
ohiraruwé . ohìyé . , muluku ni soruma iya onninikhottiherya pahi , walá onninithonyerya ephiro y opuha wekekhai ?
ti sivi ikano ni solimalela s ephattu ahu sinnikhottiherya owirela akhw ihu sorera ?
atthu a isarayeli yanimumulela muteko esábadu , hiyo akristu ninnimumula nihiku na ttiminku ; exeni ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
ettiminku nihiku n apwiya , nnupuwelahu okhwa n uhihimuwa wa yesu , ninnitthapela masu apwiya n okaristiya .
muluku nthiti , akhwiri t ari nrima !
ehapari yorera ya yesu : okhalihana
yesu ahipacerya wavoniha aretta ni walevelela anatampi okhala wira onniphavela wirà na vasyá w atthu , makhalelo masyá , othene ekhalihanaka .
atthu anjene annikhalihana , nto momusini mwaya palti walá mopatthanani mwaya . siso-tho okathi wa yesu , atthu othene yanaphenta apatthani aya , nto ayuda yanathanya agalileya ni othene yananyokha asamariya .
antthuna okela momweneni mmo , khanwerya owomola akina , nnákhala awanani aya .
yesu owakhulela atthu othene yatthuna ovanela n uwo . ohaphavelatho mafarisi n awixuttihi a ikano yamwapa .
yesu ohaphenta atthu othene , khaphentale ame awe n amusi awe pahi , ohaphenta-tho awanani awe okhala wira othene ana a muluku .
makhalelo ahu
nikhuru nimosá na makatekúmeno nanetetela obatizo n uthelana mukereja . ahikhala memmo lúsia n iy awe yoaki n akhw aya . yahikhala-tho memmo anakhulu n anamukhweli .
nattamelaka nira n obatizo , yoaki ahirowa othuma ikuwo s amwar awe . vahokolowalyawe , lúsia ahona ikuwo , khusiveliwa vanjene .
ehapari yorera
murima wa katekese
òreriwa t ale animwamini yesu ni anvahererya ekumi aya wira yarumeleke atthu othene .
yesu ahirowa omwako olompa : molompani mmo atithi amuruma yesu olaleya n upaka nloko nisyá . tivó vàthanlalyawe arummwa wira ekelé nloko nenlo . awixutti othene a yesu , ti nloko nirummwe olaleya omwene w atithi mpakha wokiseryani w elapo .
yesu akhuruwaka vamwako ahaphwanya atthu anjene yarwenle omwiwa , n uvonihiwa iretta saya . othene yawo t axinn awe , tivó vàvonihalyawe ni vàlalènryawe oreriwa wekekhai omphwanyaneya nikhalaka ntoko axinna , nikawelanaka sorera sinvahiwahu n atithi amosaru .
yesu ti mulupale a nloko n axinn awo. ti masikhini ni òwiyeviha , khamphavela mihakhu sa vathi-va , kharwiye waruma atthu , khanisukery etthu . oreriwa wawe warumela atthu othene ni wavaha ekumi awe .
amasikhini òreriwa t ale animwamini yesu ni ankhala ntoko sakhanlyawe : anamini wira sothene sirinaya , ti muluku àvahale wira ekawelaneke ntoko axinna . opuha waya khahiyó okhalana mihakhu sinjene , masi okhala ana a muluku n axinna atthu othene .
nimphentaka yesu , nnamutthara , nihana okawelana sothene sirinahu ntoko amusi , siso omwene wa muluku t onarwelaya atthu othene . atthu othene òwamini yarina murima mmosá n iroho emosá . khavo mutthu aihimya wira mihakhu sawe sari sawaweru pahi : sothene khula mutthu sarinawe sari s atthu othene . yesu ahiwihana arummwa wira ekhaleke vamosá ni yowo ela leyaka omwene wa muluku . vano ti hiyo nnihaneliwa orummwa olaleya omwene yowo .
ovekela
pwiya yesu munivahe eparakha y okhala vamosá ni nyuwo , munivahe otteliwa murima nàkawelaka akhw ihu ekumi ahu .
ovanela ni olehana
tivi ephiro ahu wira niphwanyeke oreriwa ?
athajiri anathanya atthu òthoiwa t òreriwa ?
khino okhala mukristu t ophwanya itthu sothene owĩyeryaka akhw awe , ntoko siniraya atthu akina ?
vatthokoni mulopwana n amwar awe anikawelana sai sorera simphwanyaya ?
mukomunidadeni ninkawelana sai ekumi , miteko ni sorera simphwanyahu ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
òreriwa t ale ari amasikhini murohoni mwaya , okhala wira omwene wa wirimu ti wawaya .
òreriwa t ale òripiwa murima , okhala wira muluku onimwakurunuxa murima .
òreriwa t ale òmoriwa ikharari , okhala wira muluku onimwamorela ikharari .
òreriwa t ale òrera murima , okhala wira anomona muluku .
òreriwa t ale amphavela wiwanana ni murettele , okhala wira muluku onimwakhaliha an awe .
òreriwa t ale anihaxiwa mwaha w omwiwelela muluku , okhala wira omwene wa muluku ti wawaya .
makhale lo ahu
muttetthe mmosá w opoma , ahikhala mama mmosá nakhulu . ohiyu omosá ahirimeliwa maratth awe maxexe . vano ahikelela ophavelasa n ukohakoha mw anamwattamanani awe , masi othene aya khavo asuwela . ahiripiwa murima vanjene okhala wira arina mihuwo iyo pahi . ti maratth awo yanvaha moje makina yapeyawe , makina yatumihawe wira athumeke iye saphavelawe .
ehapari yorera
yesu ahira-tho :
nyuwo mwaphentakaru ale anophentani pahi , ophenta wanyu xen iwo ? hatá alipa-òtakhala annaphenta ale anarerela murima . mwawirelaka sorera ale aniwirelani pahi , ophenta wanyu xen iwo ? hatá alipa-òtakhala anmra siso . ankhi mwawolihaka ale pahi anakupalinyu wohokoloxeryani , ophenta wanyu xen iwo ? hatá alipa-òtakhala annolihana , eroromelaka wakhela volikanela .
nto nyuwo mwaphenteke awanan inyu nwireleke sorera akhw inyu ; nwoliheke , muhilipelelaka ohokoloxeriwa . siso otthuveliwa wanyu onokhala wulupale , munrowa okhala àna a muluku : tthiri muluku t òwarerela murima ale ahinimuxukhuru n ale òtakhala murima . mukhaleke òmoriwa ikharari , ntoko muluku tith inyu oryawe òmoriwa ikharari .
murima wa katekese
nikhalaneke okathi t ukathi murima w olevelela .
muluku tithi onnamorela ikharari atthu othene . ikharari iyo s atithi ti muthuko onettiherya mwettelo ahu w akristu .
niwunlelaka ikuhu ale annirela sotakhala , ninrowa winjererya sotakhala ni sotakhala sikina . moro khunttipihiwa ni moro . nalevelelaka ninnivukula sotakhala seiyo . yesu onninixuttiha oxintta sotakhala niwirelaka awanan ihu sorera .
akina anihimya wira : nalevelelaka ale annlyerya , awo anotepa , khaninwerya walevelela .
exeni ennirelawe muluku ? hiyo othene ninnimutthekela imara sinjene , nikhottaka molumo awe . owo onnettiha sai ? vano muluku ònithonyerya khuluwi oniphenta waive wulupale , tthiri kristu ònikhwela hiyo , varyahu nlelo anatampi .
yesu , mwana a muluku , ahalompela hatá ale yamwiva wira eleveleliwe .
oniphenta wawe yesu ti wekekhai , okhala wira t opajenrye oniphenta hiyo nari anatampi , nihinatthi orukunuxa murima . khavo omphwanela wopoliwa mwaha wa sorera sinirawe . ninnopoliwa mwaha w orera wawe murima muluku .
okhala wira nophentiwa ni muluku nihiphwanelaka , hiyo-tho naphenteke awanan ihu . siso nnolikana ni yesu nikhalaka ana a muluku .
ovekela
apwiya yesu !
nyuwo mulenve ekumi anyu mwaha wa hiyo anatampi .
nivaheni eparakha y okupali oniphenta wanyu , wira naphenteke hatá ale annitthekela .
ovanela ni olehana
ononihereya sai ophenta wekekhai wa mukristu vatthokoni vawe ? mukomunidadeni ni mmakhaleloni mw atthu othene ?
muluku onniniphenta mana ninnimwettela katekese ninnitthara molumo awe ? walá okhala wira owo tith ihu ?
nakhaliheryaka akhw ihu walá niraka sorera niroromelaka pahi wakhela sorera nnimutthara yesu ?
muluku onnimuhukhumu natampi walá onnikhotta etampi ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
miteko sa ikharari s eroho t iya :
ovaha miruku sorera
omwixuttiha ohinsuwela
omuttaruxa onira sotakhala
omukurunuxa murima òripiwe .
omulevelela oniruwanne .
ohawa n uvilela sopahula s akhw ihu .
wavekelela wa muluku atthu akumi n alipa-okhwa .
mwire murima khurunu , ntoko namanriya akhuraka miwi !
makhalelo ahu
mukomunidadeni mw akristu yakhala anamwane a iyakha simphiyerya wunnuwihiwa , axipapa aya annitthokihanasa . yalikanela vale , annimphavela mulipa-òlyiha masoma wira awunnuwihe , annivanela n uwo wira esuwele esisapo enrowaya omuliva .
numalá annivira yàsuwelihaka makhulupale a mmuttettheni , ntoko mamwene n atthu a guvernu . masi mamwene awo khansiveliwa ni mutek ola w akristu , tivó annivira yàxankihaka akristu ni yàkumiheryaka mulattu , ehimyaka wira anniwakha omwene aya ni miyavulo saya .
ehapari yorera
yesu ahitthikela owani . vano muttitthi w atthu wahithukumana-tho : siso yesu n awixutti awe hatá yanojela olya . amusi awe yesu , vaiwalyaya siso , yahimurowela wira emukuxe , mana yanihimya wira : orovahuwa . nave awixuttihi a ikano , yakhumme oyerusalemu , yanihimya wira : ole ovariwé ni bèlizebuli . akina yanihimya wira : owerya wa mulupale a malaikha òtakhala t onomolanawe malaikha awo !
vekekhai , yanihimya wira : owo ori ni nlaikha notakhala .
vano yahiphiya ame awe yesu n axinn awe . awo yahemela vaté , khumwihaniha . atthu anjene yira ekilanthe emurukurenryene . vano yahimuhimerya wira : amam inyu n axinn inyu ari vaté vale , annophavelani .
yesu ahiwakhula wira : amama n axinn aka tani ?
awehawehaka atthu yakilanthe emurukurenryene , ahìra : amama n axinn aka t ala . tthiri , othene ale anettela otthuna wa muluku , yawo t akhanle axinn aka n axirokor aka n amam aka .
murima wa katekese
amusi èkekhai a yesu t ale anettela otthuna wa muluku , ettharaka exariya .
atthu anjene yansiveliwa ni yesu . tthiri , owo ahavoniha aretta ni ahiwòpola atthu yavariwe ni malaikha ònanara .
awixuttihi a ikano yanona wira itthu sirawe yesu sari sorera , masi yanova wakhiwa owerya waya , tivó vamulupatthaya . ohimya wira ti yotakhala eyo ekhanle yorera , ni wira ti yorera eyo ekhanle yotakhala , ti oveha eroho yowarya. n ukhotta ekekhai .
yesu ahalopola awixuttihi a ikano iraka : ale anveha eroho yowarya , khanrowa ophwanya nlevelelo . ni molumo ala yesu aphavela wahimerya wira etthokeleleke ni ehimyeke ekekhai ni ettharuweke .
yesu ti muluku èkekhai , khikuxerenrye mwaha wa sorera sawirenlyawe atthu ni khaphavenle wasiveliha makhulupale nnákhala axinn awe , iraka satthunaya nto ahahimerya ekekhai khula okathi .
amusi èkekhai a yesu t awo aniwiriyana masu awe . ale aninwiriyana yesu , enamwiwelela , annira sintthunawe muluku . masu a yesu makumi ni annavaha atthu ekumi ya muluku n uphenta wawe .
ovekela
apwiya yesu , nivaheni eparakha y owiriyana sana masu anyu annithonyerya otthuna w atithi , netteleke .
ovanela ni olehana
hiyo akristu ninnilavula sinjene sa yesu . nto vekekhai ninnisuwela omwene wa muluku walaleyawe , ninnettela ?
amusi a yesu yanihimya wira : orovahuwa . awixuttihi a ikano yanihimya wira : ole ovariwé ni bèlizebuli . hiyo nnihimya-ni ?
nnimusuwela sai mutthu , òbatiziwa walá òhibatiziwa , wira t a nloko na yesu ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
eroho yowarya ti muluku oniwettiherya atthu a maloko othene mw ekekhai ni òniwatàniha omusi omosá .
ohileleya ohawa mutthu !
malikanyiho omwene wa muluku
atthu anjene yanimutthara yesu ephavelaka wona sirawe walá orerihiwa ni yowo , nto khiyaivahererya mmansaya wira epajeryeke omwene yesu wàlaleryawe .
malikanyiho t ithale yesu onahimeryawe atthu animwiwa wira etthokeleleke sana . malikanyiho anisuweliha omwene wa muluku opajenrye ni onikhala mwa yesu . alipa-òhona , vano annòna , alipa-òrakala , annetta orattene , anamakuttula annivonihiwa , alipa-òhiwa , vano anniwa , atthu akhwiye annihihimuwa .
mitikiniho iyo t ithonyeryo s omwene wa muluku . epyó y etrigu yamorela vathí , khuhikhwá , enikhala emosaru yeyo pahi . vano epyó eyo yakhwá , ennima mihokorokho sinjene .
makhalelo ahu
ehavo elapo emosa y afrika enihaniwa uganda . atthu anjene èlapo ele akristu . masi khalai khiyàphwanyaneya akristú .
okathi ophiyalyaya weiwo , mapatiri yahipacerya olaleya ehapari yorera . atthu akina yahikupali , khuvekela obatiziwa .
akina a yawo yari arumeyi a mwené èlapo eyo , ihaniwa mwanda . mwené owo khakhottiherya atthu awe okhala akristu , masi atthuna wira yiweleleke sothene sarumawe , seiyo savirikanya soruma sa muluku .
akristu yanikhotta otthara ikano sotakhala sa mwené aya . owo ahinanariwa vanjene , khuruma wiviwa arumeyi awe miloko mili n anli , amiravo n anakhulu . akina yarohitiwa , akina yapahiwe yonaka .
ehapari yorera
numalá , yesu ahira : ari ni màru òwiwa , yiweke !
vakhanlyaya wiphini , ale yakhala ni yesu vamosa n arummwa mulokó nanli , yahimukoha mwaha wa malikanyiho . yesu ahahimerya wira : nyuwo movahiwa osuwela esiri y omwene wa muluku . vano ale ahikhanle awihu anixuttihiwa sothene ni malikanyiho , wira ewehaka orattene , ehoneké ; yiwaka orattene , ehisuweleké : siso , ehirukunuxe mirima saya , ehileveleliwe .
yesu ahahimerya wira : nyuwo muhinsuwela nlikanyiho nla , muntthuna osuwela sai malikanyiho makina othene ? mulipa-òmisa t ule onlaleya ehapari yorera . mphironi mwamorenle epyó munlikana n atthu ale anìwa ehapari yorera , nto emalihakaru wiwa , onnorwa satana nananoru , khuwakha ehapar ile yorera yàliwe mwa yawo .
murima wa katekese
niroromeleke ikuru sa masu a muluku .
ntoko siwalyahu mmithukumanoni sivinre , yesu ahilupatthiwa : amusi awe yanimwapa , mafarisi yanivanelela mamwivelo . vano yesu inre-ni ? apajenrye orukunuxa mwettelo awe wira àsivelihe atthu awo yamulupattha ? nnari . nlikanyiho niwalyahu. ninnithonyerya wira yesu anroromela khuluwi ehapari yorera yàlaleryawe atthu , hatá asuwelaka wira akina yanimukhotta .
yesu khamakenle olavula pahi wira : òreriwa t ale ari amasikhini . , nto yowo ari masikhini , òwimàliha , òmoriwa ikharari ni aphavelexa exariya . yesu mmansawe t okhanle epyó . atthu akina enamwi ephavelaka ohonona mwixuttiho awe , molumo awe yahiraneya : tthiri ahiviwa , nto òhihimuwa , vano ehapari yorera yomwarela mulaponi mothene .
ovanela ni olehana
khula mutthu aikoheke mmurimani mwawe : kinwiriyana sai ehapari yorera ? murim aka onlikana n iphiro , walá n itthaya yattanne masorosoro ni miwa mapuro makina , walá n itthaya yowunttelana ?
exeni enkikhottiherya okhala etthaya yowunttelana ?
alipa-òwiveliwa wamini a wuganda khiyàtthanre okathi mmosá molumo a muluku ni okathi mukina molumo a mwené aya. nto yatthanre ehapari yorera khula okathi . hiyo nnira-ni ?
ninnasuwela atthu a mulaponi mwahu yahawenle wettela wamini waya ?
makhalelo ahu
akatarina yahitheliwa n afelisi mukereja , yahikhalana anamwane anili . vano afelisi yahatteya , khuhiya wetta okapela . akatarina yahijikula vanjene , masi yahilipiha wamini waya , khiyarowa olompa khula ettiminku .
vano mwana mwamukhani ahiwereiwa . ohiyu ahitepa . afelisi khiyarivo . amama yahinvekela mukristu , namwattamanani aya , wira ambatize mwan owo . mukrist uwo khwakhula wira anova mwahá w atithi awe atteiye . vano ohiyu yole mwana ahikhwa . akristu yahirowa wakhaliherya amusi awo , masi ansiau khiyàlompale .
ehapari yorera
yesu ahahimerya atthu nlikanyiho nikina iraka : omwene wa wirimu onlikana ni mulopwana mmosa ànle epyó yorera mmatta mwawe . vano ohiyu , atthu othene erupaka , nwanani awe mulopwan owo ahirwa , ahàla-mo epyó yonanara , mmatta memmo mwàliwe etrigu , kjpurowa .
yesu ahahimerya atthu nlikanyiho nikina iraka : omwene wa wirimu onlikana n inuku ya murale , mutthu mmosa akuxalyawe , khwàla mmatta mwawe . enuku eyo eri yamukhanixa ovikana inuku sothene : vano yamelá , yannuwaka , ennikhala mwiri mulupale , ovikana miri sikina sa mmatta . siso axipalame annorwa oteka ipurú saya mmirittani mwaya .
yesu ahahimerya-tho nlikanyiho nikina iraka : omwene wa wirimu onlikana ni miropo muthiyana sinkuxawe , khutakanyiha ni miphimo miraru sa makeya , khwetheya . vano , makey ale annìpelana .
itthu iya sothene yesu ahahimerya atthu ni malikanyiho : khivo yàhimeryawe ehikhanle ni malikanyiho , wira slraneye sahimyalyawe muluku ni molumo a maprofeta wira : kinrowa olavula ni malikanyiho , kinrowa olaleya itthu sipithihiwe okhuma vapattuxiwaya olumwenku .
yesu ahalaxerya atthu awo , khurowa owani . vano awixutti awe yahimuthukumanela , khumwirela wira : munitaphulele nlikanyiho na nthakathaka na mmatta .
yesu ahiwakhula wira : onàla epyó yorera ti mwana a mutthu . ematt eyo , olumwenku . epyó yorera t ale anettela omwene wa wirimu . nthakathaka t ale anetta ni satana . nwanani onàla epyó eyo yonanara ti satana yowo . okathi w ohepha , nihiku n omala olumwenku . alipa-òhepha , malaikha òrera .
murima wa katekese
masu a muluku anninnuwa hatá eriyari y atakhali .
sihavo itthu sinnitikiniha vanjene : atthu anjene khanamini ehapari yorera , khunamutthara yesu . akristu akina , yari òroromeleya , vano àhiya nloko nahu , khiyettela iphiro sikina . mapuro othene ninniphwanya sorera ni sotakhala .
vano yesu ni malikanyiho yiwalyahu. onninitaphulela sotikiniha iyo , onninisuweliha itthu sipithihiwe .
ehapari yorera mmurimani mwahu eri ntoko enuku yamukhanixa , nto enamwi eri yamukhanixa yokhalana ikuru sulupale wira exintte sotakhala .
nwanani onnàla nthakathaka , siso atthu anjene annira sotakhala , hatá hiyo akristu ninnira . vano epyó yorera yàlalyawe muluku. yokhalana ikuru s oruwerya hatá eriyari ya nthakathaka .
yesu mmurimani mwawe arina epyó yorera pahi , ahiwonela othunku anatampi. khaphavenle walamula ni wahukhumu , anawehererya wira erukunuxe mirima saya .
yesu onnitthanela wira nikhaleke epyó yorera vamosá ni yowo .
itthu sipithihiwe sinlaleyawe yesu ti ikharari sa muluku. onvaha khula mutthu okathi wira arukunuxe murim awe .
ovanela ni olehana
muluku onnakumiherya nsuwa atthu òtakhala murima vamosá n ale òrera murima . hiyo nnavilela sai ale ankhalela nthiti wira itthu sotakhala ?
muluku onnimorela ikharari hiyo nnimutthekela , wira nitthikeleke ottheka walá wira nirukunuxe murima ?
nniwettiherya sai alipa-òttheka : òwatteya , òmwalana , anawíye , anamuttompe ? vanrerela owomolaka mukomunidadeni ? walá nakhaliheryeke wira yiweke ehapari yorera ni erukunuxeke mirima saya ?
mukristu okhottale ombatiza mwanamwane ahanle okhwa , anamini ikharari sa muluku ? ankhi ansiau uwo ohamulompenle anvithaka ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
yesu ti mwana a muluku onàla mmurimani mwahu epyó yorera y ophenta wawe .
makhalelo ahu
anifa varyawe mwalí , mwene èlapo awe ahinvekela okhala pwiyamwene , wira aheleleke makeya minepa s atthu avinre . amusi awe yahakhulela wira nsina n apipi awe nihirimele .
numalá anifa ahitheliwa ni mukristu amurowanne okatekeseni .
n uwerya wa muluku anifa ahihiya opwiyamwene ni murim awe wothene , khutteliwa murima akhalaka mukristu .
ehapari yorera
omwene wa wirimu onlikana ni muhakhu ovithiwe mmatta . mutthu oniphwanya muhakh ule onnivitha-tho nananoru . vano , atteliwene murima , onnirowa otumiha sothene sirinawe , khuthuma ematt eyo .
omwene wa wirimu onlikana-tho ni mulipa a nakoso , omphavela maluku òwarya òrerexa . aphwanyá nluku nowarya ni norikexa , onnirowa otumiha sothene sirinawe , khuthuma nluku nle .
murima wa katekese
wamini omwene wa muluku ti muhakhu wyekumi ahu .
mmithukumanoni mili sivinre nihiwa wira omwene wa muluku onlikana n ipyó yamukhani . epyó eyo yamelá , enninnuwa eriyari ya itthu sinjene sinvirikanya . eriyari y etrigu ninnikhumelela nthakathaka .
mwanene ematta ti muluku , khantikinihiwa . masu awe t oweryexa , khivo enojelaya . hiyo ninnivekeliwa wamini , mana muhokorokho onnivahaya masu awo , khunoneya nananoru .
mutthu onkumana ni yesu , onniphwanya muhakhu w omwene wa muluku , atteliwene murima , onnihiya itthu sothene wira amutthareke .
yesu pahi ti mòpoli , mwa yowo nimphwanyahu ekumi n upuha , nimuhiyaka nimphwanya okhwa .
atthu animona mutthu ontumiha sothene sirinawe , annupuwela wira òvahuwa . owo pahi òhona muhakhu ovithiwe , khantthuna wira omurimele .
siso otteliwa murima nnimphwanyahu niwaka wira nophentiwa ni muluku. noleveleliwa , nri an awe , ti muhakhu ovithiwe , ti nluku nowarya ni norikexa . oniphenta wawe muluku ti worera ovikami ekumi !
mutteliweke murima okathi p ukathi . mulompeke vohihiyererya , mmutthapele muluku mwa itthu sothene : p itthu enihaneliwanyu n utthuna wa muluku mwa yesu kristu .
ovekela
eroho aka ennohawelani , ntoko etthaya yowuma , ehikhalanne màsi .
ovanela ni olehana
yesu atthuna onitaphulela exeni ni malikanyiho yiwalyahu mpakha vano ?
hiyo nnupuwela wira omwene wa muluku exeni ?
eriyar ihu , ithonyeryo s omwene wa muluku ti sivi ?
khula mutthu akoheke murima we : khino kiwaka ehapari yorera kinnitteliwa murima ? kinamini wira ti yesu mòpoli aka onkilavuliha ?
paulo murummwa ahlttottopa mwaha w akristu yalalenryawe ehapari yorera ni ahalepela molumo ala : mohawani mothene kosareya ohakalala , kotepa otteliwa murima .
miyo kotoko otteliwa murima mwaha wo wettela ehapari yorera , ntoko kihawelaka omuxekurya muretta , walá kimulevelelaka okiruwanne ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
eroho enniphwanyiha ophentana , otteliwa murima , murettele , ovilela , othunku , orera murima , ororomeleya , wiyeviha , wisumaliha .
khivo ekano envirikanya makhalelo ala òrera .
avahaka yolya muttitthi w atthu yamutthara , yesu onisuweliha omaliherya w omwene wa muluku . momweneni mmo atthu othene anrowa okilathi vamosá ni muluku ephentanaka ntoko tithi n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; an awe elyaka vamosá .
omwene wa muluku khahiyó mitekoru sorera sinvarahu . omwene owo ti wamini wulupale wira muluku onkhala mmurimani mwahu . wamini onnivaha murerelo miyupuwelo sa mutthu , molumo anlavulawe ni miteko sinvarawe .
makhalelo ahu
ahikhala thajiri mmosá namilili . mahiku othene anilikanyiherya yolya yinjene ni yosivexa , nto khàvaha akhw awe , àlya mekhawe . vano ahiwereiwa vanjene , khuloha ariheliwene omoroni .
ehapari yorera
mahiku awo , wahithukumana-tho muttitthi w atthu , vano yolya yahamalela . yesu ahiwihana awixutti awe , khwahimerya wira : muttitthi ula kihònela othunku . atthu àvira mahiku mararú ekittharaka , vano kharina yolya . kawirela orowa owani evoliwene , anomora etala mphironi : nave atthu anjene akhumme ottaiwene .
vano awixutti awe yahimwakhula yiraka : ninwerya ophwanya sai yolya yo wavoniha atthu ala othene mothakoni-mu ?
yesu ahakoha iraka : muriná iphau ikavi ?
awo khwakhulasa wira : nriná ithanú na pili .
yesu aharuma atthu okilathi vathi . ahikuxa iphau iyo ithanú na pili , ahimuxukhuru muluku , ahimeyanya , khwavaha awixutti awe wira yakawele atthu othene . awo khwakawela . yahikhalanatho ihopa vakhani soyeva : yesu ahirèriha-tho seiyo , khwaruma awixutti awe wakawela atthu . atthu othene yahilya mpakha ovona . ale yalyiye yahanle ophiyerya atthu ikonto xexé .
yesu ahamwarya atthu awo .
numalá , ahikela mukalawani vamosá n awixutti awe , khurowa elapo y odalmanutha . afarisi akina yahirwa , khupacerya ovanyihana ni yesu . ephavelaka onvelaveliha , yahinvekela ethonyeryo y okhuma wirimu . yesu ahlttha iphumu , khwahimerya wira : atthu ala anikivekelela-ni ethonyeryo ? kinohirneryani ekhweli wira nloko nla khaninvahiwa ethonyeryo .
siso , ahahiya , ahikela-tho mukalawani , analapuwela ekhopela ekina . awixutti yahiliyala okuxa yolya : yarina ephau emosá pahi mukalawani . vano yesu , àlakaka , ahiwirela : mwipasope orattene ni miropo s afarisi ni sa mwené herodi .
awixutti yahipacerya wapelana yaworu wira : tthiri , khanrina iphau . nto yesu ahìwa , khwahimerya wira : munàpeianela-ni mwaha w ohikhalana iphau ? ninlelo khamunòna walá khamunsuwela ? ankhili anyu arottiyeliwa ? mokhalana maitho : muhinònela-ni ? mokhalana màru : muhinìwela-ni ? khamunupuwela ? okathi wakawannyaka iphau thanu , khwavaha atthu ikonto thanu , mwakunxe ithokwa ikavi sasanrye mapattuxa yahanle ?
awo yahakhulasa wira : mulokó ni pili .
yesu ahakoha-tho wira : ankhi okathi wakawannyaka iphau thanu na pili , khwavaha atthu ikonto xexé , mwakunxe ittanka ikavi sasanrye mapattuxa yahanle ?
awo yahakhulasa wira : thanu na pili .
vano ahàkoha wira : nto ninlelo khamunsuwela ?
murima wa katekese
othunku wa yesu onninatà niha mokawanani .
muluku òpattuxa elapo wira atthu othene ekhaleke ni ephwanyeke mo mirerelo s ekumi aya . khathanlale akina wira ekhaleke axinene ni akina-tho ehaweke . owo ori ntoko mama onakhapelela an awe othene .
yesu n awixutti awe mothakoni yarina iphau thanu na pili pahi n ihopa vakhani . sinamwi sari vakhani , yesu ahonela othunku muttitthi w atthu yavoliwa etala . ahaxukhurela yolya eyo atithi ni ahikawana n atthu awo othene . waroromela wawe atithi ni waphenta axinn awe , ahimuthanlaka mutthu , ahinjererya yolya mpakha othene ovona .
yolya yowatta yesu yàvonihanalyawe atthu , mpakha ohala , ti ethonyeryo y ophenta wulupalexa wa muluku , ontthuna wira atthu othene ekhaleke òwitthyala ni òpuha .
khula mutthu onnipuha vekekhai akhalanaka ophenta w atithi , awonelaka othunku akhw awe , avaraka muteko onweryawe , wira othene epuheke .
wamini wira muluku onnaphenta atthu othene , onninvaha khula mutthu ikuru s oxintta milili. onnikawana mihakhu sawe n akhw awe , ntoko siralyawe yesu ekumi awe yothene .
omeyanya ephau , omuxukhurela muluku ni wakawela atthu ti nthonyeryo n otthuna wa yesu wivahererya n ekumi awe wira àreriheke atthu othene , ntoko siralyawe mokhwani mwawe ni mokaristiyani .
ovekela
pwiya , mahiku othene munivaheke ephau ene yeyo !
apwiya , nivaheni murima wolikana ni murim anyu , wira namorele ikharari atthu othene anihawa , niwoneke ntoko axinn ihu n ana a muluku , awo-tho t axinene itthu sirinahu .
ovanela ni olehana
amuhakhalai yanihimya wira : khavo onrupala sawaweru . ninnikupali wira itthu sirinahu , khaniphwannye n ikuru sahu pahi , nto atthu akhw ihu t anikhalihenrye ? ninnikupali wira hiyo nihana weteteya mwaha w akhw ihu ?
nimukhaliheryaka mulipa-òthoiwa , ninnisona okhala alupale oholo wawe , walá ninkupali wira nninvaha eri yawawe mana ti munn ihu ?
yesu ahakoha awixutti awe wira : munàpelanela ni mwaha w ohikhalana iphau ? ankhili anyu arottiyeliwa ? hiyo ninnikohiwa-tho molumo ala : ninnikhupanyerya mwaha w onihalela itthu sinjene , nto khaninkhaliheryana nivaraka muteko othene vamosá . exeni ?
nisukeke mmurim ani mwahu
yesu ahilimalela okuxa ephau , omuxukhuru muluku , omeyanya ni wakawela atthu .
khavo oninnuwela sawaweru !
makhalelo ahu
ehapari yorera
vano yesu ahivenya n awixutti awe , arowaka mittetthe sattamenle okesareya wa filipe . mphironi ahakoha awixutti awe wira :
atthu amra wi miyo ka pani ?
awo yahimwakhula wira : àkhala anihimya wira nyuwo mwá yohani mbatiza , akina wira mwá eliya , akina-tho wira mwá mmosá a maprofeta .
yesu ahakoha-tho iraka : mankhi nyuwo , munihimya wira miyo ti pani ?
pedru ahimwakhula wira : nyuwo kristú .
vano yesu ahakhottiherya n ikuru omulèla mutthu sa yowo .
vano-nto ahipacerya walèla awixutti awe wira :
mwana a mutthu ohana ohawa vanjene n uruniwa n anamukuttho ni mahumu n awixuttihi a ikano . ohana wiviwa n uhihimuwa mokhwani mmurottoni mwaya .
yesu anihimya itthu iya ahivithaka etthu . vano pedru ahimwihana wiphini , khupacerya onvanya . nto yesu ahirukunuwa àwehaka awixutti awe , khumpwapwela pedru , iraka : okhumé va , satana ! we khunupuwela itthu sa muluku : onupuwela s atthu pahi .
yesu ahlhana muttitthi w atthu vamosá n awixutti awe , khwahimerya wira : akhalá mutthu ontthuna okitthara , aikhotte mwanene , akapatteke mwikimanyo awe , akitthareke . tthiri , ole ontthuna wopola ekumi awe , enomurimela ; vano , ole onikupali orimeliha ekumi awe mwaha wa miyo ni wa ehapari yorera , owo onim òpola yeyo .
mutthu onttotta-ni okhala mwanene itthu sothene sa vathi , ekumi awe erowaka opweteya ? walá ontthuna ovaha exeni wira àkakhanye n ikumi awe ? akhalá mutthu onuliwa muru mwaha wa miyo ni wa itthu sinixuttihaka , uliwaka eriyari y atthu ala òhiroromeleya ni òttheka , nave miyo kinimuleliwa muru yowo , vanrwaka movuwani mw atithi vamosá ni malaikha òwarya .
murima wa katekese
otthara otthuna wa muluku vankhweleya wikhotta mwanene ni okupalela ohawa mpakha okhwa .
mwirirya wa yolya yokaweliwa muttitthi w atthu onnithonyerya etthu yulupale yaphavelawe yesu : omwene wa muluku , eyo t iyo , opaka nloko nisyá n atthu , ohikhanle-vo òthanyiwa nnàkhala òthanliwa , akhanle-vo alupale yarumelaka atthu othene wira ekhaleke sana .
yesu ahòna wira attharaka vomalela otthuna wa muluku , ahana ohawa n ukhottiwa mpakha wiviwa . tivó vapajenryawe olaleya ohawa wawe .
mutthu ontthuna , ntoko satthunawe yesu , opaka nloko nisyá ninlipana n ophenta onlvaha ni onrumela , ohana wikhotta mwanene , ohiphavela mihakhu sinvikana s akhw awe , ohiya oruma , olikanela othanyiwa n ale amphavela sawayaru pahi .
nloko nisyá n axinna , eyo t iyo , omwene wa muluku ti wawaya ale anlikanela ophenta yivahereryaka mmansaya wira yarumeleke akhw aya mpakha wakhwela .
ovekela
apwiya ti makampusi aka , khivo enikihalela .
annikiviriha iphiro soloka mwaha wa nsina naya .
kaviraka mwepiphini mowopiha , nkinova etthu yotakhala , mana nyuwo , apwiya , munkhala ni miyo . nyuwo munnikisuka , munnikilipiherya murima .
ovanela ni olehana
khula mutthu upuweleke mmurimani mwawe ni othene ehimeryaneke supuwenlyaya . yesu ahakoha awixutti awe wira : nyuwo , munihimya wira miyo ti pani ? olelo onimukoha khula mutthu mwa hiyo : miyo ka pan inyu ? munnamini wira ki mpatthan inyu , kinophentani ? munnitthuna okitthara mpakha okhomeliwa vamwikimanyo ?
exeni yesu àkhottihenryawe awixutti omulela mutthu sa yowo ? pedru n akhw awe yanimusuwela yesu apaka mitikiniho , nlelo yari ehinatthi omusuwela yesu okhomeliwe vamwikimanyo . yanimulipelela mòpoli òweryexa . mankhi hiyo mòpoli xeni oninwehereryahu ?
khula mutthu aikoheke murim awe : kinivilela sai sohawa wira kimutthareke yesu ? .
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
yesu ònihimerya wira : akhalá mutthu ontthuna okitthara , aikhotte mwanene , akapatteke mwikimanyo awe , akitthareke .
mwalapwa òvara onsuwanyeya mirala !
makhalelo ahu
ehapari yorera
yesu ahikela mukalawani , awixutti awe yahimutthara . nananoru , ahikhumelela mwanamukhaya mphareya , mpakha mawimpi enahala osamiha ekalawa . vano yesu ira arupaka .
awixutti awe yahisuserya varupawe , yahinvenxa , khumuhimerya wira : pwiya , munòpole !
yesu ahiwakhula wira : munòveia-ní , wamini wanyu ori vakhanene ?
vano , ahemela , ahipwapwela n ikuru epheyo ni màsi , khukhumelela omàleleya wulupale . alopwan ale yahitikinihiwa vanjene , khwira :
mano , mutth ula ti pani hatá epheyo n iphareya sinimwiwelela yola ?
murima wa katekese
mawimpi emorelaka mukalawani , yesu ira arupaka . awixutti esareiyene wova , yahinvenxa .
yesu pwiya ni mwanene itthu sothene , ahimàliha epheyo , numalá ahakoha awixutti awe iraka : munòvela-ní nyuwo munikirela miyo mòpoli ni miyo kikhalaka va ni nyuwo ?
hatá arupaka walá akhwaka vamwikimanyo yesu onninòpola .
hiyo , ntoko awixutti awo , nopacerya omwamini yesu àvoniha aretta , apuhuwiha iphau. alavula ni malikanyiho , amàliha epheyo ni ephareya . vano yesu onninihimerya wira nimwaminiki yowo pahi okhwiye ni ohihimuwale .
simoni pedru ahimwakhula wira : pwiya , nintthuna omutthara pani ? marina molumo anivaha ekumi yohimala , ti nyuwo . vano hiyo nihamini , nosuwela wira nyuwo mwá kristu , orummwe ni muluku .
ovekela
apwiya !
kinnimàliha murim aka , kinnitthyaliha , ntoko mwanamwane ovonne mmutheteni mw ame awe .
ovanela ni olehana
muluku ti ekekhai khanvonya ni khaninthepya . hiyo ninnikupali wira ontthuna onòpola hatá sinikhumelelaka itthu sinnòpopiha ?
nòpopihiwaka mreke exeni wira nihòveké ?
nettelaka okristu ahu mwaha wo wova , ninnettihiwa n iroho yowarya ?
nisukeke mmurima ni mwahu
yesu ti muluku onkhala ni hiyo khula okathi ni onnihimerya wira : muhòveke .
mutthu khanira : kètte nani ? muluku ari-vo !
makhalelo ahu
antónio ni veronika akristu òthelana mukereja . vano mwan aya awereiwa vanjene . amama verónika yahilavula wira : nimukuxe mwan ola , nimurohe oxipiritali . vano apipi aya yahihimya wira : nàxerye ehako .
averónika yahikhotta , khurowa wavekela amama akristu akhw aya wira : kakhaliheriwe . yahimukuxa mwan owo , enamuroha oxipiritali .
mwan owo ahikhala mahiku vakhani , khuvona . vano amusi yahitteliwa murima. okhala wira yahimona mwan ole avonne .
ehapari yorera
yesu ahilapuwa-tho ephareya , khuphiya okhopela . muttitthi w atthu wahimuthukumanela weiwo : owo ari ophareya .
vano ahiphiya mukhulupale mmosa a empa y othukumana , ihaniwa jairo . amonakaru yesu , ahikokhora oholo wawe , khunvekela amuthipelelaka wira : kihovarani metto , mwan aka mwamuthiyana ohanle okhwa . murwé mmwixatherye matat anyu , wira avone , akhale mukumi .
yesu ahirowa ni yowo . atthu yamutthara khiyàrere , enamphunya vanjene .
mw atthu awo ahikhala muthiyana mmosá , amanle iyakha mulokó ni pili ephom awe ehononeyaka . owo ahaphwanya akulukhana anjene , ahononaka muhakhu wothene warinawe . akulukhana yahimuhaxa vanjene , vano , khaphwanyale okumi , masi yanvira atepaka .
vano awixutti awe yahimuhimerya wira : nyuwo munnona wira muttitthi ula annophunyani , munnikoha sai wira : okikwannyale tani ?
masi yesu ahiwehaweha okherekhere , wira amone irale eyo . muthiyan owo anthukumela ni wova , okhala wira ansuwela samukhumelenle . vano , ahirwa , ahlrihela vamettoni va yesu , khumwalikelela ekekhai yothene . vano yesu ahimuhimerya wira :
mwan aka , wamini wanyu wowopolani . muroke ni murettele , mukhaleke mukumi .
nlelo alavulaka siso , yahiphiya atthu ekhumaka owannyawe jairo , khwira : mwan inyu ohòkhwa . munimukhulela-ni-tho mwixuttihi ula ?
nto yesu khajanle molumo ala , khumwirela jairo : muhòvé . mwamini pahi .
vano khatthunne oholiwa n atthu akina , ahikhanle pedru ni yakobo ni yohani , munn awe yakobo . vaphiyalyaya owannyawe mukhulupale owo , yahaphwanya atthu yanyakulasa , ekhuwelaka , yinlasaka valupale . yesu ahikela mpani , khwahimerya atthu ale wira : munnyakulela-ni ? muninlela-ni ? mwanamwane owo khakhwiye : onorupa .
nto atthu ale yahimutheyasa . yesu ahiwòmola othene , aharowana atithi awe n amam awe mwan ole , n ale yarinawe ararú , khukela mpani-mmwe mwari mwanamwane . yesu ahinvara ntata khwira : talithá kùm ! eyo enihimya wira : mwanamwane , kiniwirelani ti mi , nvenyé !
mwarusi uwo ahivenya nananoru , khupacerya wetta : arina iyakha mulokó ni pili . atthu yahituthuwa , khutikinihiwa vanjene . yesu ahalopola n ikuru wira ehimulèle mutthu etthu ila , khwaruma onvaha yolya mwanamwane owo .
murima wa katekese
omwamini yesu onnixintta mixankiho sahu .
molumo ala annithonyerya murerelo mulupale wo wamini , oniwerya owòpola atthu hatá mokhwani .
omwamini yesu onlikana ni omukwannya yowo . muthiyan owo ahimukwannya yesu. mana animwamini yowo .
attharaka solimalela s ephattu y ayuda , muthiyan owo ari ni mwikho mwaha w erett awe eyo , yamurava-tho mwikho atthu yakwannyawe . tivó vuliwawe muru ni wova , khuphiya ottuli wa yesu pahi .
yesu khonve wanyiheriwa oravihiwa mwikho ni muthiyan owo , nto ahimphavela. khumuttottopela iraka : mwan aka , wamini wanyu wowopolani .
omwamini yesu okhala ntoko muthiyan owo omukwannyale , axinttaka solimalela sa mwikho ni ahòvaka woneliwa ni muttitthi w atthu . omwamini yesu omuroromela hatá okathi ohimphwanela ororomela .
ti siso siralyawe jairo , òmwamini yesu hatá ahimeriwaka wira , mwan inyu ohòkhwa .
ovekela
apwiya yesu !
miyo kinnamini. mukikhaliherye , nto wamini waka orokhala vakhani .
ovanela ni olehana
muthiyan owo , amukwannyale yesu , ahixintta itthu sinjene samukhottiherya omwattamela yesu . hiyo tisivi mikhottiheryo sinxinttahu wira nimwamini yesu , nimutthareke ?
muthiyan owo ahipacerya wiwa sa yesu , ahimwamini , ahirowa omukwannya . wiwa sa yesu , omwamini , omutthara ni watàna ni yowo ti ephiro enttharahu hiyo ?
muhòvé . mwamini pahi . ninnamini wira nakhwa. ninrowa okhala vamosá ni yesu mahiku othene ? walá nnimutheya yesu ntoko siralyaya atthu ale ?
nawereiwaka nimmutthyawelela yesu nimuroromelaka ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
yesu òhimya wira : miyo ki ohihimuwa ni ki ekumi . ole onikamini miyo , hatá anakhwaru , onokhala-tho mukumi .
vano ole onetta ekumi , onikamini miyo , khankhwa-tho .
mutthu khankhwa ntoko mutathi wa nakhuwo ; onkhwa ntoko mutathi wa mele !
alaleyi omwene wa muluku
hiyo nihaneliwa opacerya mulaponi mu omwene wa muluku walaleiwe ni yesu : watàniha maloko othene wira ekhale omusi omosá w axinna .
omusi musyá w axinna , alopwana n athiyana , ti ovalui wa muluku . yesu onnikawana n awo ekumi awe ya mwana a muluku ni onnaruma olaleya wira : omwene wa muluku ori vakhiviru wanyu .
mwixutti a yesu onniphavelexa omwene wa muluku ovikana ekumi awe . waphwanya axinna t otteliwa murima vanjene , tivó yesu onnitthapa alyaka vamosá n anatampi erukununxene murim aya .
nira nlo nahatikiniha ni nahiwumiha owanonimafarisi n awixuttihi a ikano yakhotta omwamini yesu , nto nonisuweliha muluku èkekhai .
makhalelo ahu
mulaponi mu mmiravo aphavelaka owixutta okalapintero ohana ovara muteko vanjene wira amukhaliherye mwixuttihi awe mwa miteko sothene , hatá sihikhanle ekalapintero . simalaka iyakha sikina , aixuttalene ovara muteko , onimuliva mwixuttihi awe , khumulaihaka wira apajeryeke ovara muteko mekhawe vaté vawe .
ehapari yorera
murima wa katekese
yesu onninitthana ni onninruma oteka maloko òwiwanana .
okathi wa yesu , amiravo akina wira ekhale awixuttihi a ikano yanrowa omusoma biblia vaté vawe mwixuttihi mulupale , envarelaka miteko sarumawe wira awixuttihe otaphulela ikano sa moise . siviraka iyakha sikina sowixutta , yanikhalihiwa awixuttihi a ikano .
yesu ti mwixuttihi àkhweli , nto khawihanne awixutti wira àsomihe ikano sa moise envarelaka miteko sawe .
yesu ahiwihana awixutti awe wira yetteke ni yowo ekumi aya yothene ewanaka ni sotakhala ni elaleyaka omwene wa muluku .
yesu òrummwa n atithi , yowo-tho aharuma atthu ni onnaruma-tho othene animwamini wira vamosá ni yowo , evareke muteko mulupale atithi wanvahalyaya . mutek owo ti wathukumanya atthu wira ekhale nloko ni omusi . tivo vanarumawe orowa anli-ànli .
olaleya omwene wa muluku ti wowakuveya , okhala wira ilapo sothene siri ntoko ematta yulupale memmo muttokontthe yolya yolikana ohempwa . atthu othene mmurimani mwaya anniphavela exariya , murettele ni ophenta , annilikana wiwa ehapari yorera . ti wokhweleya olaleya murettele onkhuma wa muluku , tithi àtthu othene , onimuruma mwan awe òpacerya waphavela anawe akina othene .
awixutti annilaleya orwa wa mwan owo a muluku ni mulupale àtthu othene . ti yowo onrwa wavaha atthu nlevelelo ni watàna , okhala wira yari ethanyanaka mukina ni mukhw awe mwaha wa itampi .
evekelaka opuro vatthokoni vamphiyaya , annavaha murettele axinene anakhelela ni siso t ampaceryaya omusi w akristu . vavo atthu vamphentanaya ntoko axinna . atithi aya ari vo . ole oniwakhelani nyuwo , onikakhela miyo : vano yowo onikakhela miyo , onimwakhela ole okirumme .
ovekela
muluku tith ihu !
nyuwo ti mwanene ilapo sothene .
mwanjererye alaleyi a masu anyu , wira atthu othene yiwelelaka masu awo , yatàneke ni murettele momweneni mwanyu .
ovanela ni olehana
antthuna onvekela sai ole ahinimwaminaya ? antthima omwamini sai , ehilalèriwe ? vano , antthuna olalèriwa sai , ehikhanle atthu òwalalèrya ? t ani ontthuna olaleya , ahirivo orummwe ?
yesu khawíhanne arummwa mulokó nanli pahi , nnaḱhala khàrumme awo pahi , nto ahathanla awixutti akina miloko mithanu na mili n atthu anli , wira anithonyerye hiyo othene nimmutthara , muteko ontthunahu wavarela axinna ahinatthi omusuwela . nnira exeni wira nilaleye ehapari yorera ?
yesu ahiwihana-tho athiyana okhala awixutti awe , hatá okathi yole athiyana yahalimalelaya okhala ni olavula vathukumanaya alopwana . ililamelo xeni sinakhottiherya athiyana ovara miteko sa mettelo a elapo ahu ?
athiyana annikawana n alopwana mwettiheryo wa ikomunidade ni miteko sikina sa nloko n akristu ?
axitithi annetetela wira an aya axithiyana esomeke oxikhola ntoko siniwirelaya an aya axilopwana ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
solya khasirere mmatta : vano alipa-òhepha ari vakhani .
nanso munvekeleke mwanene ematta , wira àrumihele anamuteko mmatta mwawe .
warya wa nsuwa onnimwalèla elapo yothene , okhumaka nipuro nimosá !
makhalelo ahu
ehapari yorera
ale miloko mithanu na mili n anli yahihokolowa n utteliwa murima , ehimyaka wira : pwiya , hatá malaikha òtakhala annimwelela mwa nsina nanyu !
yesu ahahimerya wira : miyo komona satana amoraka wirimu ntoko overunya . mwiwé : kihovahani owerya w onyakatta inowa n iyalala , kihovahani owerya w opwetexa ikuru sa satana : khivo eniwerya owirihani yotakhala . vano , muhitteliwé murima mwaha wo wiweleliwa ni malaikha òtakhala : mutteliweke murima , okhala wira masin anyu àlempwa wirimu .
okathi ene yowo , yesu ahitteliwa murima mw eroho yowarya , khwira : miyo kinottottopelani nyuwo tithi , mwanene wirimu ni vathí , okhala wira muhakhuwa itthu iya atthu òsuwela n a miruku , khwasuweliha axikhani . ayo , tithi ! tthiri ti siso sitthunnyanyu n urera wanyu murima . itthu sothene kivahiwe n atithi .
khavo onimusuwela mwana , ehikhanle atithi : khavo onasuwela atithi , ahikhanle mwana , n ale mwana ontthunawe wasuweliha .
vano yesu , arukunuwelaka awixutti awe , ahiwitiherya iraka : àreriwa maitho anona itthu sinònanyu . kinolèlani ti miyo , wira : maprofeta ni mamwene manjene yahiphavela wona itthu sinònanyu , khuhona ; yahiphavela wiwa itthu sinlwanyu , khuhìwa .
murima wa katekese
otteliwa wahu murima okhala àna a muluku .
awixutti yahitthika etteliwaka murima vanjene , nave yesu ahitteliwa murima , khwattottopela atithi okhala wira ahavaha atthu axikhani ankhili wira esuweleke mirirya s omwene wa muluku .
ninnitteliwa murima nikhalaka ni murettele , natànaka ni muluku tith ihu n axinn ihu othene .
satana owo , yesu omonalyawe amoraka wirimu , t itthu sothene n atthu othene anavalanya atthu , enamwalanasa ni muluku n akhw aya . awixutti yarummwe ni yesu wavaha atthu murettele , yahimomola satana owo , mwlnanihi oniruha ekhotto .
yesu khanniruma wira naruhele atthu anjene mukomunidadeni mwahu wira ebatiziwe , nto onninruma walalòrya atthu othene ophenta omosaru ni ohina mukano wa muluku . muluku khamurumme mwan awe mulaponi wira àhukhumu atthu : òmurumme wira atthu yopoliwe ni yowo .
mwirirya mulupale ontthunahu osuwela hiyo akristu , n atthu othene , amaka n ale a idini sikina , t ula : muluku onnaphenta atthu othene ntoko an awe . vano ophenta nno ti yesu pahi onwerya wasuweliha atthu , mana owo ti mwana olenve ekumi awe wira aphente othene .
wamini wira muluku tith ihu , ophwanya ephattu y ekumi ahu ni osuwela makhalelo ahu . mutthu ohinsuwela wira muluku onimphenta ntoko mwan awe , khansuwela vankhumawe , exeni enkhalelawe vathi-va ni vammalelawe . ori ntoko mutthu ohinsuwela nloko nawe .
naminiki wira muluku tith ihu , ninnimusuwela-tho wira khula mutthu ti mwan awe ontthunahu omphenta ni omuttittimiha .
ovekela
miyo kinottottopelani nyuwo tithi ,
mwanene wirimu ni vathi , okhala wira muhakhuwa itthu iya atthu òsuwela ni a miruku , khwasuweliha axikhani .
ayo , tithi , ti siso sitthunnyanyu n urera wanyu murima .
ovanela ni olehana
ti sivi itthu sinnitteliha murima ?
ninnitteliwa murima okhala wira eroho yowarya enikhala mmurimani mwahu ?
nniwakhela sai atthu anvekela okela mukomunidadeni mwahu ?
ninnittittimiha osuwela w atthu axikhani ?
ninnimutthuniherya khula mutthu wira ahimyeke omwamini wawe ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
yesu ti mwana onnisuweliha atithi .
mwamuthupi khanrummwa wipa , onona mmansawe !
makhalelo ahu
mukristu mmosá , nsina nawe silvio , ohana ematt awe ya mihali . imara pili ahĩyeriwa mihali sawe . ekwaha yanenli yarwiyawe nawí ye , sílvio vamosá n amwar awe elivira n akristu othene yari okapela evarasaka muteko wo wupa ixixolo wira yinjereryeke ekapel eyo . nawiye khaphiye omihalini pahi , ahirowa-tho owannyawe silvio , khumwiyerya iparatho .
sílvio khamakenle omàla pahi , vano ahupuwela orowa omphavela mukhulukana wira avirele ematta vamosá ni vate vawe wira nawiye akhwé .
esumana eyo , muhim awe silvio , ori mmaka . silvio ahimuxekurya , khumuhimerya wira : mwakhala wira mophiya ematta yovireliwa , mukihimerye orattene wira kiwerye wotaphulani . jorje ahimwakhula wira , miyo nkiphiye mmatta mwanyu .
vathukumanalyaya , mwalimo ahahimerya amaka n akristu wira elevelelaneke .
muluku pahi t onimulamula khula mutthu .
ehapari yorera
alipa-òliviha mpósito othene n anatampi yanimwattamela yesu wira emwiwe . vano afarisi n awixuttihi a ikano yanimwàpa , ehimyaka wira : ola onlimalelana n anatampi , khiyalya ni yawo !
