vano yesu ahahimerya nlikanyiho nla , ìraka : t ani a nyuwo , akhalaná ipwittipwitthi sawe miloko mulokó , yamurimela emosá , ahinahiya iye sikina miloko mithanu na mixexe ni thanu na xexe mothakoni , arowaka ophavela ele emurimenle , mpakha ophwanya ? aphwanyá vale , onnitteliwa murima , khukapatta epwittipwitth iyo mmakhatani . aphiyakaru owani , onnathukumanya apatthani awe n anamwattamanani awe , anahimerya wira : mutteliweke murima vamosá ni miyo ! kophwanya epwittipwitthi aka yakirimenle .
siso , miyo kinolèlani wira : wirimu onotthapeliwa volikana natampi mmosá onttharuwa sottheka sawe , vowavikana atthu miloko mithanu na mixexe n athanu n axexe àxariya , ahimphwanelela orukunuxa murima .
nkhi muthiyana xeni onlra akhalanne ilívura sawe mulokó , yamurimela emosá , ahinapattiha muthuko , ahinavela mpani , khuhiphavela orattene , mpakha ophwanya ? aphwanyá vale , onnathukumanya apatthani awe n anamwattamanani awe , anahimerya wira : mutteliweke murima vamosá ni miyo : kophwanya musurukhu aka wakirimenle . siso , kinohimeryani wira : malaikha a muluku anotthapa volikana mwaha wa natampi mmosá onrukunuxa murima .
murima wa katekese
yesu ti makampusi òrera murima onaphavela ale antthara iphiro sothweleliha .
awixutti yahirummwa ni yesu wahimerya atthu wira : omwene wa muluku ori vakhiviru vanyu ! yahihokolowa n utteliwa murima okhala wira hatá malaikha ònanara yaniwiwelela . nto entthuna wakhumelela exeni ale yakhontte wiwa ? onokhottani , onikikhotta miyo . vano , ole onkikhotta miyo , oni mukhotta ole okirumme .
yesu ti naxariya mmosarú ni makampusi òrera murima , ohipaka mwapwittipwitthi orimenle n uhitiwe wira anòpole .
yesu onnimulikanyiha-tho muluku ni muthiyana òthoiwa . musurukhu omphwanyawe ni muteko awe , ti wokhweleya . hatá elivura emosá pahi yamurimela , onona ntoko etthu yulupale emurimenle tivó khammumula mpakha ophwanya .
muluku kharina an awe wira àrihele ota . muluku onnimulemeliha vanjene khula mutthu amphwanelihaka vamaithoni vawe , muluku khanwerya omuliyala nnákhala mmosán awe , alopwana walá athiyana , hatá yamutthekenle vanjene . muthiyana ommwamwiha mwan awe onowerya omuliyala ? walá onowerya oliyala ommorela ikharari yowo ori ephome awe ? vano , onamwi owo amuliyalaka mwan awe , miyo nkinoliyalani , nnákhala vakhani .
ovekela
apwiya , muluku aka , miyo kinnetta pure ntoko epuri erimenle : mukirwele miyo , murumeyi anyu , okhala wira nkiliyanle ikano sanyu .
ovanela ni olehana
omusuwela wahu muluku onilikana n osuwela w afarisi ? walá onnivirikana ?
yesu okhwenle wasuweliha atthu wira muluku èkekhai onaphenta anaxariya n anatampi . exeni ?
ekomunidade ahu y akristu ennilipa ni yesu , yowo oniwakhelela anatampi khíyalya ni yawo walá ennilipa n ikano ?
okhala wira nri ekomunidade enlipa n othunku nimphuka sai milattu sinkhuma eriyar ihu ? ninnimukumiha mukhw ihu vamutekoni , ninnimomola mukomunidadeni ? wira siso vannirerela ?
mutteliweke murima vamosá ni miyo ! nnakhulela sai molumo ala mmakhaleloni mwahu , nosareya otteliwa murima mwaha wa ikharari tithi sinnimorelawe khula okathi ?
yesu t ukhanle òwisetta , khonve olavula ekekhai , khatthyanwe warumela atthu . khaphavenle ottottopeliwa n atokwene èdini , nnákhala n ale èlapo .
khonve onyoholiwa mwettelo awe ovirikanaka n ule w atthu akina alupale . khaphavenle winnuwihiwa vamaithoni v atthu . khàthokorenrye atthu yamwapa , nnákhala makhulupale yamwanyiherya okhala òhiwelela . khikasompe wira ahapajeke makhulupale àhimeryaka ekekhai yaviruxa .
muluku òmuhihimuxa yesu , ekumi yoxintta okhwa . yesu t opacerya , onniniholela . yowo t ephiro aim ennipixa mwekumini .
makhalelo ahu
ilapo sikina àkhala mapuro malupale anlompiwa mukhalelo w ephattu , awo anniholeliwa ni mutthu mmosá onihaniwa xarifu n atthu akinaku animukhaliherya , alopwana n athiyana .
mmaxilopiwani mmo annirwa atthu anjene ekhumaka ilapo sikinaku , erwelaka olompa , okoha maxankiho aya monkoni mw ehako , olòliwa , omutaphula natiri ammanalyaya mukwaha mukina , yarwaka anniruha otthu , ilyakhu , musoro , ipuri .
vano ansiau , muholi àkristu awo yakhontte , ahihaxiwa vanjene ni mwené vamosá n atthu yavaranawe muteko , mwené owo ahira siso mana atthokelela wira ansiau uwo n akristu akhw awe n ukhotta waya warowa wasuweliha atthu itthu iye sinireya nipuro nlo s olavilavi ni sowiyerya . vano atthu khiyàrowa-tho olompa nipuro nlo . vireyaka siso warowa omalamala muteko walipanawe xarifu vamosá n akhw awe ni mwené aya .
ehapari yorera
yesu n awixutti awe , yattamelaka oyerusalemu , yahiphiya obetifage , vakhiviru ni mwako olivera . yesu aharuma awixutti anli , awirelaka : murowé muttetthe ori oholo iwe . mphiyakaru-wo , munomphwanya buru mwamuthiyana atthukeleliwene : ori ni mwaxan awe . mwamutaphule , mukiruhele va . akhalá onokohani etthu , mmwakhule wira : apwiya t anaphavela , animwahokoloxa nanano .
vahìraneya siso wira emalelihiwe yahimyalyawe profeta wira : mulalèrye muttetthe w oyerusalemu wira : mone : mwené anyu onrwa wa nyuwo . owo t owlyeviha , onrwa amukilathenlene buru ni mwaxana a buru ontexa miritti .
yesu akelaka oyerusalemu , atthu othene a mmuttettheni yahekeseya , yanikohana wira : ti pani ula ?
muttitthi w atthu wanakhula wira : ola ti profeta yesu , onkhuma onazarethi w ogalileya .
vottharelana , yesu ahikela mpani mwa muluku . ahiwomola-mo atthu yatumiha ni yathuma mpani memmo . ahipittula mesa àlipa-òwakakhanya musurukhu ni minyukhu s ale yatumiha ipomba , khwahimerya wira : volempwa wira : emp aka yihaniweke empa y olompa . nto nyuwo mokhaliha nikhuku n anawlye .
alipa-òhona n alipa-orakala yahimwattamela yesu mpani mwa muluku , van owo ahavoniha . axinamwane yanikhuwela mpani mwa muluku yiraka : avuwihiwe mwana a davidi ! alupale ànamukuttho n awixuttihi a ikano , vònalyaya sotikiniha siralyawe yesu , vawiwalyaya axinamwane ale , yahinanariwa vanjene , khumwirela yesu : munniwa sinihimyaya ala ?
owo ahiwakhula wira : kinniwa , ayo ! khamunasome silempwaya wira : ni masu ànamwane , ale anetta n ale a mmatatani , muhilikanyiherya ovuwa ?
vahimyalyawe siso , ahahiya , khuvenya mmuttettheni mme , arowaka obethania , khuviriha weiwo ohiy ule .
murima wa katekese
yesu ti empa esyá ya muluku eriyari ahu .
yesu vaphiyalyawe oyerusalemu nira na pásikha nari vakhiviru . atthu anjene òrera murima yahirwa oyerusalemu wira etaphuliwe mikho saya .
omwene yesu orwenlyawe opacerya vathí-va , onònihereya hiyo nirumelanaka mukina ni mukhw awe . mureyaneke miritti mukina ni mukhw awe : siso munomaliherya ikanó sa kristu .
yesu anisuwela wira makhulupale ànamukuttho yarowa onanariwa mwaha w owomola anamarotta mpani mwa muluku , nto yesu ahonela orera wiriha siso , mana ahiyale marotfawo , wari okhaliherya edini yohononiwa . yesu , mahiku othene , ahilaleya wira muluku onsiveliwa omoriwa ikharari , nto khamphavela mikuttho .
yesu vawomolalyawe anamarotta , alipa-òhona n alipa-òrakala , yanyiheriwa okhala ni mwikho ekhottiheriwaka okela mpani mwa muluku , vano yahiwerya okela ni yesu khwavoniha .
yesu ahimaliha enamuna atthu yupuwelaya wira empa ya muluku yari oyerusalemu pahi .
yesu yowo ti muluku onkhala vamosá n atthu : ale animwamini yesu ari empa ya muluku .
ovekela
apwiya , munivahe eparakha yo wokokhorelani nettihiwaka n eroho y ekekhai , okathi t okathi ni mapuro othene .
ovanela ni olehana
ànamukuttho n anamarotta yaniphwanya mihakhu mwaha wa mikuttho atthu sahelaya .
okhala wira mwana a muluku ohipaka mutthu ntoko hiyo , empa ya muluku eri vai ?
oraruwa , onamittompe , ohapaliwa , esuruma .
ikapela sahu ti sowi sai ? ninttittimiha sai ? ninniphavela wira sikhaleke vorera yotekiwa sana n ijanela wira mukokoleke mpani mmo ? atthu annòna wira eyo empa y atithi ni annirwa okapela ni murettele etteliwaka murima ?
ninnittittimiha ipa sahu ntoko ikereja sa vatthokoni , vavo vankhalawe muluku ?
yesu ansuwela wira makhulupale yaniphavela omwiva . nto yesu t ówisetta , t owimaliha khònve sahimyaya ni siraya atthu akina , okhala wira yesu ori mophentani mw atithi awe amurumme . vano hiyo nintthuna okhala sai ntoko atthu òwisetta nixinttaka wova ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
akhalá mutthu onkiphenta , onimwettela molumo aka , atithi anomphenta yowo . hiyo nnimorwa wa yowo wira nikhaleke mwa yowo .
makhalelo ahu
ehapari yorera
yahanle mahiku manli ophiya nira na pásikha ni na iphau sohiheliwa miropo . alupale ànamukuttho n awixuttihi a ikano yaniphavela enamuna y onvara yesu mwitiho , wira emwive . tthiri yanihimeryana wira : nihinvaré nihiku na nira , wira ohikhumelelé onyakulihana w atthu .
vano yuda isikaryoti , mmosá àle mulokó nanli , ahirowa w alupale ànamukuttho , wira àvahererye yesu . awo vamwiwalyaya , yahitteliwa murima , khumuhimerya wira anonvaha musurukhu . vano yuda aniphavela okathi wokhweya , wira anvarihe yesu .
murima wa katekese
wamini mwirirya w okhwa ni w ohihimuwa wa yesu mòpoli ahu .
katekese ovinre nihiwa wira yesu aphiyakaru oyerusalemu , yahihala mahiku vakhani ophiya nira na pásikha . yesu ahakheleliwa ni muttitthi w atthu anjene òrera murima , yamuroromela wira arwa owòpòla mihawelo sinjene sohixariya ni sopuheriwa .
atthu awo yamutthapela yesu oyerusalemu , yahitaphuwa tthiri walá yahona wòtothiwa ? hiyo nnimutthara yesu . ninnisona otaphuwa ?
ehapari yorera yiwalyahu ya muthiyana itthenle makhura vamuru wa yesu , ennikhaliherya wira nisuweleke mwirirya w okhwa wa yesu mòpoli , onnikhaliha atthu òtaphuwa .
ayuda yahilimalela wòttiha makhura muruttu ohinatthi ovitha . akhalá onkivaha esanta wira kivithaniwe , nlelo kinari mukumi , kinnòna wira owo onnikiveha . vovirikana yesu ahikupali n utteliwa murima , ninlelo ahimyaka-tho wira ehapari yorera entthunawe olaleya , entthuna olikana ni makhur awo yittheliwe vamuru vawe ni muthiyan owo .
wiviwa wa yesu ontthuna olikana opwexa murinki , ephome awe yomwarexiwe entthuna olikana ni makhura òwunkhela wira atthu othene yakhele ekumi esyá .
awanani a yesu yaniphavela enamuna y onvara wira emwive . awixutti awe yahilavula wira makhura etumihiwe wira yinjereryeke musurukhu ; mmosá a yawo , yuda , àlikanana onvahererya yesu awanani awe .
ovekela
xontte pwiya yesu !
munisuwelihe winnuwa w ophenta wanyu , ohina mukano , weiwo ohowerihaleni wivahererya owòpola atthu othene .
ovanela ni olehana
yesu àtthyawenle ottaiwene w ale yatthuna omwiva amòniherya okhala mutthu òwisetta ?
yesu ahalaka owerya ovilela ohawa n ukhwa , murim awe walipanne exeni ? hiyo nnakhelela sai mihawelo ?
miruku s athiyana sinnikupaliwa , sinòneliwa vatthu ? walá alopwana pahi t asuweli ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
ehapari yorera ya yesu ti wunkhela omwarexeliwe mulaponi mothene . murowé , mwawixuttiheke atthu a maloko othene , mwabatizaka ni nsina n atithi ni na mwana ni na eroho yowarya .
muthiyana namirukú , khanaminiwa nananoru !
makhalelo ahu
atthu anetta ekwaha yokhuma wamphula orowa onakhala , eviraka omonapo. muttetthe w omweravale anniphwanya ekereja yotekiwa n ixixolo , yotthuneliwa n isinku ni yottelihiwa . epantte eniweha nivá kulo , mukhora khuvo , masi sihavo mikimanyo mili sulupale muxirini okhala wira ekerej eyo etekeliwe wira yupuweleliweke mamisionário manli akhwiye vavale okathi w ekhotto .
mahiku yettaka mararu mweri wopacerya w eyakha 1985 , ohiviwa irmã teresa , ari namasomiha èxikhola yulupale y onattetthe . nihiku nenlo yahivakasiwa-tho atthu akina anjene .
mulupal ihu alfredo ahisoma iyakha sinjene wira akhalé mukhulukana , ahirwa elapo ela wira aloleke aretta . masi ohokhwa vohipisa , sothene sarinawe n usuwela wawe solakaseya . nireke wira muluku oromuthanya n usuwela warinawe wira iviwe ?
akristu òmweravale ahakhulasa wira : nná ri ! khathanyiwe ni muluku . hiyo ninnamini wira ephome y atthu othene emwarexeliwe nipuro nla , enniphwanelela vamaithoni va muluku . tivó vathukumanalyaya othene vamosá , khupuwela oteka ekereja wira yupuweleke wivakasiwa w axinn ihu ni evekeleleke murettele okathi wothene mulaponi mwahu .
ehapari yorera
vaphiyalyaya okathi , yesu ahikilathi vamesa vamosá n awixutti awe , khwahimerya wira : kaniphavela vanjene olya ni nyuwano nlra nla na pásikha , kihinatthi ohawa . tthiri , kinolèlani ekhweli wira : nkinimulya-tho pásikha , mpakha vanrowawe omalelihiwa momweneni mwa muluku .
vano , ahikuxa ekálisi , ahimuxukhuru muluku , khwira : mukuxeke evinyu ila , mukawaneke . mana kinohimeryani wira , okhuma olelo vava , nkinwurya-tho evinyu mpakha vanrwaya omwene wa muluku , nave ahikuxa ephau , ahimuxukhuru muluku , ahikawanya ephau iyo , khwavaha , ahimyaka wira : ela erutthu aka , evaheriwe nyuwo . mwireke iya , mukupuwelaka miyo .
siso-tho , vamanlyaya olya , ahavaha ekálisi , ahimyaka wira : ekalis ila ti watàna wa nanano , opakiwe n iphome aka , yela emwarexeliwe nyuwo . vano-nto , musuwele wira ole onrowa okivahererya ori ni miyo vamesa . vekekhai , mwana a mutthu onrowa okhwa , ntoko silempwaya sa yowo : masi òtakhaliwa mutth ule onrowa onvahererya mwana a mutthu !
vano , awixutti yahikelela okohana , ephavelaka omusuwela t ani a yawo arowa wira etthu ene yeyo .
murima wa katekese
okristu okhala mophentani warumelaka atthu ntoko siralyawe yesu .
okhuma opajenryahu omuthukumanela katekese , nihòna wira mmurimani mwaya amakhuwa othene anniphavela vanjene watàna n akhw aya ni okhala ni murettele . tivó amuhakhala ihu epakaka nira n omusi aya yanalattula atthu a maloko makina . nira nanitepa otteliha murima ephiyaka atthu yahawehereriwa .
ephau n ivinyu sikaweliwe atthu , t ithonyeryo sa yesu onvaha erutlhu n iphome awe ni onivahererya wira atthu othene ekhaleke amusi , yatàneke mophentani mw atithi amosarú .
okathi onlompahu okaristiya niwaka molumo a yesu : kuxakani , mulyeke othene : ela ti erutthu aka , ninnamini wira yesu onnikhala vamosá ni hiyo ni onninivahererya ekumi awe wira nihiyeke milili , navahereryeke akhw ihu ekumi ahu .
khula mmosa ivahereryaka warumela akhw awe , ninkhala nloko nisyá ni mipantte s erutthu emosarú ya kristu .
ekomunidade emphattuwa mokaristiyani , ti omusi omosá onatànihiwa n iphau emosarú , eri kristu , mukomunidadeni mmo khavo onaruma akhw awe , othene annirumelana .
yesu àkawelaka awixutti awe ephau , ahalalèrya omwene wa muluku . ephau eyo yakaweliwe awixutti , ti ethonyeryo enrowa omusuweliha yesu ohihimuwalene .
ovekela
ole onkhura erutthu aka ni onwurya ephome aka , òkhalana ekumi yohimala : vano miyo kinomuhihimuxa mokhwani nihiku nokiserya .
pwiya , mahiku othene munivaheke ephau ene yeyo !
ovanela ni olehana
amuhakhala ihu anixuttihale sai murerelo w okawelana itthu sarinaya amusi a nihimo nimosá ni wo wakawela-tho amalapo ?
yesu òhimya wira : mwireke iya , mukupuwelaka miyo . nintthariha lini molumo ala a yesu ? vanniphiyerya okhala okathi pahi onlompahu ni onakhelahu okaristiya mukomunidadeni ?
atthu othene animusuwela sai mutthu okhala mukristu walá ohikhala ?
mukomunidadeni mwahu nalaihana muteko , othene ninnòna mmansihu wira nihana okhomalela mutek owo mana othene n amusi ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
okaristiya ti murima wa nloko n akristu , okhala wira mokaristiyani yesu kristu ti mukumi eriyari ahu .
namulya wiphini , ahimukhura wamwe a ekonya , ekhapelelaka hapá !
makhalelo ahu
eyakha 1992 vakenle murettele mulaponi-mu , mittetthe sikinaku sa distrito wakharowa wahipisa wiwanyeya ohimmwa wa murettele wahakalaliha atthu . mamilisa yanithipelela wakhanyereriha athiyana otthupula , oruha màsi n itthu sikinaku sowavarela . yanakhottiherya atthu okhuma mmawani ntoko okathi w ekhotto .
misionário mmosá ahirowa olavula n alupale awo , khwakoha exeni yathipelelaya sothene ntoko okhottoni . awo yahakhulasa wira khiyàwerya wahiya atthu wisetta. nlelo khiyàrummwe ni guvemu a distrito .
vano misioná ri owo ahipacerya wahimerya atthu arunyaka wira : ekhotto yomala ! atthu othene anniwerya ohokolowela vakhalaya khalai . muteko wo warumela mamilisa womala . okhuma okathi yowo atthu yahipacerya okhuma mmawani mmo . mamilisa yahiniwa murima vanjene , khumopopiha misionário owo ehimyaka wira anomwiva vamosá n akristu yarinawe , enahimeryana yaworu yiraka : nrowe , nimwive mukuny ola onihonona elapo ahu .
misionário ahèmela oholo waya àhimeryaka wira : mukiveke ntoko sintthunanyu , miyo kiri va . mamilisa awo yahihokolowela okwaritelo emuruwanaka pahi .
misionário ahivenya mmuttettheni mmo , khurowa , animadore a parókia ni a zona yahihalasa elaleyaka ehal ile ya murettele mittetthe sothene sa localidad ele .
akristu anjene yahirowa waxekurya manimadore , vano mulupale òkhatteya ahathàmiherya manimadore owannyawe , misionário ahirowa orupa weiwo vamosá ni manimadore . orupa oxeleliwa , mulupale owo òkhatteya aharumasa okhuma àhimeryaka nihiku nophukiwa mulattu aya . nihiku nlo yahirowasa manimadore ni misionário n akristu akina , masi anamalepa awo , yawotheryasa manimadore , khiyàrwasiye .
okhuma okathi ole atthu othene t asuwenlyaya wira vekekhai murettele wophiya mulaponi-mu. khula mutthu ohana ohoko lowela owannyawe wa khalai .
ehapari yorera
yesu ahivenya , khurowa omwako olivera , ntoko salimalenlyawe .
awixutti awe yahimutthara . vaphiyalyawe nipuro nlo , ahahimerya wira , mulompeke , wira muhimoré mwehereriwaka .
vano owo ahahiya , khwarakamela vakhani , khuko khora , analompa ahimyaka wira : tithi , mwatthuná , mukak iherye ohawa waka nno . nto , ehireyé ntoko sintthunaka miyo , yireye ntoko sintthunanyu nyuwo .
okathi uwo , nlaikha na wirimu nahimukhumelela wira nimulipihe murima . vano yesu , asareĩyene winiwa murima , ahilipiherya olompa , khuretthela ntoko mattonttoni èphome , enamorela vathí . vamanlyawe olompa , ahivenya , khurowa okumana n awixutti awe : ahaphwanya erupasaka mwaha w oripiw a murima . owo ahakohasa wira : munrupela-ní ? nvenyé , mulompeke wira muhimoré mwehereriwaka .
ninlelo alavulaka siso , wahiphiya muttitthi w atthu . mmosá awixutti mulokó nanli , yowo ihaniwa yuda , anahola atthu awo . owo ahimwattamela yesu , wira anvahe ebejo . nto yesu ahimuhimerya wira : yuda , n ibejo t ininvahereryananyu mwana a mutthu ?
awo yahinvara yesu , yahimukuxa , khumurowa na owannyawe mulupale ànamukuttho . vaxiyaya , makhulupale àyuda , alupale ànamukuttho n awixuttihi a ikano yahithukumana : yahimukeliha yesu oholo waya wira emphuke , khumukohasa wira : mwari mòpoli munlèle .
yesu ahiwakhula wira : miyo kòlèlani , khamunkikup ali ; kòkohani , khamunakhula etthu . nto okhuma olelo , mwaa a mutthu onokilathi mono wolopwana wa muluku òweryexa .
othene aya yahimukohasa wira : weso nyuwo mwá mwana a muluku ?
yesu ahiwakhula wira : ti siso sinhimyanyu .
vano yahìrasa : nnaphavelela-ni-tho anamona ? hiyano mmansihu nomwiwa mwanene !
atthu othene yahivenya , khumuroiha yesu wa pilato . weiwo , yahipacerya omotherya , yiraka : mulopwan ola nimphwannyé àhapuxaka atthu ahu , àkhottiheryaka oliva mpósito wa mwené mulupale òroma , nave-tho ìsiraka mòpoli ni mwené .
pilato ahimukoha yesu wira : nyuwo mwá mwené àyuda ?
yesu ahimwakhula wira : munihimya ti nyuwo !
vano pilato ahahimerya alupale ànamukuttho n atthu othene wira : miyo nkinimphwanyana mulattu mulopwan ola .
masi ale yahithipelela , ehimyaka wira : owo onahapuxa atthu , axuttihaka oyudeya wothene , okhuma ogalileya mpakha nno !
vano pilato , okathi wa pásikha ahana wataphulela otthukweliwa mmosá . nto atthu othene yahikhuwela vamosá , ehimyaka wira : mmwive ola , munitaphulele barabá .
barabá owo àtthukweliwe mwaha w ekhotto yawaniwe mmuttettheni ni mwaha w omwiva mutthu . pilato aniphavela omutaphula yesu tivó , ahilavulana-tho atthu . nto awo yahitepa okhuwela , yiraka : mmukhomele ! mmukhomele vamwikimanyo !
pilato ahakoha-tho ekwaha yaneraru , ahimyaka wira : masi , otthenke-ni yola ? miyo nkimphwanyanne mulattu wophwanela okhwa . tivó , kinoruma omaniwa , numalá kimutaphule .
nto awo yahithipelela okhuwela valupale , evekelaka wira akhomeliwe . onyakula waya wanvira otepaka . vano pilato ahilamula wira yireye yavekelaya : ahimutaphula ole àtthukweliwe mwaha w ekhotto ni wo wiva , yowo yanvekelaya , khwavahererya yesu wira emwirihe yatthunaya .
murima wa katekese
okhala mukristu wamini wira yesu , olamuliwe wiviwa , ti muluku èkekhai .
alupale ànamukuttho , alipa-òwixuttiha ikano , mafarisi yahinanariwa vanjene ni yesu mulattu wa molumo yapwapwelanawe . yanimulupattha yesu mana anahimerya wira yattittimiheke atthu othene ntoko simphwanelyaya ni ekhotteke otokwene waphwanyaya yahaxaka atthu anjene .
nto awo khiyàwenrye onvara yesu yowo mmansawe ahivaherenrye votthuna wawe . yesu aivaherenrye sai wira avariwe ni alamuliwe wiviwa ?
yesu ahotheriwa wira ahapuxa atthu , khunakhottiherya oliva mpósito wa mwené mulupale òroma . yesu ahikumiheriwa-tho mulattu mana ahinveha muluku ahimyaka mmansawe okhala mwana a muluku .
mmakhaleloni mwawe mothene yesu ahilipiha murima akhottaka solimalela savalanya atthu ni sahawonela vatthu athiyana , ana mwane , aretta , amalapo .
yesu ahilipiha-tho murima wavanyiha alupale èlapo ni èdini hatá opòma oyerusalemu : ahavoniha aretta nihiku na sá badu ni ahiwomola alipa-òtumiha mpani mwa muluku .
tthiri yesu ahivariwa , khulamuliwa wiviwa mulattu wa mukhalelo awe : yowo ari vekekhai mutthu aikhalihaka mukhw aya atthu othene , ni ari vekekhai mwana a muluku arummwe n atithi .
hiyo akristu ninnamini ramurimani mwahu , ninnilaleya-tho ni molumo ni miteko wira mutthu ònazarethi , nsina nawe yesu , akhomeliwe vamwikimanyo ni iviwe oyerusalemu , yowo ori vekekhai muluku .
ovekela
mulompeke , wira muhimoré mwehereriwaka . tithi !
mwatthuná , mukakiherye ohawa waka nno .
nto , ehireyé ntoko sintthunaka miyo , yireye ntoko sintthunanyu nyuwo .
ovanela ni olehana
exeni yesu yakupalenlyawe otthukiwa n uhaxiwa ?
ti sivi itthu ayuda samuhimyanalyaya yesu wira emwivihe ?
mahiku ala , ti sivi itthu atthu akina sinihimyanaya ekereja nloko n akristu ?
mahiku ala yesu onilamuliwa-tho saí ? ninnikupali wira hiyo-tho nnimulamula yesu imara sothene sinanyakattahu akhw ihu wira nikhalé alupale ?
nisukeke mmurimani mwahu
kinnimwamini yesu kristu. ahawale momweneni na ponsio pilato , akhomeliwe vamwikimanyo , akhwiye n avithiwe .
ole ohòneliwa vatthu , ahiwopola atthu othene !
watana wakhalai
wopaceryani muluku apattunxe erimu n ilapo ya vathí . elapo yàri mwàri ni khiyàrina etthu . vano eroho ya muluku yettakasa vasulu va màsi .
vano muluku ahira : okhumelele warya . warya khukhumelela . muluku ahòna wira warya wari worera . muluku ahivalanya watana n epiphi , khukhaliha othana n uhiyu . siso nahikhala nihiku nopacerya .
muluku ahira-tho : okhumelele osulu , weiwo okhaleke meku , memmo ekhumeke epula . vano ahivalanya masi osulu ni masi a vathí . khuvaha osulu nsina na erimu . siso nahikhala nihiku nanenli . muluku ahihimya-tho wira : màsi epwexerereye nipuro nimosá , wira nikhumelele nipuro nowuma . nipuro nlo nowuma muluku ahivaha nsina n elapo . vano , othu kumana wa masi ahivaha nsina na ephareya .
muluku ahira : vatthayani simeleke ni sinnuweke mixovo sothene sa malaxi ni sa mirí . vano-nto miri sahiphuwela makukhu makithi n inuku saya vatthayani vothene . muluku ahòna wira erimu n ilapo , ephareya n itthaya yowuma , malaxi ni miri sari sorera . siso nahikhala nihiku naneraru .
muluku ahíra tho : osulu sikhumelele mithuko , wira simwaleleke elapo . nsuwa nimwaleleke othana , vano mweri n itheneri simwaleleke ohiyu . iyo sivirikanyiheke othana n uhiyu , sisuweliheke-tho miyeri n iyakha , sithonyeryeke eyita ni elimwe . muluku ahòna wira sothene iye sari sorera . siso nahikhala nihiku nanexexé .
muluku ahira-tho : mmasini sirelaneke ihopa . musulu sivaveke axinuni . muluku ahipattuxa ihopa n ipalame sa khula muxovo . siso nahikhala nihiku nanethanu .
muhina mwa mahiku mathanu na mosa muluku opattuxa olumwenku ni erimu , elapo ya vathí ni ephareya n itthu sothene sikumi . nihiku nanethanu nenli muluku khumumula . tivó , nihiku nanethanu nenli ti nihiku norerihiwa ni muluku . ti nihiku nowarya w atthu othene .
muluku onakhaliha atthu nipuro norerexa
muluku ahimupa n uloko mutthu opacerya , vano ahimwiselela n iphumu sa ekumi . siso mutthu khukhala mukumi .
numalá muluku ahipaka ematta wedeni , khwala-mo miri sinjene sa mihokorokho sa khula muxovo . sari sorera , vano mihokorokho saya sari sosiva sana . eriyari ya ematta sahikhala mirí mili : mukina w ekumi , mukina w osuweliha oreriwa ni otakhaliwa .
muluku ahimpweha mmatta-mme mutthu ampattunxawe , wira adam uwo alimeke ni akhapeleleke . muluku ahimwirela : nyuwo mulyeke mihokorokho sa miri sothene sa mmatta . masi nkintthuna wira mulye mihokorokho sa mwiri w osuweliha oreriwa ni otakhaliwa . nyuwo mwalyaru , munimokhwa .
atthu khanimwiwelela muluku , anayelela oreriwa
vano muluku ahirela enowa : kinimotakhalihani nyu wo mwaha w etthu yiralyanyu . nyuwo munaipurulaka n erukulu ni munolyaka etthaya . kinimwinanihani nyuwo ni muthiyana , kinimwinaniha nloko nanyu ni nloko na muthiyana : osulu awe onimonyakattani muru , nyuwo mphavelaka omuluma nxitta nawe .
muluku ahimwirela-tho muthiyana wira : nyuwo mu nohawaka mwayaraka an inyu : munimonaka masoso manjene . numalá , muluku ahimwirela mulopwana wira : nyuwo khamwettenle soruma saka : weso etthaya yotakhaliwa mulattu wa nyuwo . munophwanyaka yolya n urettela wa witho wanyu , mpakha nihiku ninrowanyu otthikela mutthayani , okhala wira mupiwe ni etthaya yeyo .
adamu ahavaha amwar awe nsina na hawa , nnihimya wira muthiyana mukumi . owo ti mama atthu othene . muluku omwikara mutthu oparadiso , khumpweha vamukhora mulipa-òlipelela arina ekatana ya moro mmatatani , wira mutthu ahivire arowelaka muhokorokho w ekumi .
kayini ni abeli
kayini ahikhupanyerya ìraka : ehukhumu aka votepa wunnuwa . nyuwo mokikumiha mmatta ni mokbmola vamaithoni vanyu , khukikhaliha namwettakasi ohemeleleva . mutthu ti mutthu onrowa okiphwanya onokiva . masi muluku ahihela ekanyeryo vavuji va kayini , wira ahikhale arowa omwiva .
nowé ni mutaseke
muluku ahòna wira atthu , apattunxawe volikana ni ekhove awe , yahitepeleleya wira itthu sotakhala mulaponi . muluku ahinanariwa , khwira : fatari kahapattunxe . kinorupiha epula va mutaseke , ewivakase atthu othene ni emalamalihe itthu sothene sikumi .
numalá , epula yahikelela ompa mpakha mahiku miloko mixexé , khusamiha elapo vamosa n inama n atthu othene . khavo-tho ahanle onaka . hatá axinuni khiyapluvanya miri s okota-vo . siso sahikhwasa itthu sothene sikumi sari mulaponi . atthu yari mukalawani pahi , eyo p iyo atthu athanu neraru , ti yoponwe , okhala wira ekalawa eyo yaphempa vasulu va màsi .
muluku ahatàna ni yowo vamosa n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; atthu n inama sothene , khwira : watàna nno muhivirikanye . kinnilaphela wira nkihanle orupa epula ya mutaseke , enrowa ohonona ekumi mulaponi . vano ethonyeryo yo walana weiwo ti ekhweli .
makhulupale
muluku onimwitthana abrahamu
sara ira akilanthene mpani . vamwiwalyawe mulopwan owo ahimyaka siso , anitheya upuwelaka mmurima ni mwawe : owo khansuwela iyakha sirinaka . nave-tho abrahamu ohuluvala . masi mulopwan owo ahikoha wira : yokhala muluku enojelawe ? .
wamini w &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; abrahamu
muluku ahimutthukula natiri ammanenlyawe abrahamu . vano sara , aharere wuluvala , ahimuyarela mwana abrahamu , yowo-tho ari owuluvala , khuwerya okhalana mukelamp awe sara n abrahamu yahinvaha niwan aya nsina muluku nòthonyenryawe . nsina na isakhi nnihimya wira : muluku ontteliwa murima n upatthani . isakhi anivira annuwaka .
abrahamu ahimureya ikhuni isakhi , owo mmansawe ahikuxa mwalo ni moro . vano isakhi ahíra . tithi , hiyo va nokuxa ikhuni ni moro , enama ene y &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; opaka mukuttho eri vai ? abrahamu ahakhula ìraka : muluku ononiphwanyiha , mwan aka . vamwako vasulu , abrahamu ahiteka ethatapo ya maluku , ahipweha-vo ikhun iye . numalá ahimutthukwa mwan awe , khumwatalela vasulu va ikhuni .
vano-nto ahitholola mwalo wira amuhiteke mwan awe . nto nananoru ahìwa nsu namwitthana nìraka : abrahamu ! muhimwive mwana ! vano kosuwela wira munnikiwelela ni munnikiroromela , mana khamuklmanne mwan inyu mmosene isakhi .
abrahamu ahalikelasa muxerexere , khumona mwapwittipwitthi aphanrene inyaka vamiwani . ahimukuxa yowo khumpaha , amuhelelaka mukuttho nipuro na mwan awe . numalá abrahamu ahikhuruwa vamwako vamosa n lsakhi .
isakhi ni esawú ni yakobe
isakhi vaiwalyawe mikhitto ahikoha wira : ti pani ? yakobe ahakhula ìraka : ti miyano , mwan inyu esawú . koruhenleni enama yowoxiwa . mukhureke toko , numalá mukivaheke eparakha ntoko sikilaphenlyanyu . isakhi ahinvarakasa mwan awe mmyononi , khona manri a ipuri , ahikupali wira ari esawú , khumuxonttela yakobe ìraka : muluku ovaheni sothene simphavelanyu vathí-va . oreriwa akhale ole onrowa worerihani .
yakobe ahiphiya wa labano , aninvarela muteko w olyiha inama sawe n ukhapelela-tho iye sawawe . ahimuthela mwar awe , ari rakheli , mwan awe labano , khwayara an awe . vavinryaya iyakha miloko mili , yakobe ahihokolowela okanani n amusi awe othene . ahokolowaka , ahiviriha ohiyu omosá muxerexere mwa muro yaboki : ahilapuxerya mihakhu sawe ekhopela ekina , khuhala mekhawe . ohiy ule ahiwana ni mulopwana mmosá mpakha oxa .
vamanlyaya ekhotto eyo , mulopwan ole ahimureriha yakobe , khumuhimerya wira : okhuma olelo vava , nyuwo khamunihaniwa-tho yakobe , masi muntthuna wihaniwaka israyeli , enihimya wira mukhotto a muluku . tthiri nyuwo mowana ni muluku , mowana-tho n atthu , khíyawerya oxintta .
yakobe ahatana-tho ni esawú , munn awe . anikhala elapo y okanani , weiwo wayanryawe an awe muloko nanli : rubeni , simeyoni , levi , yuda , isakari , zabuloni , yosefe , beniyamini , dani , nefetali , gadi ni aseri . ala yahikhala makhulupale a nloko na israyeli .
yosefe onrowaniwa wejitu
yosefe ahiphiya wejitu akuxiwene n anamarott ale vamuthumme . weiwo , yahimutumiherya namuteko mmosá , itthaniwa putifari . yosefe ahihala anvarelaka muteko mulopwan owo , vano itthu sothene savarawe sanikhumela orattene , okhala wira muluku ari ni yowo . putifari ahimuruma yosefe wira ettiheke etthoko awe . amwar awe
yakobe onrowa wejitu vamosa n n awe
savinryaya iyakha pili , farawó , mwené a wejitu , ahiloha . vano , ahakoha asuweli n alipa-òtaphulela oloha othene a mulaponi mwawe , masi khuhikhala awenrye otaphulela . nto mulipa a sowuiya ole akumihiwe mukhatteya ahimupuwela yosefe , khumuhimerya farawó wira : mukhatteya òkhala mmiravo mmosá mwlsrayeli . owo otaphulela oloha waka n uloha wa mulipa owoxa iphau . tthiri khukhumelela itthu sanihimenryawe .
farawó ahimwihaniha yosefe , khumwalikelela oloha wawe . miyo koloherya inyompe thanu na pili sothiyana soneneva , sikhumaka omuro nilo . weiwo-tho sahikhuma sikina thanu na pili sowereiwa ni sowotta . iva sokiserya sahimiryakasa inyompe iyo sopacerya sari soneneva . vottharelana , mpantte yowotho sahikhumelela makala mathanu na manli òrera ni òsarya etrigu . numalá , yahikhumelela-tho makala makina mathanu na manli , yari mivelo sene sowuma , khukhurasa makalale yari òrera ni òsarya etrigu .
yosefe ahimuhimerya farawó wira : muluku owoniheryani itthu sinrowa okhumelela . mpakha iyakha thanu na pili onokhala muhuwo woneneva ni mmatta enoruweriwa etrigu yinjene . vasulu vaya , sinokhumelela iyakha thanu na pili sa nsuwa , vahinrowaya orupa epula nnakhala vakhani . inama sinrowa okìnvasa ntthona . siso-tho ipyo sinrowa okhwelakhwela mmatta .
nto axinn ale yahihokolowasa , khurowa olavula ni yosefe . owo ahahimerya wira : akina othene erowaseke . ontthuna ohala atthukeliwene t ule pahi ophwanyaniwe ekahi aka . vano yuda , mmosá a axinn awo , ahimwakhula ìraka : atith ihu annimphenta valupale mwan ay &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ola ètthyako . awo animokhwa ehàmu , namuhiyaru wenno . mukihiye miyo kikhale nipuro na beniyamini .
vano yosefe khawenrye tho wisipithiha , khuhimya wira :
moise onettiha nloko na israyeli mothakoni
muluku onimopola moise
vakhwalyawe yosefe , vakhwalyaya-tho axinn awe , an aya n axisulu aya , nari nloko na israyeli , nlelo yakhalasa wejitu , khukhala nloko nulupale . vano wejitu ahikela mwené mukina , farawó , ahamusuwela yosefe ni ahasuwenle mukhaliheryo yosefe uwo wiralyawe okathi w etala .
mwené owo aniwova anaisrayeli , khuhimya wira : awo atthu owilipiha , ahana àna anjene . vano-tho anrowa wun jerereya onivikana hiyo . okhuma vavo , farawó owo ahakhanyereriha anaisrayeli ovara miteko sowoma . siso yahirummwa oteka ipá sa maluku . ohiya vo , farawó ahiruma wira ana othene axilopwana emalakaru oyariwa , eriheliweke mmuro nilo , mana nloko nihirina ana axilopwana , wakuva omalamala .
moise aninnuwa ni akhala vatthokoni va mwené farawó . owo ahileliwa ntoko mwejitu , masi khaliyanle wira ari a nloko nenle napakiwe epottha . okathi mukina ahimona mwejitu amuhaxa mwisrayeli mmosá . moise ahinanariwa , khumwiva mwejit ule . nto ahitthyawela elapo y omadiyani , khukhala avaraka muteko w omakampusi vatthokoni va namukuttho mmosá , lhaniwa yetoro .
muluku onimuruma moise owopola atthu awe
moise alyiha inama sa yetoro mothakoni . alyihaka sisale , ahiphiya osinayi , ori mwako wa muluku . weiwo ahòna miwa savarela , masi sihinalala . owo ahitikinihiwa , khwattamela wira onexexe . vano ahìva nsu nihimyaka wira : moise ! moise !
miyo ki muluku axitith inyu , muluku abrahamu , muluku a isakhi , muluku a yakobe . moise anòva onweha muluku , tivó ahikhunela owitho . nto muluku ahimuhimerya wira : miyo kihona ohaxiwa wa nloko naka wejitu .
kihiwa-tho okhuwela waya mwaha wa masoso anonihiwaya . kosuwela mahawelo aya . tivó , miyo kinorumani wira murowé mwamphwanye farawó , òvahereryeni nloko naka . vano moise khwira : mivo ki pani w orowa okumana ni farawó n umulèla mitthaka iya ? masi muluku ahimwirela : murowé . miyo kinokhala ni nyuwo .
moise ahoniherya-tho muxankiho mukina , ìraka : anaisrayeli khanrowa okikupali , kahimeryd wira ti muluku axitithi aya okirumme orowa wa vawo . awo anokikoha wira :
van owo ahihokolowela wejitu vamosa n amusi awe . aroni , munn awe , ahirowa okumana ni yowo . moise ni aroni yahathukumanya anaisraveli othene , khuwalikelela muteko muluku warummyawe ovara. anaisrayeli yahòna wira muluku aphavela owopola mmaxakhani mine mwaryaya : yahimuroromela muluku yowo , khumukokhorela .
muhiye nloko naka nitaphuwe !
moise n aroni yahirowa okumana ni farawó , khumwirela : muluku ontthuna wira muhiye nloko nahu nitaphuwe . mwené farawó khaphavela wahiya anaisrayeli , mana awo yaninvarela miteko sinjene . tivó ahimukoha moise n aroni wira : ti pani muluk uwo a israyeli vowira miyo kimwiwelele ?
miyo nkinimusuwela , nto nkinahiya anaisrayeli erowaka . kinimunjererya-tho miteko sinivaraya , wira ehimuliyalé mutthu onruma elapo ela . nihiku nene nenlo aharuma alipa-òwehaweha wira : mwavarihe muteko vanjene , muhahiyeké emumulaka , wira ehikinyonyihe-tho .
anaisrayeli yanihawa vanjene mwaha wa miteko sowoma sakhanyereriwaya ovara . moise ahavekela apwiya . vano muluku ahimulaphela ìraka : miyo ki muluku anyu , kinimokumihani wejitu . nyuwo munrowa okhala nloko naka ni munosuwela wira miyo ki muluku anyu . kinimoholani mpakha elapo yamulaphenlyaka abrahamu n isakhi ni yakobe . miyo kinimovahani elapo eyo ntoko yohiyeriw anyu .
muluku ahimoniherya farawó owerya wawe . siso ahikumiherya wejitu iwo ihasara muloko sotakhalexa : ewiriphi , ohiruwerya mmatta , masi yahithatuwa ephome , inama yahirwela eretta ya makhwatta , epheyo yothene yahisareya iretta , vano atthu othene a wejitu yahisareyatho makhwatta mwerutthuni .
farawó ahisuwela wakhumalyaya ihukhumu iye , tivó ahothererya imara ttharu , ahimyaka wira rowa wataphula anaisrayeli ale yahaxiwa evarihiwaka miteko sowoma . masi , evirakaru ehukhumu , farawó anitthikela ottuli , khihinatthuna wataphula .
ohiyu wopacerya wa pásikha
sothene sahìreya ntoko muluku sahimmyawe : yahivakasiwa ana othene axilopwana opacerya oyariwa , okhuma ana amasikhini mpakha mwana opacerya a mwené farawó . ohiy &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ule wothene atthu a wejitu yahiwunlela àn aya . vano farawó ahimwihaniha moise n aroni , khuwirela : mwakuveke , mwakuxe atthu anyu vamosa ni mihakhu say a , murowaseke nanano . siso anaisrayeli yahikhuma wejitu , khuvira yettaka .
nloko na israyeli khanniliyala-tho ohiy &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ule wopacerya wa pasikha . siso-tho , axipapa n aximama a israyeli khinaliyale wira muluku ahisuka ekumi y an aya opacerya oyariwa . okhuma vavo , mwana mwamulopwana opajeiya oyariwa anninvaha muluku . khula eyakha annimwira pasikha , nira n okhuma : siso anniwalikelela an aya wahal ola : ntata nowei ya na muluku ti nnoponle mwepotthani wejitu .
muluku onopola nloko nawe
miriyamu , murokor &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; awe moise , ahipacerya wina ni wipa vamosa n athiyana othene , ewipelaka apwiya wira : mwattottopele apwiya , mwavuwihe . awo ahasamiha mmasini awanan ihu .
muluku onikhapelela nloko nawe
valapunwaya ephareya yoxerya , moise ahettiha nloko na israyeli mothakoni . vaviralyaya mahiku mararu yettaka , yahiphwanya ehime . vano masi aya van owawa : khavo mutthu awerya owurya . anaisrayeli yahimukuphanya moise yiraka : mwaha wa nyuwo hivo ninrowa okhwasa ntthona mothakoni-mu .
moise ahinvekela muluku ìraka : xontte , munikhaliherye ! muluku ahimuthonyerya moise mwiri nimosa : owo ahiríhela eritt aya emosa mmasini , masi awo yahihiya owawa , khukhalaka osiva . atthu othene yahiwuryasa .
eviraka-tho mahiku vakhani , anaisrayeli yahipacerya omulavulela moise , yiraka : fatari nahanle wejitu !
okhuma vavo , axipapa anniwalikelela an aya enamuna muluku yakhapelenlyawe nloko nawe n inamuna enkhapelelawe nlelo . atthu othene esuweleke wira muluku t ororomeleya ni ti mukhaliheryo aya .
muluku onavaha atthu soruma sawe
mweri waneraru vakhumalyaya wejitu , anaisrayeli yahiphiya omwako si nayi , khumakasa mukhitte mwa mwako yowo .
vano muluku ahihimya wira : miyo k apwiya muluku anyu . miyo kihokumihani wejitu waryanyu ipottha .
muhikhalane amuluku akina , okihiya miyo . muhipake ilatarato sa muluku .
muhivehd nsina na muluku .
muhiliyale ottittimiha nihiku na esabadu : ahikhale onvara muteko nihiku nenlo .
mwattittimihe apap inyu n amam inyu .
muhimwive mutthu .
muhiraruwd .
muhiye .
muhothe , nnakhala muhimotherye mukhw inyu .
muhimukhalele nrima mwar awe mukhw inyu .
muhikhalele nrima itthu sa mwanene .
apwiya yahimunnya moise mapawe manli a maluku , vavo apwiya mmansaya yalempyaya soruma iye muloko . mapawe ala ti mukhalelo wo watàna muluku wiralyawe n aisrayeli , nloko nawe .
makhalelo makinaku owettela
nyuwo , atthu a israyeli , mwiwe : apwiya ti muluku anyu , apwiya pahi : khavo-tho mukina . tivó , nyuwo muhana omphenta muluku ni murim anyu wothene n iroho anyu yothene n ikurú sanyu sothene .
mwatuphela muttetthe mukina , muhihonone miri sa mmatta . mulyeke mihokorokho saya , masi miri sene muhuhe .
muhimpuherye muthiyana okhweliwe n iy awe , nnakhala ekwasuni , yawo ahirina owakhapelela . mwawirelaru yotakhala , awo khukikhuwelela , miyo kinowiwelela .
nyuwo mona wira enyompe walá epwittipwitthi ya mukhw inyu yorimela , mujalele . murowé mwanvahererye mwanene .
mulipa-òthoiwa ovarelani muteko , muhipise omuliva . mmulive nihiku nenlo .
mwamutholaka mattuvi anyu walá mwahattaka mèle anyu , muhimaliheke-mo othene . muhiyahiyeke , wira alipa-òthoiwa ettotteke .
muhimuhaxeke namunva onkhala mulaponi mwanyu .
mmuhiveke yowo apuheke mirerelo sothene nyuwo sirinanyu .
mwaphenteke anamurwa ntoko nyuwo siniphentananyu . muhiliyale wira ni nyuwo-tho mwahikhala anamurwa wejitu . ti miyo kinotumereryani itthu iva : miyo apwiya muluku anyu .
muhimuruwane mulipa-òhiwa , mana owo khanweiya wisakiha . muhimutekelele ephiro mulipa-òhona , mana onokela vexani .
muhimunlele nrima munn inyu nnakhala vakhani . mukhw inyu ìraka yotakhala , mmuhihe , wira ni nyuwotho muhiphwanye mulattu . muhikhale mulipa-òwunla ikuhu walá nanrima . mumphenteke mukhw inyu ntoko siniphentanyu mmansinyu .
okhwa wa moise
muluku ahopola nloko nawe napakiwe ipottha wejitu . mpakha iyakha miloko mixexé yettaka mothakoni , anaisrayeli yahixutta omuroromela muluku , vahixutta-tho okhaliheryana mukina ni mukhw awe .
alopwana nathiyana yakhumanse wejitu vamosa ni moise yahivira yuluvalaka , khukhwasa mothakoni . navetho moise ahuluvala . ahona wira , wavira okathi vakhani , arowa okhwa . tivó ahireriha nloko na israyeli ìraka : oreriwa ti nyuwo , israyeli ! nloko xeni ninlikana ni nyuwo , muri nloko nopoliwe n apwiva ?
numalá , moise ahiwela vasulu va mwako neho . vavo apwiya yahimuthonyerya elapo yothene y okanani , yeyo yalaphenlyawe wira yarowa okhala va nloko nawe . moise akhwiye nipuro nenlo , ola wa mikano s elapo yolaiheriwa . tthiri mulnku ahimuhimerya wira : nyuwo munimona elapo eyo ni maitho anyu , masi khamunikela-mo . anaisrayeli yahimunlela moise mpakha mahiku miloko miraru .
mamwene ni maprofeta
mulaponi yolaiheriwa
moise ahinatthi okhwa ahimuthanla yoxuwa wira aholeleke nloko nawe . owo ahana waholela anaisrayeli mpakha wakeliha mulaponi m &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; okanani , memmo mwakhanlyawe abrahamu n isakhi ni yakobe .
masi maloko vakhalasa weiwo khiyatthunne wira atthu a israyeli ekele elapo ele . khiyalhiyereni ye yomoliwaka mulaponi-mme . anaisrayeli , yettihiwaka ni yoxuwa , yahiroromela yele muluku yalaphenlyawe .
siso yahivira ekuxaka elapo ele vakhanivakhani . yahiteka ipa sava , khíyalima imatta saya , ntoko akanani .
anaisrayeli yahixuttihiwa itthu sinjene n akanani : yahisuwela okathi wo walá n ukathi wohatta ; yahixutta opaka ikaruma sa eyuma ; yahixutta-tho wetetela yolya yosivexa n utthava ikuwo .
masi etthu emosa pahi yahaweryaya watakiha akanani , wari wakokhorela amuluku okanani , mana yawo yahatana ni muluku . anaisrayeli wanarikela vanjene wet tela yoruma ela , okhala wira akanani yahisariha mapuro othene edini ava : mmatta , mmyakonini mukhitte mwa miri sulupale , memmo mwakokhorelaya-mo amuluku aya , evekelaka epula n uruwerya .
okathi anaisrayeli yamwiwelelaya muluku a abraha mu ni a isakhi ni a yakobe , muluku yowo anakhapelela ni anareriha . masi okathi yamuhiyaya muluk uwo , sanakhumelela ihasara n uhawa wulupale . vano , yanjkunuwakam enwehaka muluku , yatthamwakaru envekelaka nlevelelo , muluku anaweha-tho atthu awe ni mphento , anareriha .
anaisrayeli animphavela mwené
anaisrayeli vaphiyalyaya okanani yahikawelana mittetthe sokhala , ettharihaka mahimo muloko ni manli saryaya . vano makhulupale a mahimo yahakawela amusi othene mapuro omaka . khula etthoko yahakhela etthaya yaphiyerya olima . maloko awo yakhala otaphuwa , masi okathi wekhotto yanipwexereryana wira yisakiheke oholo w awanani aya . okathi ene yowo , muluku anarumihela mopoli , yowo awakiherya mmaxakhani .
nto anaisrayeli wanalipela omuroromela muluku mmosá pahi n uwehererya wira owo amwarumihela mòpoli wa khula muxankiho warowa okhumelela . awo yaphavela okhalana mwené okathi wothene .
samuweli ari mopoli mmosá ni profeta yarumiheliwaya ni muluku , vano atthu yahinvekela samuweli uwo wira athanlele mutthu , wira akhale mwené aya . owo ahakoha anaisrayeli wira : vekekhai nyuwo mumphavela omukokhorelaka mutthu , onvarela muteko numuliva mpóxito ? makhulupale a maloko a israyeli yahakhula wira : hiyo nimphavela okhala ntoko maloko makina . mwené onrowa onitaphulelaka itthu siri soloka n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; iye siri sohiloka . mwené onrowa-tho oniholela okathi w ekhotto .
muluku ahimwirela samuweli : nwirele simphavelaya , mana khamuhiyó nyuwo anokhottelayani , masi ankikhottela miyo . vano samuweli , ammmwaka ni muluku , ahimuttikitthela makhura sawuli , wira akhalé mwené anaisrayeli . muluku ahinvaha eroho awe sawuli : owo ilmukhala mwené òrera murima van wira ahimuroromela muluku ni murim awe wothene .
masi sawuli khatthuna omuroromela mutthu mukina , nnakhala muluku . khavo-tho amuroromelawe . tivó ahiripiwa murima , khuhapuwa . nave muluku ahimunyanyala yowo . tivó-nto , khawerya-tho waholela anaisrayeli , hatá owakiherya .
davidi , makampusi obethelehemu
davidi , ayariwe obethelehemu , ahikhalihiwa mwené anenli aisrayeli ni mulupale wavikana akina othene . owo animuroromela muluku , vano muluku ari ni yowo . tivó nloko na muluku khinaliyanle-tho nsina na davidi . wisrayeli sinnalikeliwa ihantisi sinjene sa davidi .
davidi ari mwana mukhani a yesé . owo ira alyihaka ipwittipwitthi okathi waphiyalyawe samuweli wira amuttikitthele makhura omwene . owo ari makampusi òrera murima . anisuwela ni aniphenta ipwittipwitthi sawe : okathi havara walá kharamu wipawe arwaka , owo khatthyawa . davidi uwo ari owilipiha : khawova awanani a muluku n atthu .
vannihimmwa wira , varyawe mmiravo , ahirowa waxekurya axinn awe omaxaxani . wei wo ahisuwelihiwa wira ahikhala mulopwana mmosá , orekamexa ni òtupa , ihaniwa goliva , aveha anaisrayeli vamosa ni muluku .
khari-vo n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; aisrayeli aminyanyela owana ni mulopwan owo .
masi davidi ahinvirikanva , khumwirela : nyuwo munosuwela enamuna enweryawe muluku a israyeli . davidi ahihela nluku mpharanjikulani mwawe , ahapheliha muru n ikuru sawe sothene , ahinvonyerya goliva , khumpwexa eyuji , khumorela vathí . awanani awe yahovasa , yahitthyawa , khuhitthuna-tho owana n anaisrayeli .
davidi anisuwela wipa isipo n umopa xittatta . mmasalimuni , eri elívuru ya isipo sa nloko na muluku , sokhalamo isipo miloko muloko n isipo miloko mithanu ntoko seiye simpwa ni davidi .
owo ahikhala ni mwené sawuli mpakha okathi munjene .
okathi mwené waripiwawe murima , davidi animwipela isipo , owo khiyahakalala . davidi aniwerya waxintla awanani awe , okhala wira muluku an ni yowo . tivó mwené sawuli ahimuruma owetlihaka anakhotto awe .
davidi ahixintta mittitthi sulupale s awanani awe , siso-tho atthu vanimutthapela . nto sawuli ahimukhalela nrima . vano-nto yahivira mahiku manjene amulupatthaka wira amwive . davidi vamosa nakhwawe yahimwipitha sawuli .
nihiku nikina , afilisti yahatuphela-tho anaisrayeli , masi anakhotto a mwené sawuli khivawemye oxintta . omwako gilbowa yahiviwa ana araru a sawuli , owo-tho ahivulaliwa vanjene : tivó ahisiva ni xow awe .
davidi , mwené oyerusalemu
vakhwiyawe sawuli , davidi ahikhalihiwa mwené a wlsrayeli wothene . ahikuxa-tho muttetthe w oyerusalemu , khukhaliha muttetthe mulupalexa womwene awe . davidi ahiruma oruhiwa oyerusalemu nivuku no watàna ni mapawe a ikano , yawo yalempwe somma muloko sa muluku . davidi atthuna wira oyerusalemu okhale muttetthe wa muluku .
mmeloni mwaya , profeta natani ahirowa-tho okumana ni davidi , khumuhimerya wira : muluku khantthuna wira mmutekele empa . masi uwo t okhanle wotekelani empa nyuwo : emp ene ekumi , eri etthoko yolipa . mwakhwa vale , mwan inyu onrowa wettihaka nloko na muluku . molumo ala khankhwelihiwa-tho wa mahiku othene .
tivó , atthu a israyeli annikupali wira mopoli mulupale , yowo apwiya àlaphenlyava wavelela atthu , ontthuna oyariwa munlokoni mwa davidi .
nsipo na davidi
apwiya ti makampusi aka : khivo enikihalela .
awo annikihola mapuro òwatta yolya : annikihola omuró ori màsi òrirya wira kamumuleke .
awo t anlipiha murim aka , annikiviriha iphiro soloka .
kaviraka mwepiphini mowopiha , nkinova etthu yotakhala , mana nyuwo , apwiya , muri ni miyo .
salomoni onimutekela empa muluku
mwené davidi vakhwiyawe , ahivithiwa oyerusalemu . salomoni , mwan awe , ahihala ettihaka nloko n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; aisrayeli .
mwené salomoni khawanne ikhotto ntoko atithi awe davidi . owo ahiphavela ovanela ni watàna ni maloko makina . ahinjererya marotta mulaponi ni ahirumiha ikalawa sawe sulupale olapuwa iphareya ni wakakhanva marotta ni maloko makina . siso ahithajiri vanjene . ahiwihaniha aratti a ilapo sikina , ahathela athiyana a ilapo s ottaiwene .
masi amalapo awo yarwiye elattuliwaka ni salomoni vaniphavela wakokhorela amuluku aya . mwené salomoni ahatthuniheiya atthu awo watekela altari amuluku aya mulaponi mme mwa wisrayeli . salomoni yowo ahalompa amuluku amalapo , anakokhorela . siso , ahimuhiya muluku ekekhai , khuvirikanya watàna wawe .
miruku sa salomoni
mwana orina ankhili onnatteliha minima atithi awe ; vano mwana ohirina ankhili onnaripiha murima ame awe .
nrima ninrwana ekhotto ; nlema n uphenta ninliyala ovehiwa .
mulipa-òvaha onovahiwa vowatta : onakhaliherya akhwawe onokhaliheriwa .
onetta ephiro va exàriya onnattittimiha apwiya ; onihapuwa ephiro eyo onnathanya apwiya .
oreriwa t ule onakhapelela òthoiwa : wathanya akhw ihu , etthu yotakhala .
ohiniwa okhuwela wa masikhini , akhuwelela vale , khanakhuleliwa .
mamwene manli munlokoni nimosa pahi
vakhwiyawe salomoni , mwan awe ihaniwa robowamu ahihala ettihaka omwene oyerusalemu . makhulupale yahinvaha miruku yiraka : atith inyu yahaliviha alimi n anamatumiha mpóxito munjene . nyuwo mwavukula mpoxit &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; owo , anaisrayeli othene anowakhelani ntoko mwené .
masi robowamu khawiwelenle makhulupale awo a miruku . tivó , mahimo muloko , yakhala mpantte w onikela epheyo w elapo , yahimuhimerya wira : khinnimphavela-tho mwené mukina a etthoko ya davidi . hivo nnomuthanla mwené ahu .
nihimo na yuda pahi , nakhala mpuwa moyemsalemu , ti namwiwelenle robowamu . nihimo nlo naihaniwa siso okhala wira nari osulu wa yuda , mwan &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; awe yakobe .
okhuma vavo khakhanle-tho mwené àrumela oyerusalemu pahi , masi ahikhala-tho mwené mukina osikemi , elapo yosamariya .
muluku mukumi
yerobowamu ari mwené opacerya ettiha mahimo muloko onikela epheyo . owo ahupuwela wira : khivanrerela wira atthu aka eroweke okokhorela n uhela mukuttho mpani mwa muluku oyerusalemu . tivó ahiruma opakiwa amwanyompe anli ewero . mmosá ahimpweha mpantte wonikela epheyo womwene awe , muttettheni w odani .
mukina , ahimpweha mpantte w okusini , mmuttettheni wobetheli . numalá , ahilaleya mulaponi mwawe mothene wira : nyuwo , atthu othene , muhiroweke-tho oyerusalemu opaka nira nanyu walá ohela mukuttho anyu . nyuwo munniwerya omphwanva muluku mmuttettheni modani ni m obetheli . muluk uwo ti mmosám yole akumihale axitith inyu wejitu .
anaisrayeli akina khiydjanle etthu yahimmyawe yerobowamu , okhala wira yanupuwela wira muluku ahakhottiherya opaka ilatarato samuthonverya yowo , ntoko sapakaya atthu a wejitu ; yanisuwela-tho wira , vamwakakhanva muluku mukumi n ilatarato yokhwa , yanvirikanya watdna muluku wapankyawe n awo .
muluku owerya sothene
mamwene a wlsrayeli yanimuliyala muluku ni watàna wawe imara sinjene . muluku yowo aharuma maprofeta , vari anamitthak awe , orowa olavula ni mamwene n atthu othene a wlsrayeli .
eliya ahova onanariwa wa mwené : siso ahitupha mukano , khutthyawela ofenisia . weiwo ahimaka vatthokoni va muthiyana mmosá masikhini , ari namukhweli ni arina mwana mmosá pahi mwamulopwana . mwan awe owo ahiwereiwa , khukhwa . vano namukhweli uwo ahimwirela eliva : nyuwo mwa mpatthani a muluku , munkhala vaté vaka vava .
tivó muluku onnikdna , onniweha tho itampi saka , khiyakihukhumu . eliya ahikuxa murutthu wa mwanamwane owo akhwiye , khwatalela volilini : numalá ahuramela , khulompa ìraka : apwiya muluku aka , mmuhokoloxerye ekumi mwanamwane ola . muluku ahìwa ovekela wa profet awe : mwanamwane ahihihimuwa , khukhala-tho mukumi . eliya ahimukuxa mmatatani , khunvahererya mam awe .
muluku mmosáru
savinryaya iyakha pili , muluku ahimuruma tho profeta eliya orowa okumana ni mwené akhabi . mwené owo ahimwirela profeta wira : mwaha wa nyuwo , anaisrayeli othene ehathowa yolya . masi eliya ahakhula wira : nkihiyo miyo kithowinhe yolya : ti nyuwo n amus inyu muthowihanse .
nyuwo momuhiya muluku ahu , khumuttharaka bayali . mwarume atthu othene ethukumane omwako karmelo : weiwo onrowa osuwanyeya muluku ekekhai . mwené ahathukumanya atthu othene a mulaponi mwawe omwako iwo : yahithukumana maprofeta othene n anamukuttho othene a bayali vamosa n atthu anjene .
eliya ahihimya wira : mwateke altari , mwixathi vasulu vava enama emosa , numalá munvekele muluku anyu .
khino owo onorumiha moro wirimu onrwa wakhelela mukuttho anyu . vano anamukuttho ni maprofeta a bayali yahateka altari aya , khupweha enama vasulu vava : yahimulompa muluku aya okhuma vasisu mpakha othana eriyari .
nto , okhuma othana eriyari mpakha makaripi yanihimya wira : bayali ! muniwiriyane ! masi awo yakhuwela mahala . khivo etthu yakhumelela . makaripi eliya ahimutekela altari muluku a israyeli : ahipweha enama vasulu valtari , khwitthela masi .
numalá ahilompa ìraka : apwiya ! nyuwo mwá muluku abrahamu n a isakhi n a yakobe !
nwoniherye atthu othene wira mwa muluku anaisrayeli ni wira miyo ki murumeyi anyu . apwiya , mukiwiriyane ! vano wahikhuruwa moro wirimu , khupaha enama yothene . atthu othene yari vavale yahilhukumela ni wova , khuhimya wira : apwiya ti muluku ! oviraka okathi vakhani , wirimu wahiripela , khupacerya orupa epula yinjene .
muluku onimukuxa eliya wirimu
eliya ahòna wira muluku aniphavela omukuxa . owo ari elapo ya mpantte mukina wa muro yordani : aphavela okhalaka mekhawe , masi eliseyo , mwixutti awe , khatthuna omuhiya mekhawe . siso , amuholaka eliya , ahòna moro okhumwaka wirimu ntoko niwimpi nulupale . eyupuru iyo ya moro yahimukuxa eliya , khumurowana osulu ntoko wira akuxiwe mukaroni .
alipa òthoiwa anolya mpakha ovona
muluku onivaha ethonyeryo nloko nawe
okathi akhazi ettihawe oyerusalemu , mamwene manli yahimukumiherya ekhotto , khuphiya oyerusalemu n anakhotto anjenexa , khurukurerya muttetthe . vano mwené n &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; atthu awe othene yahithukumela ni wova , nloko sinttikinyeyaya miri sa mutakhwani yopaka epheyo yulupale .
mwené akhazi ahirowa owehaweha muratthi waruha masi . profeta yesaya ahiphiya tho vavale . owo ahinvahererya mwené mutthaka arummwawe ni muluku , amuhimeryaka wira :
mukhurunuwe murima , muhové . mamwene awo manli ahìwanana wotuphelani , masi mmuroromele muluku : owo onimolipihani . owo omphavela wovahani ethonyeryo y osuwelexa wira onnokhaliheryani . ekanyeryo t ikanyeryo entthunanyu onvekela , onimovahani . masi akhazi ahikhotta yovah eyo , ìraka : nkintthuna omuttehatteha muluku . vano yesaya khwira :
muluku yowo tontthuna wovahani ethonyeryo . mone : harusi nimosa onompala , amuyare mwana mwamulopwana , onkelawe onvaha nsina na emanuweli , nnihimya wira : muluku ori ni hiyo .
profeta amosi onihimya otakhala w atthu
apwiya anihimya wira : sotakhala ttharu , nnakhala xexé , sinìriwa n atthu oyuda . miyo nkinalevelela : kinimwahukhumu . awo athanya masu aka , akhotla wiwelela soruma saka . awo ahihiya ekuxiwaka n amuluku a ethiru , ntoko siralyaya axitithi aya . tivó kinopaha elapo y oyuda , ipa s oyerusalemu sinopatta moro .
apwiya t anihimya wira : mwaha wa sotakhala ttharu walá xexé sinìriwa n aisrayeli , kinimwahukhumu . awo amutumiha mutthu ohitthenke n isisapo ya musurukhu , annanyakattela vathí ale olhoiwa , annakhottiherya ale olosowa opuha mirerelo saya .
tivó etthaya enothukumela , yokhuneleni , ntoko sinthukumelaya ekaro yamukhani yalemeliwa . nnakhala nuilipa-otthyawexa khanrowa owerya oxerekela . hatá ale olipexa animokhwa , vano ale otupexa animova .
yeremiya onalopola atthu ahimeryaka wira enimorwa ehukhumu ya muluku
atthu yahanle yettelaka watàna waya ni muluku yari vakhani . anakhotto aya khiyawerya owana n anakhotto a ilapo sowerya . khiyàwerya-tho owana n asiria , yawo yatuphenle elapo ni yavanre atthu anjene a mahimo muloko onikela epheyo , khwakumiha mulaponi mwaya yarowanaka omalaponi . ale yamini yanona itthu iya okhala ehukhumu ya muluku , ehukhumu yeyo yawopopihanawe ni molumo a maprofet awe .
oyerusalemu profeta yeremiya anihimya wira : sovira iyakha miloko mili ni ttharu kinari profeta a muluku . kiholaleryani molumo othene a muluku . masi nyuwo khamujalenle . miyo kohimya wira : muhiye iphiro sanyu sotakhala : muhiye wira itthu sonanara nyuwo mwaiwelela vale , munrowa okhalaka mulaponi muluku àvahalyawe axitith inyu ni nyuwo wa mahiku othene . nto nyuwo khamukiwelenle .
tivó apwiya annihimya wira : kinimwaruha atthu a elapo yonikela epheyo . kinomukuxa nabukodonosori , mwené òbabilonia , akhale ekopo aka . kinomuruma wotuphelani n utuphela ilapo sothene sirukureniye oyerusalemu . owo onopwexa elapo . vano nyuwo munomurumelaka mwené òbabilonia &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; .
tthiri , vahiraneya siso : nabukodonosori vamosa n anakhotto awe yahirukurerya muttetthe w oyerusalemu . muhina w okathi vakhani khuvo aweiya othuma ephau nnakhala emosa .
ohawa n osikhini wahinjerereya . numalá , atthu òbabilonia yahithorolasa ixiri sa kako òyerusalemu , yahituphela muttetthe , khupaha empa ya muluku ni empa ya mwené n ipa sikina sari sottittimiheya . akako yahipwexakasiwa . ikamma sorerihiwa sa mpani mwa muluku sahikuxiwa . makhulupale n aratti othene yasuwela otthava yahivariwa , khurowaniwa omalaponi .
yahiwe mulaponi mwaya t ale pahi yari otepaxa òthoiwa n alimi .
muluku omphavela olevelela nloko nawe
atthu oyuda ni òyerusalemu vavariwaya , yahikhala obabiloni mpakha iyakha miloko mithanu . vano kiro , mwené òpersia , ahikuxa òbabilonia ni ahilaleya ekano emosa mulaponi mwawe mothene , yahimya wira : apwiya , muluku a wiiimu , akivaha owerya w ommaka omwene wothene wa vathí . awo akiruma oteka-tho emp aya oyerusalemu . atthu othene yale ari nloko na muluku ehokoloweleke oyerusalemu , eteke-tho weiwo empa ya muluku .
othene ale yupuxeriwe ni eroho ya muluku yah i venya , khiyetta erowaka . anamwattamanani-aya yahavaha ewero ni eparatha ni muhuwo ni sorera sikina . mwené kiro ahiruma ohokoloxiwa itthu sorerihiwa sakuxalyawe nabukodonosori mpani mwa muluku , khurowana òbabilonia .
nsipo n ale anihokolowela mulaponi mwaya
apwiva yahokoloxeryaka mulaponi mwaya atthu a israyeli yatthukweliwe , hiyo nona ntoko oloha . mwano mwahu mwahisareya otteliwa murima : nlumi nahu nahipa nsipo n otthapa .
vano maloko makina yanihimya wira :
apwiya awirela itthu sotikiniha !
ayo ! apwiya anirela itthu sotikiniha : tivó vantteliwahu murima vanjene .
atthu aninwehererya mópoli
ayuda
atthu yahokolonwe opotthani òbabilonia yari a nihirno na yuda , yayariwe oyerusalemu n ilapo s okhuvela . awo yahipaka nikhuru na nloko n ayuda . awo yaphavela okhalaka ntoko sakhanlyaya axitithi aya , masi khiyaweiya okhala siso , mana mamwene òbabilonia yahavaha elapo y oyerusalemu ni mittetthe sowattamela amalapo yale yatthara solimalela saya ni yakokhorela amuluku aya .
akako , yakiherya khalai oyerusalemu , yahipwexakasiwa . empa ya muluku yatekiwe ni mwené salomoni navetho vahipwexiwa . ayuda yahiteka-tho ipa saya n akako oyerusalemu . eyakha yanenli numalá otthikela mulaponi mwaya , yahirihela nluku nopacerya w empa yanenli ya muluku .
ayuda yahihokolowela okhala mulaponi mwaya , masi nlelo elapo yavira ehaxiwaka ni mamwene omalaponi .
mamwene awo yanarumihela oyerusalemu anakhotto aya n alipa-òliviha mposito ni maguvernatoro .
wahikhala okathi anamurwa yaphavelaya wahiha a yuda wamini w abrahamu . okathi ene yowo mwené mmosá mmalapo ahakhanyererya atthu othene yakhala momweneni mwawe wettela ni wamini itthu owo mwanene settelawe ni sain inawe ni wakokhorela amuluku awe .
muhiná mwa iyakha iyo , anamukuttho òyerusalemu yahivira etthikelaka solimalela iye sorerihiwa . okathi utvo , atthu òloka yanlwelela ikano ni mixuttiho sa muluku . yanixutta-tho vasyá ti pani muluku ni watina wapakalyaya ni yowo . awo yaninwehererya mwené arowa owòpola , yowo alaiheriwe ni muluku . anaisrayeli yanilupatthiwa ni yaniviwa mwaha wo wamini .
masi hatá okathi yaiviwaya yanihimya omwamini waya muluku mukumi , yowo oniwerya owopola atthu awe enamwi yiviwe .
yobi oninvekela muluku wira amwakhule
yobi ari mutthu oloka . amuroromela muluku pahi , nto khajalela atakhali . owo ari thajiri . ahikhalana an awe muloko : athanu nanli axilopwana , araru axithivana . arina ipwittipwitthi sinjene nikamelo n inyompe . yobi khiwanvila omuttara muluku , yowo anvahale sorera iye sothene .
masi muluku ahimwehererya yobi . anawiye anjene yahituphela inama sawe , yahiwivakasa amakampusi , khukuxa sothene . yobi khatthikenle ottuli mwaha w etthu ila .
owo amuroromela muluku pahi . oviraka okathi vakhani , yahimukhumelela ehasara ekina . nihiku nimosá n awe axilopwana n axithiyana yahilattuleliwa yolya ya nira . elyaka siso , empa vahapittuwela , khukhwasa othene .
yobi vaiwalyawe ehasara eyo yakhumelenle , ahira : miyo va kiyariwe epwitipwiti . siso-tho kakhwaka , kinrowa epwitipwiti . apwiya t akivanhe sothene : vawo-tho t akankhe . apwiya ettottopeliwe !
vottharelana , wahimphwanya tho ohawa okina wotepaxa : wahimurwela oretta wa makokho .
yobi , yole ari thajiri , vano akilathi vatturwani : anisuna makhwatt awe ni makula .
amwar awe vahimwattamela , khumwirela : ti worera omuroromela wanyu muluku , khahiyo ?
vano mmutakhalihe muluku , mukhwé ! masi yobi ahiwakhula wira : nyuwo munlavula ntoko mutthu ohinimusuwela muluku . hiyo ninnakhelela wa muluku sothene siri sorera , nto nihinweryela-ni wakhelela-tho iye sohaxa ?
yobi ahikhalana apatthani awe araru . vasuwenlyaya wira ahiphwanya ohawa , yahirowa omuxekurya , ephavelaka omuhakalaliha . vamonalyaya ni mahawelo ale othene , yahipaceryasa wunla . yahikilathi varyawe mpakha mahiku mathanu na manli , othana n uhiyu .
khuvo a yawo ataphunle eyano wira amulavulihe , mana yanona wira masoso a yobi khiyàrere watta . vano yobi ahipacerya olavula ni muluku n uvanyihana ni yowo . anikhupanyerya mwaha wa masoso awe ni animotherya muluku yowo wira t amuruhenle ihasara iye sothene , anari òrera murima .
axipatthani awe yobi yahitikinihiwa ni wova .
awo yaniphavela omwakiha muluku viraka :
nyuwo mumverya sai omotherya muluku ?
hiyo othene ninnisuwela wira muluku naxariya .
owo onnitthuvela sorera ni onnihukhumu sotakhala .
nyuwo mwahatthenke ni mwahaphwanenle ehukhumu ila n uhawa nno wothene , muluku khoruhelani .
masi yobi anikupali etthu yahimyawe . owo ahinvekela muluku wira amulele mulattu xeni wamphwanyiha ohawa iwe wothene , owo anari mutthu oloka .
axipatthani awe ale yahilavulana vanjene wira yahimukupalihe yobi ovonva wawe . owo ahittheka , mana muluku khanira vahixariya . masi yobi khatthunn etthu : aphavela osuwela pahi xeni muluku ahalaka otthuvela wamini wawe ni makhalelo ohawa .
muluku ahimulavuliha yobi mpheyoni yulupale , khumukoha ìraka : mwa pani nyuwo mumphavela osuwela miteko saka ? munihimerya-ni itthu sihinweryanyu osuwela ?
nyuwo mwari vai miyo kitikithei yaka elapo ?
ti nyuwo nvalannye etthaya n iphareva ?
ti nyuwo mukhalinhe okathi w othana ni okathi w ohiyu ?
ti nyuwo mpwenhe itheneri osulu ?
ti nyuwo muniphwanyiha yolya inama ?
yobi ahìwa sokoha iva , khuhona yo wakhula .
vano-nto ahòna wira khavo onwei ya osuwela evulupale awe muluku . muluku t otepaxa wunnuwa , atthu vanweryaya omuroromela , enamwi ehisuwelaka miteko sawe .
yobi ahiwakhula apwiya ìraka : vano kosuwela wira apwiya t owerya sothene . miyo n uhisuwela waka kihavekela okoniherya miteko saya , seiyo siri sotikiniha , miyo kihiweiyaka osuwela . mpakha va miyo kasuwela apwiya wiwasa pahi : masi vano maitho aka annaweha . tivó korurya sothene sihimyalyaka , wira karoromeleke apwiya .
yona onixutta omusuwela muluku
yona ari profeta . muluku ahimulavuliha ìraka : nvenye mwetteke . murowé ònínive : mwahimerye atthu a weiwo wira kinimwaruhela ehukhumu aka , mana t otakhala murima . masi yona khaphavela orowa ònínive : tivó ahiwela ekalawa varina ekwah aya y ottaiwene . siso yona aphavela otthyawela ottaiwene ni muluku .
masi apwiya yahikumiherya epheyo yulupale mphareya . mawimpi yahikakhasa ekalaw eyo , enahala vakhani osama . atthu othene yahova vanjene : khula mmosá ahimulompa muluku awe . masi yona amumpa muhina mw &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ekalawa . nahota ahinvenxa ìraka : nyuwo munwerya sai orupa ?
nvenye , mmulompe muluku anyu ! owo onowerya onopola . anakalawa yahihimeryana wira : nrowé naxelye ehako , wira nimusuwele mwanene ehasara ela . ehako eyo yanvanre yona ; owo khuhimya wira : mukinhele mphareya , wira nyuwo mopowase . ti mwaha wa miyo okumihenrye epheyo eyo . anahota yanihuluxa ekalawa n ikuru saya sothene : nto khiyawerya , mana epheyo vahitepa wupa .
vano vahilompa yiraka : apwiya , muhikhalihé votakhala etthu enkelahu wira . muhupuwele wira nintthuna omwiva mutthu ohitthenke . numalá , yahinvara yona , khumurihela mphareya . nananoru masi yahikhalela .
vano apwiya yahiruma ehopa yulupale ommirya yona . owo ahikhala mahiku mararu othana n uhiyu mmirimani mw ehop eyo . anari mmirimani mmo mw ehopa , ahalompa apwiya , muluku awe . ehop eyo yahetta mpakha muxerexere mw ephareya , khumwimula yona .
muluku ahimuruma yona ekwaha yanenli , ìraka : murowé muttetthe mulupale w ònínive . mwalaleye weiwo sothene sinrowaka wohimeryani .
yona ahivenya , khurowa oninive . weiwo , ahilaleya arunyaka wira : muhina mwa mahiku miloko mixexé , ònínive onrowa opwexakasiwa . atthu ònínive yahinwiriyana yona , khumwamini muluku . yahipacerya otthukwa wulupale ni yahiwara mattapwatta , ethonyeryaka ottharuwa wava . atthu othene yahira siso , makhulupale n akhani , athajiri n ale òthoiwa . muluku ahòna ottharuwa w atthu onmive , khuhiyererya owopopiha wawe . masi yona ahinvonyiwa vanjene mwaha w etthu ila .
ahinanariwa , khulompa ìraka : ih ! apwiya ! fatari ti vale miyo kakhottaka orwa onmive nno . miyo kanisuwelexa wira apwiya annaphenta atthu , annalevelela . miyo kintthuna okhwa , kiwenhene itthu sinonaka . yona ahikhuma mmuttettheni , khurowa mpantte mukina w oxerexere .
ahikilathi , khiyawehererya yarowa okhumelela . vano muluku ahiphatteva vavale murapela mmosá , wira onvaheke muttutthi yona . owo , vonalvawe murapel owo , ahitteliwa murima vanjene . masi ohiyu ahirwa mwamukokho , khukhurasa mitathari saya , owo khuma .
othana , nahopa nsuwa novihexa : yona khawerya-tho ovilela oviha iwo , khuhimya wira atthuna okhwa . vano muluku ahimukoha wira : nyuwo munnonela othunku murapela omenle ohiyu omosa , vano ohiyu omosaru yowo khuma . vano miyo nkakhanle omorela ikharari muttetthe mulupale ntoko ninive , memmo muri-mo anamwane anjene vamosa n inama ? .
omwene wa muluku
profeta danivele onalikela supululeliwawe ni muluku . sahixathiwa ihije . humu mmosá ahikilathi vehijeni . sowara sawe sari sottela ntoko nipheru : vano ikharari sawe sari ntoko nlinya nopepheya . ehij awe vari ntoko malumi a moro yavarela oholo wawe . atthu anjene sana vanimurumela . akina miloko miloko sene yahemela oholo wawe .
miyo kahimona mutthu mmosá ntoko mwana a mutthu akhuruwaka wirimu mmekuni . owo ahimwattamela humuwo , khwithonyiheiya oholo wawe . humu ahinvaha owerya ni nttittimiho n umwene . maloko othene n atthu a malavulelo othene ni a mahimo othene yanimurumela . omwene awe ti wa mahiku othene : khummala-tho . owerya wawe khunihononeya .
nsipo na murumeyi a muluku
profeta mmosá onnipa isipo sa murumeyi oniwelela sothene sintthunawe muluku . mwaha wa mulipa-òwiwelela yowo , enokhumelela exariya ya muluku mulaponi ni wopola wawe .
mmone ! ola ti murumeyi aka onimulipihaka : ola t ule omuthanlalyaka , yowo onkitteliha murima . miyo konvaha eroho aka , vano owo onolaleya òrera waka murima mulaponi mothene . owo khanrowa ovanyihana ni mutthu , walá onyakulihana . khavo onrowa wiwa masu awe mmawani . owo khanrowa osinsa mutathi wowunteyene khalayi . khanrowa ottipiha ntthampo nintthuwa mwixi , masi onolaleya exariya vororomeleya .
khanrowa wojeya , nnakhala oweriwa , masi onoruhela exariya mulaponi mothene . atthu ottaiwene anolipelela ikano sawe .
elapo esyá ya muluku
apwiya t anihimya wira : atthu sothene kinokhaliha isva : siso-tho erimu n ilapo sinokhala isva . makhalelo a khalai anovirikana . nyuwo munotteliwa murima vanjene mwaha wa itthu sinrowaka opattuxa . khavo-tho onrowa wunla , nnakhala wikhupanyerya . khaniyariwa-tho anamwane anrowa okhala mahiku vakhani pahi . khavo-tho onrowa okhwa n iyakha vakhani . munokhala akumi iyakha sinjene ntoko mwiri .
khuvo onrowa owiyeryani yoly anyu . hatá nyuwo muhinatthi okivekela etthu p itthu , miyo kinowakhulani . nlelo nyuwo mwalavulaka , miyo kinimowiriyanani . vano mwiji ni mwapwittipwitthi anolyaka poromosa .
kharamu onimolya malaxi ntoko enyompe , nto khanrowa wiriliana yotakhala . khavo onrowa ohonona etthu .
watana wa nanano muluku onimutthukula natiri awe : yesu ti mopoli
yesu ti mwana a muluku
muluku ahiruma nlaikha gabriyeli , namitthak awe , orowa onazarethi , omphwanya mwali mmosá ihaniwa maria , yowo akameliwe ni mulopwana mmosá nsina nawe yosefe , a nloko na mwené davidi . nlaikha gabriyeli nahimwattamela maria , khumuhimeiya wira : mutteliweke murima , maria ! muluku ori ni nyuwo . owo ohothanla ni mw athiyana othene . maria ahitikinihiwa ni molumo ala .
masi nlaikha nle nahimuhimeiya wira : maria , muhòvé . morereliwa murima ni muluku : owo onnophentexani . tthiri nyuwo munorupala , mmuyare mwana mwamulopwana , yowo munrowanyu onvaha nsina na yesu . owo onrowa okhala mulupale ni onrowa wihaniwaka mwana a muluku mulupalexa .
maria ahikoha nlaikha wira : vantthuna wiraneya sai , miyo kihikhalaka ni mulopwana ? gabriyeli ahimwakhula wira : eroho yowarya n ikuru sa muluku enimokhuruwelani . muluku khivo enojelawe . vano maria khwira : miyo ki murumeyi apwiya : yireyeke mwa miyo ntoko muluku sintthunawe ! .
yesu onihaniwa emanuweli : muluku ori ni hiyo
yosefe ari mutthu àxariya ni òthunku . owo ahisuwela wira maria , mwarawe , ahirupala . okhala wira ànimphenta vanjene ni khatthuna omulaleya , anupuwela omuhiya vohisuweliwa .
yesu oyariwe obethelehemu
ekuluttu yeyo vahikhala amakampusi varupelela inama saya . nananoru , nlaikha n apwiya nahakhumelela , ovuwa wa muluku wahamwalela . awo yahova vanjene . vano nlaikha nahahimerya wira : muhove ! koruhenleni ehapari yorera enrowa watteliha murima atthu othene .
olelo , muttetthe wa davidi , moyareliwa mòpoli , okhanle kristu pwiya . etthu enrowa wosuwelihani t ila : munomphwanya mwana akhuneliwene n ikuwo , ataleliwene vamalaxini . nananoru wahikhumelela-tho muttitthi a malaikha a wirimu , emuttottopelaka muluku , yiraka : avuwihiwe muluku wirimu : vathí-va evahiwe murettele atthu muluku onaphentawe .
malaikha yahivenya vale erowaka wirimu , amakampusi , vahanlyaya mekhaya , yahihimeryana yaworu wira : naso nrowé obethelehemu , nawehe itthu sikhumelenle .
yesu ti mwené ayuda
yesu avariwaka , herodi ira anari mwené oyudeva . vano asuweli akina vahivenya elapo yonikhuma nsuwa , khuphiya oyerusalemu . weiwo yahikoha wira : ori vai mwené àyuda ayariwe nanano ? nrimona etheneri awe onikhuma nsuwa , nrwenle omukokhorela .
vano herodi ahiwihana asuweli ale wiphini , khwakohakoha wira asuwele orattene nihiku nònalyaya ethener ile . numalá , aharuma orowa obethelehemu awirelaka : rowakani , mwamphavele orattene mwan owo . mwamphwanya vale , munve mukilele , wira ni miyo-tho kirowe , kamukokhorele .
vahokolowenlyava ephiro aya , asuweli ale yahòna-tho etheneri vonalyaya onikhuma nsuwa , khutteliwa murima vanjene . ethenerile yahahola mpakha ophiva nipuro naryawe yesu , khwemela . asuweli ale yahikela mpani mine , kluimphwanya mwana ni maria , ame awe , khukokhora emuttittimihaka mwanowo .
numalá , yahitthukula mirupa saya , enanvaha ewero , erupani ni emira . vano muluku ahahimerya molohani wira ehivire-tho wa herodi . tivó , ehokolowelaka elapo aya , yahivira ephiro ekina .
yesu onilupatthiwa
vavenyalyaya asuweli ale , nlaikha na muluku nahimukhumelela yosefe molohani , khumuhimerya wira : nvenye , mmukuxe mwana name awe , mutthyawele wejitu . mwakhaleke weiwo mpakha miyo wohimeryani , mana herodi onrowa omphavela mwana , wira amwive . yosefe ahivenya ohiyu , amukunxene mwana name awe , khurowa wejitu .
vano herodi , vonalyawe wira ahotothiwa n asuweli ale , ahinanariwa vanjene , khwamma atthu awe orowa obethelehemu n ilapo sowattamela , wira yawivakase anamwane axilopwana othene yarina iyakha pili orowa vathí .
herodi vakhwiyawe , nlaikha na muluku nahimukhumelela yosefe molohani wejitu , khumuhimeiya wira : nvenye , mmukuxe mwana name awe , muhokolowele elapo va israyeli .
yosefe ahivenya , khumukuxa mwana name awe , khuhokolowela elapo ya israyeli , khurowa okhala onazarethi .
yesu t &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; a muluku
iyakha sothene , atithi awe name awe yesu yanirowa oyerusalemu okathi wa nìra na pasikha . yesu , vaphiyenryawe iyakha muloko ni pili , ahirowa ni yawo . vamanlyaya nira , yosefe ni maria vahivenya ehokolowelaka onazarethi .
vano mmiravole yesu ahihala oyerusalemu weiwe , atithi awe name awe ehisuwenle . nihalaka okela nsuwa , yahikelela omphavela yesu mw amusi aya ni mwatthu yasuwelaya , khuhimphwanva . vano vahihokolowela oyerusalemu , emphavelaka weiwo . yahimala mahiku mararu emphavelaka , khumphwanya mpani mwa muluku .
yesu ira akilanthene eriyari vasuweli : aniwiwa yawo , anakoha-tho . othene ale vamwiwa yanithamala mwaha w osuwela wawe . vano , atithi awe name awe , vamonalyaya , yahitikinihiwa . ame awe yahimukoha wira : mwan aka , munirelenle-ni sisa ? atith inyu ni miyo nahiripiwa murima n uxanka , nophavelakani .
vano yesu ahiwakhula wira : mwakiphavelela-ni ? khimwasuwela wira kihana okhala mpani mw atithi aka ? vano yesu ahivenya vamosa n awo , khuhokolowela onazarethi , aniwiwelela yawo .
olaleya wa yohani mbatiza
yohani mbatiza , mwana a namukuttho zakariya n a elizabeti , akhala mothakoni . muluku ahimuthanla wira akhale namitthak awe . vano yohani ahirowa elapo vowattamela muro yordani , khupacerya walalerya atthu ìraka : muttharuwe sottheka sanyu . murukunuxe makhalelo anyu , mbatiziwaka mmuro yordani , wira muluku oleveleleni sottheka sanyu .
siso sahiraneya iye silempwe mulivuruni mwa profeta yesaya wira : nsu na mutthu ninnikhuwela mothakoni nìraka : mwalokiherye ephiro apwiva , mmwapatthele ephiro muluku ahu . malitti othene vuheliwe , myako ni mapuro owalakakha vataleye , iphiro sokottopa sokololasiwe ni maxepa elikanyihiwe . vano atthu othene anrowa osuwela wopola n uvuwa w apwiya &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; .
atthu anjene yanikoha mmansaya wira : khino yohani ula ti kristu mopoli ? vano yohani ahahimerya atthu othene wira : miyo kinorapihani ni màsi , nto onimorwa mukina okivikanne miyo owerya . yowo-tho miyo nkiniphwanela otaphula mikhoyi sa ixapattho sawe . owo t unrowa worerihani ni eroho yowarya ni moro .
onamona wa muluku tìthi
yesu vaphiyenryawe wattamela iyakha miloko miraru ahirowa omuro yordani omphavela yohani wira amurapihe ntoko atthu akina . vano abatiziwakaru ni alompaka , erimu yahitthukuwa , eroho yowarya yahimukhuruwela , yoneyaka ntoko epomba . vano , wirimu nahiwanyeya nsu nahimya wira : nyuwo mwa mwan aka onimphentexaka ni dkitteliha murima .
yesu onixuttiha ni onavoniha aretta murukunuxe makhalelo anyu
ehapari ya yesu
yesu ahihokolowela ogalileya , weiwo walaleyawe ehapari yorera ya muluku , ìraka : okathi wa muluku wophiya : omwene awe ohanle orwa . murukunuxe murima ni mwamini ehapari yorera kinoruhelakani .
atothi a ihopa yamutthanre yesu
yesu ahirowa muxerexere mwa ephareya y ogalileya .
weiwo ahimona simoni , yowo onihaniwa-tho pedru , vamosa ni andreya , munn awe . awo yira erihelaka matthavi aya mmasini : yari atothi a ihopa . yesu ahiwirela : mukitthareke . miyo kinimokhalihani atothi atthu . owani aya yahihiya matthavi aya nananoru , khumutthara yesu .
vottharelana , yesu ahimona yakobo , mwana a zebedeyo , ni yohani , munn awe . yàri mukalawani vamosa n atithi aya , elokihasaka matthavi . yesu ahiwitthana . nananoru , awo yahihiyasa ekalawa n atithi aya , khumutthara yesu .
mulipa orakala apajenrye wetta
yesu ahihokolowela okafarnawu . atthu othene a mmuttettheni yahisuwela nananoru wira yesu ari owani . anamunjene yahiphiya etthimakasaka , khuthukumana oholo wa mukhora . yesu ahalela othene wira muluku onnaphenta .
vano yahiphiya atthu axexé emuruhaka mulipa-òrakala . awo yaphavela omwattamiheiya yesu mpatthani aya owo , masi muttitthi w atthu khiwatthuna waviriha . ehiweryaka ovira , alopwan awo axexé yahiwela vampani vowataleya , vahivenula nipatho eluluwanyaka varyawe yesu , khumukuiaixa orakal ole ataleliwene vanrepani vawe . yesu ahòna wira alopwan ale yanimwamini yowo , tivó ahimwirela brakal ole wira : itampi sanyu soleveleliwa .
yesu onimwitthana natampi
alipa-òliviha mpóxito khiybniwa sana n atthu . imara sinjene awo yaniliviha mpóxito evikanaka ole warummyaya n ikano . ohiya vo , yanavarela muteko makhulupale aroma yakunxe elapo . tivó afarisi vahatthunanaya ni yawo .
yesu onathanla arummwa muloko nanli
yesu onthanla nloko
yesu anettetta ogalileva wothene . anixuttiha mampani m olompa ni anilaleya ehapari yorera ya muluku . anavoniha othene ale yawereiwa ni vahawa . mulaponi mothene anilavuliwa yowo . atthu a mipantte sothene yanirwa omwiwa . yesu , awehaka atthu anjene siso , ahiwela vamwako vasulu , ahikilathi , vano awixutti awe yahisuserya varya we . yesu ahipajeiya owixuttiha , ìraka :
othene ale ansuwela wira ari amasikhini vamaithoni va muluku etteliweke murima , okhala wira omwene wa win mu ti wawava .
othene ale aripiwe murima etteliweke murima , mana muluku onimwahakalaliha .
othene ale ahinira mpantta w ekhotto etteliweke murima : muluku onimwakhaliha axinene elapo .
othene ale amphavela wira wiweleliwe otthuna wa muluku etteliweke murima , mana muluku onomaleliha ophavela waya .
alipa-òmoriwa ikharari etteliweke murima , okhala wira muluku onimwamorela ikharari .
othene ale òrera murima etteliweke murima , okhala wira anomona muluku .
othene ale anvara muteko w okhaliha murettele etteliweke murima , mana muluku onowakhela ntoko an awe .
othene ale anlupatthiwa mwaha wowiwelela otthuna wa muluku etteliweke murima , okhala wira omwene wa wirimu ti wawaya .
mwixuttiho worera wa yesu
nyuwo munnisuwela yoruma enihimya wira : muhimwive mutthu ; ole onimwiva mutthu onoroihiwa omilattuni . vano mivo kinohimeryani wira : hatá ole onimulumela munn awe onoroihiwa omilattuni . mwavelelaka yovah anyu wa muluku , khupuwela wira munn inyu khakhanle sana ni nyuwo , muhiye ovah anyu oholo w altari , mutthike , musamihane toko ni munn iny uwo . numalá , murweke , nvahererye vovah anyu .
olompa w &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; awixutti a yesu
yesu ahahimerya awixutti awe wira : nyuwo muhana olompa so : tith ihu muri wirimu ! nsina nanyu nivuwihiwe ; omwene anyu onrwele hiyo ; otthuna wanyu wireye ntoko wirimu siso vathí-va . munivahe olelo yoly ahu ya khula nihiku . munlevelele sottheka sahu , ntoko hiyo nnalevelelahu anitthekenle . muhinihiye omora nehereriwaka : vano munakiheiye sotakhala .
yesu onimuhokoloxerya ekumi mulipa okhwa
yesu ahiphiya muttetthe w onayini vamosa n awixutli awe . atthu anjene yanimuhola . ehalaka ophiya mmu ttettheni , yahikumana n atthu yarowa wovithani , emukunxene mmiravo okhwa wira avithiwe . ari mwana mmosene a muthiyana namukhweli , yowo vano arowa okhala mekhawe pahi . anamwattamanani n apatthani awe yanimuhola muthiyan owo oripiwa mpakha omahiye .
yesu , amonakaru muthiyan owo , ahimmorela ikharari , khumwirela : mama , muhinleke ! numalá ahattamela nrepa , khukwata . ale yathata yahemela . yesu ahimwirela mmiravowo wira : miyo kinorumani : nvenye ! vano mulipa-òkhw ole ahihihimuwa , khupacerya olavula . yesu ahavahererya mmirav ole ame awe .
othene yari vavale yahithamala ni wova , khumuttotto pela muluku , yiraka : profeta mulupale okhumelela eri yari ahu . muluku mwanene ohorwa okhaliherya nloko nawe . vano mulaponi mothene sanivira sihimmwaka iye yesu sawirelawe atthu .
munova ni ?
nihiku nimosa , makaripi , yesu ahiwirela awixutti awe : nrowé nlapuwele ekhopel ele ya ephareya . yahiwela mukalawani , khutaphula mikhoyi saya . nananoru , mphareya-mmo vahopa epheyo vulupale . mawimpi yari owopiha . vano ekalawa yanisarya masi .
yesu amurupa . awixutti yahinvenxa ekhuwelaka wira : khamunthokorerya munonaka nsamaka ? vano-nto yesu ahemela , ahulumela epheyo , khuhimei ya ephareya wira : mmale ! mwikhalele !
epheyo yahìkhalela , khukhumelela omaleleya wulupale . vano yesu ahakoha awixutti awe wira : munova-ni ? muhinaminela-ni ? awixutti yahitikinihiwa , yanikohanasa yaworu , yiraka : mano , mutth ula ti pani ? hatá epheyo ni masi annimwiwelela ! .
alipa ovoliwa etala anivona
yesu aphavela okhala mekhawe n awixutti awe , masi muttitthi w atthu wanimutthara . yesu analaleiya atthu ekumi muluku onavahawe atthu mahalene , anavoniha othene ale yaphavela mukhalihei yo awe . makaripi , ale muloko nanli yahimwattamela , khumuhimerya wira : murumé muttitthi ula omwareleke mmawani , waphaveleke opuro ni yolya . mothakoni-mu khivo etthu yorerela .
nto yesu ahiwakhula wira : yoly eyo mwavaheke yenyu . awo yahírasa : hiyo va nrina iphau thanu n ihopa pili pahi . nihana orowa othuma yolya yowaphiyerya atthu ala othene ? tthiri atthu yari ikonto thanu alopwanaru , wahiva athiyana n anamwane .
ephau y &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ekumi
