ale yakhunre iphau , khuvona , yanihimeryana yaworu wira : vekekhai yesu ti profeta orummwe ni muluku molumwenkuni mu . yesu ahisuwela wira aniphaveliwa okuxiwa wira attikhiwe omwene . tivó , ahivenya eriyari y atthu , khukhuma-vo .
mmeloni mwaya , atthu yamphavelasa okafamawu yahimphwanva , khumukoha : mphiyale lini nno ? vano yesu ahiwakhula ìraka : kosuwela wira nyuwo munkiphavelela mwaha w okhura iphau , nvona . muhukhuwaxe ke n iphau enimala : mukhuweke n iphau ekina enivaha ekumi ehinimala .
vano awo vahimukoha wira : muluku onniphavelelani ? yesu khwira : muluku omphavela etthu emosa pahi : wira mmwaminiki yole omurummyawe . mivo ki ephau enivaha ekumi . ole onkirwela mivo , khanivoliwa tho etala . ole onikamini mivo , khanivoliwa-tho ntthona .
wamini w &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; awixutti
yesu ahakhottiherya awixutti walela atthu akina , khwira : mwana a mutthu ohana ohawa vanjene . makhulupale a mulaponi n alupale anamukuttho n awixuttihi a ikano anomuthanya , numalá anomwiva . masi mmurottoni mwaya onohihimuwa mokhwani . yesu alavula itthu iya aihimyaka mmansawe yowo .
onamona w atithi
pedru n arummw ale akina anli yahirupasa , vano , evenyaka , yahimona yesu mowaryani-mme vamosa n alopwana ale anli yalavula ni yowo . pedru ahira : pwiya , hiyo khanrere wijala nipuro nla . nrowé nteke mixaxa mirarii : wawinyu , wa moise ni wa eliya .
pedru khasuwela yahimyawe . vano owo alavulaka siso , nahirwa neku noripa ni notikana , khukhunela mwako . awixutti yahituthuwasa . munekuni-mmo nahikhumela nsu nahimya wira : ola mwan aka omuthanlalyaka . mmwiweleleke . nsu vamanlyaya , khiyàmonne-tho mutthu : yesu pahi t ari-vo . awixutti , mahiku awo , khiyamulenle mutthu etthu ile yakhumelenle. omwako .
yesu onixuttiha ekumi y omukhalela muluku ni yo wakhalela atthu
ale muluku onavahawe ekumi ehinimala t avi ?
numalá , ahimpakhira vabumni vawe , khumurowana nipuro namakiwa . aphiyakaru , ahukhuwa vanjene ni yowo , khumukhapelela . mmeloni mwaya vasisu , ahinatthi otthikela ekwah awe , ahinvaha musurukhu mwanene etthoko , khumuhimeiya wira : mmukhapelele mutth ula . musurukh ula wahiphiyeiye , miyo kahokolowaka kinimwinjererya .
vano yesu ahimukoha mwixuttihi ule a ikano wira : munòna sai ? w atthu ale araru t uvi onimonanyu okhala mukhw awe ole avulalihiwe ? mwixuttihi uwo ahakhula wira : t ule ammorenle ikharari . vano yesu ahimuhimerya wira : naso , muroweke , ni nyuwo mwireke siso ! .
ti pani onrowa okela momweneni mwa muluku ?
okathi mukina yesu ahihimya wira : mwana a mutthu , vam wawe-tho , onothukumanya maloko othene , wira alamule atthu othene . vano onimwavalanya , ntoko makampusi sinivalanyawe ipwittipwitthi n ipuri : onimwapweha akina mono awe wolopwana , vano akina mono awe wothiyana .
ale anrowa okhala mono wothiyana onimwahimerya wira : ele ehimwirenlyanyu mukhanixa w axinn aka , ti miyo muhikirenlyanyu &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; .
ovonya wa thajiri mulolo
yesu ahihimya wira : siso vanimwakhumelela atthu othene yale anithukumanyerya mihakhu , masi ahikhanle athajiri vamaithoni va muluku .
epwittipwitthi yarimenle
alipa-òliviha mpóxito anjene n anatampi yanirowa wa yesu wira yamwiwe . afarisi n awixuttihi a ikano yaninyonyiwa n itthu ila ni yanihimya wira : owo onniwanana n anatampi mpakha olva ni yawo .
ayuda yawiriyana masu ala , yanivanyihana yaworu . akina yanihimya wira : munepa wotakhala onlavula n iyano sa mulopwan ola : khansuwela enihimyawe . akina yanupuwela wira : mutthu ovariwe ni xetwani khanlavula ntoko ola . khino munepa wotakhala onniweiya onvoniha muretta ? .
mwana amuhiyale tithi awe
yesu ahihimya nlikanyiho nla nikina ìraka : mulopwana mmosá ahikhalana ana anli . ole mukhani ahiwirela atithi awe : tithi , mukikawele muhakhu orinanyu okivaha . atithi awe yahinvaha epantte awe . vano mwan ole mukhani ahithukumanya muhakhu awe wothene , khuvenya arowaka ottaiwene .
atithi awe yahinweha arwaka ottaiwene , yahimonela othunku vanjene mwan aya , yahimutthimakela , khumukhuparela . vano mwana ahipacerya ohimya wira : tithi , miyo komutthekela muluku ni kihotthekelani nyuwo . nkimphwanela okhala mwan inyu . masi atithi awe yahakhula wira : nrowé , nipake nlra , nitteliwe murima . mwan aka ahikhwa , vano otthikela ekumi . ahirimela , vano ohokolowela owani .
mwan ole mulupale ari omatta . atthikaka , ahìwa wipiwa ni winiwa . ahimukoha namuteko mmosá wira : exen iyo enlraneya ? owo khwakhula wira : muhim anyu t uhokolowenle owani . atith inyu aniriha efesta mwaha w otteliwa murima , mana mwan aya ohokolowa .
vano mwan ole mulupale ahinanariwa vanjene : khatthuna okela vapu wani . atithi awe yahirowa omphwanya nipuro naryawe , akhottaka ophiya vaté : yaniphavela omulela sothene .
thajiri ni masikhini
yesu ahahimerya atthu nlikanyiho nla : khalai ahikhala mulopwana mmosá thajiri . awara ikuwo sowarya ni ahikhalana sothene saphavelawe . vano , oholo wa mukhora wa emp awe anikokhora masikhini mmosá , ihaniwa lázaro , ari òthoiwa ni otakhaliwa . erutthu awe yothene yahisareya makhwatta . anivoliwa vanjene mpakha anaphavela okhura itathela samora vamesa va thajiri . hatá alapwa yanirwa olatta makhwatt awe .
lázaro vakhwivawe , nlaikha nahirwa khumukuxa , khumurowana wirimu poromosa n abrahamu . siso-tho ahikhwa thajiri ule , khuvithiwa . mulaponi mw alipa-òkhwa anihawa ni masoso manjene . vano ahittukhula maitho , khunweha abrahamu ni lázaro , ari poromosa .
vano ahikhuwela ìraka : tithi abixihamu ! mukimorele ikharari . mmurume lázar &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; owo arwe nno , ananihe ethoka y ekath awe mmasini , aririhe nlumi naka , okhala wira kinnihawa vanjene mmoroni-mu .
masi abrahamu ahimwakhula wira : mupuwele wira , okathi wothene w ekumi anyu , nyuwo mopuha mirerelo sothene sorwenleni : vano lázaro ahiphwanya ohawa pahi . tivó , okathi ula owo onihakalalihiwa . vano-tho , nno oryahu n iwo , khurere orakamelana ni wixerya . khavo onwerya ovenya nno arwaka iwo , walá ovenya iwo oryanyu wira arwe nno oryahu .
vano thajiri ule ahihimya wira : tithi abrahamu , kihovarelani metto ! mmurume lázaro arowe owannyeya atithi , alopole axinn aka ehirwase nipuro nla na masoso .
abrahamu ahimwakhula wira : awo akhalana mixuttiho sa moise ni sa maprofeta : yatthuna , yetteleke seiyo thajiri ahihimya-tho wira : masi , akhala mulipa-òkhwa anrowa walopola , awo anorukunuxa makhalelo aya . vano abrahamu ahakhula-tho wira : awo yahimwiwelele moise walá maprofeta , khanrowa-tho omwiwelela hatá mulipaokhwa ohihimunwe &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; .
ehantisi y &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; ole aisona okhala naxariya ni ya mulipa ottheka
emara emosa yesu ahaphwanya afarisi akina yalsona okhala anaxariya . awo yakupali wira yaniwelela soruma sothene sa muluku , tivó-nto yanathanya akina othene . yesu ahiwalikelela ethale emosá , ìraka : alopwana anli yahikela mpani mwa muluku wira elompe .
mmosá a yawo ari nfarisi , mukina ari mulipa-òliviha mpóxito . nfarisi ahiholela , khwemela oholo , analom pa ìraka : muluku aka , miyo kinnotthapelani , okhala wira ka naxariya wavikana akina othene . miyo nkiniva , nkinimuhaxa mutthu , ki mulopwana ororomeleya vamaithoni v amwar aka . hatá nkihiyo ntoko mulipa-òliviha mposit ole ori ottul iwe .
miyo kinnitthukwa imara pili wa khula esumana , kinnivaha mpani mwa muluku mpantte wanamuloko wetthu p itthu kirinaka . mulipa-òliviha mpóxito ari ottuli , ira ùraminhene murú , animana etthirima ni anilompa ìraka : muluku aka , miyo ki natampi : mukimorele ikharari ! &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; yesu ahihimya wira : kinolelani wira ola ahokolowenle owani aleveleliwene . mukin ole khaleveleliwe .
wamini wa mulipa ohona
yesu anattamela muttetthe w oyerikho . mulipa-òhona mmosá ira akilanthene mphironi , anavekela esimola . vaiwalyawe wira yanivira atthu anjenexa wovirikana ni mahiku othene , ahikoha wira : exeni enikhumelela ? ahileliwa wira yesu munazarethi t aphiyale mmuttettheni .
vano mulipa-òhona ahikelela okhuwela ìraka : yesu , mwana a davidi ! mukimorele ikharari ! ale yarowa oholo wa yesu yanimukhottiherya yiraka : omale we ! ohikumiherye mulattu va ! masi uwo anthipelela okhuwela n ikuru ìraka : mwana a davidi ! mukimorele ikharari !
zakeyo onrukunuxa makhalelo awe
yesu ohiviwa , òvithiwa , òhihimuwa
yesu onrowa oyerusalemu omwira pásikha
ehalaka mahiku vakhani wiriwa pdsikha , yesu ahahimerya arummwa muloko n anli wira : nrowé niwelele oyerusalemu , weiwo kinrowaka ovahereriwa mmatatani mw alupale anamukuttho n awixuttihi a ikano . awo anrowa okilamula wira klviwe ni anokivahererya mmatatani mw aroma . awo anokiveha , anokisenelasa , anokiputthasa ni murepettho , numalá anokiva . masi yavira mahiku mararu , miyo kinohihimuwa mokhwani .
mwixutti yuda oninvariha yesu
nattamelaka nira na pasikha , alupale anamukuttho ni makhulupale a ikano yahithukumana : vaniphavela onvara yesu ni wothererya waya wira emwìve . awo yanihimeiyana yaworu wira : nihire okathi wa efesta , vahire siso muxovo onrukunuwele .
mmosá arummwa muloko n anli , ihaniwa yuda isikaryoti , ahirowa olavula n elnamukuttho , khwira : miyo kolikanana wivahereiyani yesu . awo yahitteliwa murima , khumulaphela onvaha musurukhu miloko miraru sa eparatha . okhuma okathi ene yole , yuda aniphavela makhalelo brerela onvariha yesu .
yolya yokiserya
siso-tho , vamanlyaya olya , ahikuxa ekahi va evinyu : vano , arerihaka , ahavaha-tho awixutti awe , ìraka : mukuxeke , nwuryeke othene anyu , mana ela ekalisi y ephome aka , ephome yo watàna wa vano ni wohimala , entthuna omwarexeliwa nyuwo n atthu othene , wira sottheka sileveleliwe . mwireke iya mukupuwelaka miyo .
ethonyeryo y &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; osuweliwa awixutti a yesu
numalá olya , yesu ahathonyerya awixutti awe enamuna yaphentawe ni ntoko sarinaya ophentana mukina ni mukhwawe . yesu ahivenya vamesa , khutthukwela etuwaya muyununi vano ahisarya masi mbasiyani , khukelela orapiha inawu s awixutti awe . simoni pedru ahikhotta orumeliwa siso ni yesu , khwira : pwiya , mumphavela orapiha inawu saka ? yesu ahimwakhula wira : oholo , nyuwo munosuwela etthu kiniraka vano . nto pedm ahithipelela ìraka : khamunrapiha inawu saka seiya .
nla ninrowa okhala nthonyeryo nanyu : nyuwo mwaphentanakam mukina ni mukhw awe , atthu othene animona wira nyuwo mw awixutti aka . khavo orina ophenta wulupale onvikana ole onileva ekumi awe mwaha w axipatthani awe . nyuwo mw àxipatthani aka . mwireke ntoko sorummyakani . yesu ahihimya-tho wira : vano nkinrowa okhala okathi munjene ni nyuwo . masi muhove . mmwaminiki muluku , mukamini-tho miyo .
miyo kinrowa w atithi . vano , kakhala n atithi , kinimolokiheryani opuro . numalá kinihokolowa wira kokuxeni , mwakhaleke ni miyo vohimala-tho . vano , kinimwavekela atithi wira yoruimiheleni mulipa-òkhaliherya dwerya , eyo p iyo , eroho yowarya , eroho y ekekhai . eroho yeyo enowupuxeryani itthu sothene sohimenryakani .
yesu onilompa omwako olivera
vamanlyaya olya , yesu ahirowa omatta yari omwako olivera . awixutti awe yahimuhola . vaphiyalyaya weiwo , yesu ahahimerya wira : mulompeke wira mukhale owilipiha mwereriwaka . vano ahirowa okhwipi mekhawe , ahikokhora , khiyalompa ìraka : tithi ! mwatthuna , munowerya okakiherya ohawa n ukhwa . masi ohireye ntoko sintthunaka miyo : wireye otthuna wanyu .
mohawani mwawe mokhwa , yesu anilompa ni nthiti nulupale , mpakha oretthela mattonttoni a ephome yakhola mpakha vathí . numalá , ahivenya , khuhokolowela wari awixutti . awo yamurupa , okhala wira wova ni wukhuwa wahaveliha . yesu ahakoha wira : nyuwo munweiya saiorupa ? nvenye , mulompeke wira muxintte weremva ohanle orwa .
nlelo yesu alavulaka sisale n awixutti awe , yahiphiya alopwana akina mmatta mme : yaniholiwa ni yuda isikaryoti . owo ahimwattamela yesu wira amukhomase , khunvaha ebejo .
yesu ahimukoha wira : yuda , nyuwo munrowa okivariha n ibejo ? awixutti , vasuwenlyaya wira alopwan ale yarwenle onvara yesu n umukuxa , vahimukoha wira : pwiya , ninniwerya wisakiha ? vano mmosá a yawo ahitholola ekatana , khuthikila niyaru nolopwana na murumeyi mukina a mulupale anamukuttho . masi yesu khasiveliwe , khwira : pahi siso ! vano ahikwannya niyaru na mulipa-òvulalihiwa , khunvoniha .
numalá ahahimerya anakhotto ale wira : nyuwo murwiye n ikatana n ikopo wira mukivare . miyo nkakhala mahiku othene mpani mwa muluku , erivari anyu ? vano iwo khamwawenrye okiriha etthu . nto vano wophiva okathi anyu . tukathi wa ikuru sepiphi .
pedru onimuruna pwiy &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; awe
yesu oholo wa muthukumano mulupale
yesu ahakhula wira : ti nyuwo munihimya wira miyo ki mwana a muluku . othene yahihimva wira : khinnaphavela-tho anamona akina : othene ahu nihìwaehimyalyawe .
olamuliwa wa yesu oholo wa pilato
makhulupale a nloko yahimurowana yesu wa guvernatoro òroma , ari ponsio pilato , khumothei ya ìraka : mulopwan ola onnahuluxa marú atthu . owo onihimya wira ti mòpoli ni ti mwené . pilato ahimukoha yesu wira : nyuwo mwa mwené ?
yesu khwakhula wira : omwene aka khahiyo wa vathí vava . wari wa vathí-vava , arumeyi aka yamukumiha ekhotto wira ekakihe . miyo ki mwené , vano kihorwa mulaponi wira kikhalele onamona ekekhai . ale othene amphavela ekekhai anniwiriyana sinihimyaka . vano pilato ahimukoha wira : ekekhai ? entthuna okhala exeni yeyo ?
pilato ahahimerya ale yamotherya yesu wira : nkinimonana mulatlu w ohimya wira ottheka . vano iyakha sothene , okathi wa pásikha kinnimutaphula mulipa-òtthukweliwa mmosá . mukwah ola kimutaphule mwené ayuda ? awo yahakhula ekhuwelaka wira : nnari ! yesu nnari ! mmutaphule baraba .
baraba owo ari mulavilavi vano pilato ahimulaphula baraba , khuniina omaniwa yesu . vano anakhotto , wira envèhe yesu , yahupa ekhara ya miwa , khunwariha votakhala mmumni . numalá yahimukapattiha ekuwo yoxerya mmakhatani , yaninveha , yiraka : maxikamolo , mwené ayuda ! ni animmana .
pilato ahiwoniherya yesu ale yambtheryasa , khwira : mmone ! mmoneke mutth ula ! vano awo yanikhuwelasa , yiraka : mmukhomele vamwikimanyo ! pilato ahihimya wira : mmukuxeke yenyu , mmukhomele vamwiki manyo : miyo nkinimphwanyana mulattu w ophwanela wiviwa . masi awo yahihimyasa wira : hiyo nokhalana nikano nnihimya wira owo ohana okhwa .
owo ahilavula mwanene ahimyaka wira ti mwana a muluku . vano-tho yahimukhanyereriha pilato mpakha omopiha : siso ahimulamula yesu wiviwa akhomeliwaka vamwikimanyo .
yesu onkhwa vamwikimanyo
yesu ahikapattha mwikimanyo , khuvikana muttetthe mpakha vasulu va nttumuxa naihaniwa golgotha . weiwo yahikhomeliwa vamwikimanyo . vamosa ni yowo yahikhomeliwa-tho atakhali anli : mikimanyo saya sari mmosá mono wolopwana , mukina mono wothiyana wa mwikimanyo wa yesu .
pilato ahiruma wira vamwikimanyo wa yesu nthomeiwe nipawe , nalempwe wira : yesu munazarethi , mwené ayuda . alupale anamukuttho yahinyonyiwa vanjene , khumwirela pilato : muthamihe etthu elempwe vanipaweni-vo . mulepe so : owo ohimya wira ari mwené ayuda . masi pilato ahikhotta othamiha etthu yalempyawe , ìraka : elempyaka , kolepa !
yesu ahisuwela wira ahimalilierya sothene sarinawe ornaleliha , khwira : sothene somaliheriwa ! vano ahuramiha murú , khukhwa .
ovithiwa wa yesu
yosefe a warimathaya ari mutthu òwiweleliwa . yowo-tho anira mpantta muthukumano mulupale w ayuda , nave-tho aniwehererya okhumelela omwene wa muluku . makáripi ene , ahirowa wa pilato , khunvekela wira : mukemiherye okuruxa vamwikimanyo murutthu wa yesu , wira kavithe .
pilato ahimutthuniherya . vano , yosefe ahithuma esanta , ahikuruxa vamwikimanyo murutthu wa yesu , ahiphapa n isanta ele , khupweha mmahiye yathimpwe vamwala . numalá , ahipirikixa nluku nulupale , wira attiyele mukhora wa mahiye . athiyana anli , maria omadala ni maria , mam &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; awe yosefe , yaniweha sothene , khwona nipuro napwehiwe murutthu wa yesu .
mutthaka wa nlaikha : fthihimuwa !
vavinryaya esabadu , maria omadala ni maria , ame awe yakobo , ni salome vahithuma makhura owunkhela , wira arowe omahiye ottikitthela murutthu wa yesu . vosisu ene , nsuwa nipaceryaka okhuma , vahirowa omahiye . mphironi yanikohana yaworu : ti pani onrowa onikumihilia nluku nle nri vamukhora va mahiye ?
vaphiyalyaya omahiye , yahòna wira nluku nahikumihiwa-vo . vano , yahivolowa mmahiye , khumona mmiravo mmosá awanre sottela , akilanthene mono wolopwana .
awixutti anli anikumana ni mulipa ohihimuwa
nihiku nenlo , makaripi , awixutti anli yahikhuma oyerusalemu erowaka wemawusi . mphironi yanivanela mwaha wa sothene sakhumelenle oyerusalemu . vano yesu ahiwattamela , khupacerya otthukwa muloko ni yawo : masi owanli aya khiyamusuwenle . yesu ahakoha wira : exen iyo munlavulanyu ?
òwanli yahemela eripiwene murima . mukina a yawo , ihaniwa kelopha , ahimukoha wira : vekekhai , nyuwo khamwiwale itthu sikhumelenle mahiku ala oyemsalemu ? mulipa a mukwaha ahikoha : ekhumelenle exeni ?
nananoru , awixutti anli atthimakela omahiye : aphwanya sothene ntoko athiyana sahimmyaya . masi uwo khamphwannye .
vano yesu ahahimerya awixutti ale anli wira : masi nyuwo khamunsuwela sinireya ? khamunamini iye sihimmwe ni maprofeta ? mopoli ahana ohawa itthu iya sothene . mwaha w etthu ila muluku ononvaha nttittimiho n uwerya n ikumi .
vano ahataphulela itthu silempwe mulivuruni mwa muluku mwaha wa mopoli . vaphiyalyaya muttetthe wemawusi , yesu anahiya awixutti ale anli , ntoko wira atthuna opwaherya ekwah awe . masi awixutti ale yahimulattula ohala ni yawo , emukhanyererihaka : muhale ni hiyo : vannila . epiphi ennattamela . yesu ahikela mpani , khukhala ni yawo .
awo yahahiya awixutti anli yaphiyale nanano wira : ekhweli ! apwiya ahihimuwa ! pedru òwona ! vano ale anli yahiwalikelela sakhumelenle mphironi , erowaka wemawusi , n inamuna yamusuwenlyaya yesu okathi akawanyawe ephau .
yesu onikumana n awixutti awe òyerusalemu
awixutti yahithukumana oyerusalemu . awo yanòva , khuwalaka mukhora n ulipiha . nananoru yesu ahirwa eriyari aya , khwahimerya wira : murettele okhale ni nyu wo ! numalá , ahiwoniherya mirala sa matat awe . awixutti , ewonaka apwiya , yahitteliwa murima vanjene .
yesu ahahimerya-tho vanenli wira : murettele okhale ni nyuwo ! ntoko atithi sikirummyaya , siso miyo kinnommani nyuwo . khwira : mwakhele eroho yowarya . ale anrowanyu walevelela itampi , muluku onimwalevelela . ale anrowanyu ohalevelela itampi , khanrowa oleveleliwa .
apwiya anaruma arummw &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; aya ilapo sothene
arummwa muloko ni mmosá yahirowa ogalileya , omwako wathonyeriwaya n apwiya . weiwo yahimona yesu , khuramela mpakha vathí oholo wawe . nto akina , nlelo yanihoverya . yesu ahiwattamela , khwahimerya wira : atithi akivaha owerya wothene wa wirimu ni wa vathí . miyo kinnorumani n uwerya wene weiwo : murowé ilapo sothene . mwire wira atthu othene ekhale awixutti aka .
mwabatize ni nsina n atithi ni na mwana ni na eroho yowarya . nwixuttihe ni mwalele sothene sirinaya osuwela , wira yetteke ntoko miyo siwixuttihalyakani . vano miyo kinkhala ni nyuwo mahiku othene mpakha omalá olumwenku .
yesu onkhala ni hiyo
yesu onalaxerya awixutti awe
yahivira mahiku miloko mixexé numalá nlra na pasiklia . mahiku awo , apwiya yahikumana imara sinjene n awixutti ava . vano yahahimerya wira : mukhale oyemsalemu : munwehereryeke mukhaliheryo atithi anrowaya worumihelani . yohani orapiha ni masi mmuro yordani . nyuwo munrowa obatiziwa n lroho yowarya . vano munokha la anamon aka oyerusalemu-nno n ilapo sothene mpakha mapuro okiserya elapo .
numalá wahimerya itthu iya sothene , yesu ahiwelihiwa wirimu . awelaka sisale nahikhumelela neku , khumukhunela . awixutti yahitikinihiwa , khuhala ewehexexa ka osulu . vano yahoneya alopwana anli ewanrene sottela ; awo yahahimerya wira : munira-ni va mwemenlya nyu , munawehexexa osulu ? yesu , ohiyaleni arowaka wirimu , animorwa-tho . nyuwo munomusuwela .
nloko nisya na muluku : ekereja ya yesu kristu
mahiku awo , atthu anjenexa yahirwa òyerusalemu , ekhumaka ilapo s ottaiwene , wira etthapele nlra na pentekositi . valwalyaya omma iwe , yahithukumana oholo w empa yaryaya-mo awixutti a yesu .
othene yahitiki nihiwa , mana khula mutthu awiwa awixutti elavulaka elavulelo awe . etikinihiwene siso , yanikohana yaworu wira : exen ila ?
vano pedru ahikelela olavula , khwira : mukiwiriyane : kinrowa wolelani sothene . nipuro nla ninihiku nla n olelo sinniraneya iye profeta yoweli silaleivawe ni nsina na muluku wira : wemaleloni wa mahiku , muluku onimwavaha eroho awe atthu othene .
nyuwo mmupuwele yesu munazarethi , mwana a muluku . owo oiwiye n otthuna w atithi , khuvara miteko sava . nyuwo muhona sothene . vano muluku onvahererya mwan awe wokhwani . vekekhai , nyuwo mombtherya , khwavahererya aroma wira emwìve . owo ohokhwa akhomeliwene vamwikimanvo . masi muluku omuhihimuxa mokhwani .
hiyo othene nanamon awe : muluku onvuwiha ! owo ti mopoli ! molumo a pedru yaliiphiya mmurimani mwatthu anjene . ala yanikoha wira : amusi aka , nireke sai ? pedru ahiwakhula wira : mumkunuxe makhalelo anyu . mbatiziwe ni nsina na yesu kristu , wira itampi sanyu sileveleliwe .
nto muluku onimovahani eroho awe yowarya . atthu anjene yahiwelela molumo a pedru , khuvekela wira ebatiziwe . nihiku nenlo pahi , atthu ikonto ttharu yahikela nloko na yesu kristu .
omukhalela yesu mpakha omukhwela yowo
okhuma vavo , arummwa yanivara miteko saya oyerusalemu : yanavoniha aretta , yanikhalela anamona ekumi ni okhwa ni ohihimuwa wa yesu . atthu owamini yanivira yinjerereyaka . alupale anamukuttho ni mahumu a israyeli yaphavela wira atthu emuliyale yesu : tivó , yahavara arummwa , yahaphuka , khwakhottiherya wixuttiha ni nsina na yesu .
masi arummwa khiyàjalenle okhottihiwa iwo .
sitefano , mmosá a madiyakono opacerya , ahiviwa avonyakasiwaka maluku . ahinatthi omalamala vathí va maralala a maluku vavonyakasiwe , ahihimya wira : pwiya ! muhithokorerye yotakhala ela eniraya ! pwiya yesu , akhelani eroho aka !
oyerusalemu ekomunidade y ale yamwamini yesu yahilupatthiwa . othene ale yalaleya wamini waya yandmoliwa mmuttettheni . masi nipuro ti nipuro narowaya , awo yanlaleya sorera muluku sawirenlyawe atthu ni miteko sa yesu kristu . mapuro othene saniphattuwa ikomunidade isya .
paulo , murummwa a maloko othene
paulo ari muyuda dmuttittimiha muluku , asuwela sana solempwa sa muluku . masi anupuwela wira yesu vekekhai khahiyo mopoli , masi ari mulavilavi àhapuxa atthu . tivó , paulo anettetta mmittettheni , wira ahuluxeke atthu wamini iwo ni wira ithukhumu ale yamwamini yesu .
nihiku nikina , ira atthimakelaka odamasiko , wira avarakase akristu a weiwo ni wira àruhe òtthukiwene oyeiusalemu . vano mphironi wahimurukurerya nananoru wai ya wakhuma wirimu . paulo ahimora vakhavaloni , khwiwa nsu namuhimerya wira : exeni enkilupatthelanyu ?
paulo khasuwela etthu yamukhumelela , vano ahikoha wira : mwa pani , pwiya ? khwiwa akhuliwaka wira : miyo ki yesu , yole onimulupatthanyu . vano nvenye , mukele mmuttettheni . memmo munrowa ohimeriwa erinanyu wira . paulo ahikela odamasiko . weiwo ahimphwanya ananiva , mwixutti a yesu .
ananiy &amp; amp ; amp ; apos ; owo khatthuna okupali wira paulo ahiphwanyiwa n apwiya ni wira ahirukunuxa murima , khukhala mwixutti . vano apwiya yahimuhimerya ananiva wira : miyo komuthanla paulo wira akhale mulaleyi a maloko othene , wira esuwele nsina naka . vano ananiva ahimwakhela paulo mukomunidadeni mw akristu .
okhuma vavo , paulo khahiyo-tho mulipa-òwalupattha akristu , masi khukhala murummwa ni mulaleyi a kristu . owo ahipacerya olaleya odamasiko ni mittetthe sikina wira yesu kristu ti mopoli . vano khuvira elaleyaka elapo t ilapo , elavulaka mpani mothukumana y ayu da . ahipattuxa ikomunidade s akristu ni ahivara muteko wira ayuda n amalapo a ilapo sothene epake , othene vamosa , nloko nsya na muluku .
paulo ahetta ikwaha sulupale wira alaleye ehapari yorera ilapo sale ahakhanle ayuda . imara sinjene ahilupatthiwa n ayuda n amalapo . paulo ahilepela ipaphelo ikomunidade sothene satenkyawe .
mpapheloni memmo onnavaha miruku akristu awo ni onnilipiha ikomunidade mowaminini . onnatumererya-tho atthu omwamini yesu kristu , onniwixuttiha wetta ntoko akristu dkhweli . vavinryaya okathi mukina , paulo ahivariwa oyerusalemu , khurowaniwa òroma ntoko mulipa-òtthukweliwa . weiwo ahilamuliwa wiviwa , khumukhwela yesu kristu .
molumo makina paulo alepenlyawe ikomunidade
yesu ohokhwa , ohihimuwa ni ovuwihiwa , khukhala mono wolopwana wa muluku . yesu onninivekelela hiyo . khivo etthu enwerya onivalanya ni kristu n uphenta wa we : nnakhala masoso walá etala , nnakhala olupatthiwa walá okhwa . tthiri , sothene iya noxintta , okhala wira kristu onniniphenta . miyo kiri olipene : khuvo owerya w olumwenk ula onwerya onivalanya ni yowo .
nyuwo munnimwamini yesu kristu , tivó-nto muiyanyu na a muluku . mobatiziwa ni muri mukomunidadeni mwa yesu kristu . muhina mw ekomunidad iyo khamunikohaniwa ti pani muyuda walá mmalapo , epottha nnàkhala nethi , mulopwana walá muthiyana , mana atthu othene akhalihiwa etthu emosaru pahi mwa kristu .
okathi wothene mukhaleke otteliwa murima . mulompeke okathi t ukathi . muxukhureleke sothene . eyo t itthu muluku enwehereryawe wale animwamini yesu kristu . mwiweleleke sothene iye eroho enohimeryayani . muthanleleke sothene , nto musukeke iye sikhanle sorera , mutthvaweke sothene iye siri sotakhala .
oniphenta wa kristu onninkhanyererya . nosuwela tthiri wira : mutthu mmosá pahi ohakhwela atthu othene , wira ale anikhala , ehikhaleleke mmansaya , masi emukhaleleke ole okhwiye khuhihimuwa mwaha wa yawo .
axinnaka osivela ! mutteliweke murima : muhakalalaniheke mukina ni mukhw awe . muhiwaneké yenyuru , nto mukhaleke ni murettele . siso muluku a mphento ni a murettele onokhala ni nyuwo . murettele w apwiya yesu kristu , ophenta w atithi ni wataniha wa eroho yowaiya sikhale ni nyuwo othene .
nihikhaleke ntoko atthu ahinroromela
muluku onnivaha ekumi , eri yovah awe . itthu sothene sikumi sinkhala mwaha w otthuna wawe yowo . hatá atthu vakhalaka iyakha miloko mithanu na mili , vano ale olipexa mpakha iyakha miloko mithanu na miraru , wilipiha waya ti okhulumuwa mahala , okhala wira iyo sinnivira vowakuveya ni sinnivavihiwa n ipheyo .
